Chapter 351: A Steal

“Boss, how many spirit stones for this bottle?” Lu Yang crouched down and asked casually.

“You have a keen eye, customer! I got this Jade Cleansing Bottle from a secret domain opened by a Nascent Soul cultivator. It contains diluted Taiyi True Water. Eighty thousand spirit stones.”

The corner of Lu Yang’s eye twitched. Is this daylight robbery? A Golden Core cultivator’s entire fortune is only around ten thousand spirit stones.

Besides, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy has already informed me that the Taiyi True Water inside has been diluted ten thousand times. My urine probably contains more potency than this.

In these street markets, if you’re slow-witted, inexperienced, and lack judgment, it’s easy to get fleeced.

Thankfully, I have the Everlasting Immortal Fairy with me.

“What about the effects of this pill?”

“Forming a golden core in one attempt has always been a struggle for cultivators. This bottle of pills can simulate the golden core formation process with sixty percent accuracy, drastically improving the success rates of forming a golden core. Thirty thousand spirit stones per bottle!” The vendor pitched fervently.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou exchanged puzzled glances. Aren’t all golden cores successfully formed in one attempt?

Lu Yang shook the bottle with a smirk. “Boss, you’re not being honest. Even with sealing techniques, the efficacy of the pills is still dissipating. Thirty thousand per bottle is the price for intact pills, not the ones inside these bottles.”

The vendor laughed it off by praising Lu Yang for his perceptive eye while inwardly sweating. I’ve met someone who is well-versed in this trade.

“What about this flying sword? Don’t tell me this is the flying sword the master of the secret domain wielded,” Lu Yang casually said, making his tone unambiguous for the vendor.

While the vendor was oblivious to the situation he was trapped in, Meng Jingzhou figured it out. Lu Yang’s whole charade was to pave the way for this flying sword.

It’s so battered though. Could it be that it hides some secrets?

The vendor declared with certainty, “This sword’s material is tough and enduring through the centuries. Although it cannot compare to Nascent Soul artifacts, it’s definitely a personal magical treasure of the owner. As it has experienced a major battle, repairing it would be a loss, so it was placed in the secret domain!” He spoke as though he had witnessed the Nascent Soul cultivator slaying their enemies firsthand.

Lu Yang didn’t buy the vendor’s spiel, but another question struck him. How could an immortal sword be in such an abysmal state? Even if several hundred thousand years have passed, it shouldn’t have degraded so badly.

Unless it truly experienced a major battle and was severely damaged!

Who was the enemy?

“Enough. Save the lies for gullible fools. Don’t think I can’t discern anything. This flying sword’s quality is deplorable, barely usable by Golden Core cultivators. It should be the sword of a Foundation Establishment cultivator.”

Although the vendor was clueless about the flying sword’s origins, he couldn’t allow Lu Yang to dictate the narrative.

“This was definitely the sword of the secret domain’s master at the Golden Core Stage. There’s no way it’s for Foundation Establishment cultivators!”

Lu Yang showed an expression that looked like he was too lazy to argue. “Three thousand spirit stones? It’s so broken. I’ll still need to repair it after buying it.

“The lowest is twenty thousand spirit stones!”

“Let’s go.” Lu Yang turned to leave.

“Hey, wait! We can still discuss the price. Eighteen thousand!

Lu Yang stated coldly, “Five thousand.”

The vendor gritted his teeth. When I set up my stall in other places, everyone found the flying sword too damaged. It isn’t easy to meet someone willing to buy this during the Qing Province Grand Ceremony. If I miss this opportunity, who knows when the next one could come? “Fine, five thousand then! I’ll treat this as making a friend!”

Seeing Lu Yang fulfil his wish of securing the sword, Meng Jingzhou transmitted an auditory message out of curiosity. “What’s the origin of this flying sword?”

“It was once wielded by an ancient immortal.”

Meng Jingzhou gasped, looking at Lu Yang with envious eyes. What a steal!

Originally, Lu Yang had planned to subtly inquire with the vendor where he had obtained the sword, but the moment the vendor claimed it came from a Nascent Soul cultivator’s secret domain, he knew he wouldn’t get anything out of the vendor.

To inflate prices, vendors will fabricate backstories of their products, which means that this sword likely came from a Nascent Soul’s secret domain at best. Some random Nascent Soul cultivator had probably picked up this sword from somewhere. Its true origins can no longer be traced.

Lu Yang examined the flying sword for a moment. Though it was damaged, it bore no bloodstains or chips. The fractured edges were rough, as if someone had snapped it with brute force.

My Sword Spirit Root intuition is telling me that this is undoubtedly a peerless sword.

“Was the Qilin Immortal a sword cultivator?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shook her head. “No, the Qilin Immortal didn’t use swords. Come on, let’s keep moving and see what other good stuff we can find.”

“Hold on a minute, if the Qilin Immortal didn’t use swords, what was this flying sword for?”

“Oh, have I not told you before? Whenever the Qilin Immortal did something wrong, those two Dragon and Phoenix lasses would place the flying swords upright in a square arrangement and make him kneel on the tips of the swords.

“Thus, the Qilin Immortal requested the Heaven Mandate Immortal to forge a batch of flying swords that gleamed coldly and appeared extraordinary at a glance. But when they were used, they were harmless, and kneeling on them was like kneeling on foam.

“Later, when the two Dragon and Phoenix lasses discovered this matter, they snapped every flying sword in rage. What you’re holding right now was one of them.”

Lu Yang, “...”

So I spent five thousand spirit stones on something like this?

I even considered requesting the Everlasting Immortal Fairy to help Meng Jingzhou find a treasure and experience the thrill of scoring a steal.

But from the looks of it now, forget it. I shouldn’t let the Everlasting Immortal Fairy trample on and squander Meng Jingzhou’s spirit stones.

~~~

“Your Excellency, disciples from the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace, Five-Elements Sect, and the Demon Suppression Sect have arrived and are waiting at the entrance,” a subordinate of the provincial governor reported respectfully.

The provincial governor nodded slightly, attaching high importance to the Five Great Immortal Sects. “Only three sects? The Dao-Seeking Sect and Hanging Monastery didn’t come? Well, invite them all in.”

The Qing Province Grand Ceremony was jointly hosted by the local authorities and several local first-class sects. Having members of the Five Great Immortal Sects participate would significantly elevate the ceremony’s prestige.

The provincial governor remarked, “That old Dao-Seeking Sect founder back then really set an impressive precedent as provincial governor here.” Putting aside whether the people from the Dao-Seeking Sect are reliable, absolutely no one can match their boundless creativity and imagination.

After all, the Qing Province Grand Ceremony itself was a brainchild of someone from the Dao-Seeking Sect. A well-executed Qingzhou Grand Ceremony will be recognized as a political achievement.

The highlight of the Qing Province Grand Ceremony was the cultivators’ exchange. However, the Five-Elements Sect could hold exchanges within their own circles, where every participant was considered a genius. Why would they care about this ceremony?

Sending a representative was a diplomatic gesture to show some courtesy to the Qing Province authorities.

“What are you waiting for? Go!” The provincial governor frowned at his subordinate, who remained rooted to the spot.

“Your Excellency, there’s a slight problem. There appears to be no more accommodations for the sect disciples.”

“What about the posthouses?”

“As per Your Excellency’s orders, all high-ranking cultivators are housed there to ensure they experience our warm reception.”

“What about the inn at the foot of the mountain?”

“Completely booked.”

“Then build some temporary housing.”

“There’s no space. During the planning phase, all available space was taken up to accommodate as many people as possible.”

The provincial governor found himself in a bind. Having representatives from the Five Great Immortal Sects is an honor, but if our hospitality is lacking, this will reflect badly on us and make it difficult to invite the Five Great Immortal Sects in the future.

“Not a single room built by the authorities is left?” The provincial governor was unwilling to give up, urging his subordinate to think again.

The subordinate did think of a possible place. “Well, there is one place that can accommodate people, occupies a huge area, has plenty of rooms, and was built by us. All it takes is a word from you to move in, and no spirit stones are required.”

The provincial governor’s eyes lit up. “Where is it?”

“The prison.”

Chapter 352: Heard That Lu Yang Could Battle Opponents Three Major Realms Higher

The provincial governor took two deep breaths, barely restraining the urge to kick his subordinate.

Let guests stay in prison? Do they look like they’re from the Dao-Seeking Sect?

He glared at his subordinate. “Go invite the immortal sect disciples over. We still have a few guest rooms available in the estate. Tidy them up, set up Spirit-Qi Gathering Arrays, and place Heart-Nourishing Stones where appropriate.”

“Yes, sir!”

Soon, three immortal sect disciples, two males and one female, entered the administrative office. They were glowing with vigor, their eyes radiating confidence.

Observing them, the provincial governor nodded inwardly. As expected of immortal sect disciples. It’s obvious at a glance that they are the best among the best. They’ve already formed their golden cores at such a young age—what terrifying talent.

The provincial governor could discern their cultivation realms. According to the correspondence with their sects, these three disciples were not yet eighteen. They all reached the Golden Core stage before eighteen and possess first-grade golden cores; such cultivation speed was rare even in history.

When the Battle of the Great Era arrives, these illustrious talents will probably be the main characters.

“Greetings, Your Excellency. I am Lan Ting of the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace.” Lan Ting was lithe, and her eyes sparkled like stars. With every stride, her white robes and skirt sash fluttered and danced.

“I am Bai Ming of the Five-Elements Sect,” Bai Ming said with his usual cold demeanor.

“Yan Tianzhi. Prison Suppression Sect.” Yan Tianzhi spoke as tersely as possible, as if every one of his words was made of gold.

“I shall entrust tomorrow’s tournament commentary to you three.” The provincial governor’s face was wreathed in smiles. Although the participants tomorrow will be peers of the same age, these three immortal sect disciples’ exceptional knowledge and experience would be far from enough to serve as judges.

“We’ll do our best.”

“By the way, have you three met the representatives from the Dao-Seeking Sect?”

The three shook their heads. They had set off separately from their sects and only convened in Qing Province.

“That’s strange. The letter from the Dao-Seeking Sect mentioned sending two people, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou. They’re the top prodigies of the current generation in the Dao-Seeking Sect. Judging by the time, they should have arrived.” The provincial governor was baffled.

Hearing the familiar names, Lan Ting recalled her days running the barbeque shop in Yanjiang Commandery. Tasked with a mission from her sect, I racked my brain to find a way to infiltrate the Everlasting Creed, only to miss the recruitment window. Later, I encountered Lu Yang’s trio and learned that they had successfully joined the Everlasting Creed.

In the end, I joined forces with Lu Yang’s trio to get rid of the Yanjiang Branch’s leader.

Lu Yang’s trio even earned the favor of the Everlasting Creed’s higher-ups and got promoted, while I returned to the sect to report updates on the mission.

I considered getting in touch with Lu Yang to ask if he needed assistance in other areas—ideally, we could eliminate another branch.

Who would have imagined that in less than two months, news of the Everlasting Creed’s destruction would come? When I first received the news, I stood there in a daze for half a day, wondering if it was just a rumor.

Only two months had passed!

Although it was officially announced that the Dao-Seeking Sect and the imperial court had joined hands to wipe out the Everlasting Creed’s headquarters, I dare bet that Lu Yang was involved!

When we attended a meeting at the Dao-Seeking Sect afterward, their Big Senior Sister even proposed a marriage between me and Lu Yang, frightening Shifu so much that she grabbed me and ran away immediately.

I wonder why Shifu was so scared of the Dao-Seeking Sect’s Big Senior Sister.

The provincial governor interrupted her thoughts. “Is that so...” He didn’t think too much about it. Since the Dao-Seeking Sect replied that two people will be coming, they will definitely come. Perhaps they’re enjoying the grand ceremony today; they’ll head directly to the judges’ seats when the tournament begins tomorrow.

That seems possible.

“By the way, the Hanging Monastery asked me to relay a message. They originally intended to send Senior Brother Shi Chan over, but complications arose during his Buddhist missionary mission, and he couldn’t make it. With their limited members, it’s hard for them to send a replacement.”

Shi Chan was the true lineage disciple of the current generation in the Hanging Monastery.

“Did he meet with some danger? Should I dispatch some assistance?”

“I wouldn’t exactly call it danger. It’s just that he couldn’t comprehend the phrase ‘lay down the butcher’s knife and attain enlightenment on the spot,’[1] so he joined a slaughterhouse to test whether he could attain enlightenment by really laying down the butcher’s knife.”

The provincial governor opened and closed his mouth several times before finally saying, “It’s getting late, my three little friends. Please have a rest in the estate.”

After the provincial governor left, Lan Ting suddenly asked, “Senior Brother Bai Ming, I noticed a change in your expression when the provincial governor mentioned Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou. Do you know them?”

Bai Ming sighed deeply. “Not only do I know them, I’ve even exchanged blows with him.

“Senior Sister Lan Ting, you may not know about this, but four months ago, the Five-Elements Sect headed to the Dao-Seeking Sect for an exchange. During the Foundation Establishment category of the competition, Lu Yang unleashed elemental moves such as the Three Flavor True Fire and Earth Escape Technique. I prided myself on displaying supreme mastery of five-elements spells in class compared to my peers, but Lu Yang countered me at every turn.

“Just before I lost, I had an epiphany and broke through to the Intermediate Foundation Establishment Stage mid-battle. To my horror, I discovered that Lu Yang had been holding back all this time. When he saw me break through, he seemed to have transformed into a different person, with his gaze and movements changed drastically. Before I could even dish out a move, I was defeated in one move of his. Had my shifu not intervene in time, I might have been crippled or killed.”

With the cordial relations between the Five Great Immortal Sects, disciples typically addressed their peers as fellow senior brothers and sisters.

“That strong?!” Lan Ting was floored. I knew about Lu Yang’s astonishing talent, but I didn’t expect him to defeat Bai Ming in one move.

Yan Tianzhi also widened his eyes, expressing his shock as he had sparred with Bai Ming before. Bai Ming is well-versed in spear techniques and five-elements spells, making him a tricky opponent, be it in close or ranged combat. How could he have been defeated in one move?

“According to my shifu, Lu Yang had cast a lost ancient mighty ability—Water-Repelling Mantra. Without specific countermeasures, this move is unstoppable. It can drain all the water in the opponent’s body, desiccating them.” Bai Ming shuddered at the memory of Lu Yang casually deploying the Water-Repelling Mantra. With how effortless it was for him, it looked like if I could somehow survive the Water-Repelling Mantra, he would have worse mighty abilities waiting for me.

“Not only that. First Elder of the Dao-Seeking Sect even personally admitted that Lu Yang had challenged those beyond his level despite being at the Foundation Establishment Stage.”

Yan Tianzhi simply smiled, not paying it any heed. All three of us can challenge those beyond our level. It’s nothing to flaunt about.

Bai Ming continued in a grave voice. “Three major realms beyond! When he was at the Foundation Establishment Stage, he defeated Golden Core, Nascent Soul, and Divine Transfiguration cultivators!”

Lan Ting and Yan Tianzhi were stumped for words. Three levels higher? That only exists in dreams!

Lan Ting recalled her battle with Lu Yang, where they killed the Yanjiang Branch Leader. Lu Yang seemed to be completely in control, handling everything with ease. Now I get why. It’s because he wasn’t using his full strength. novelbuddy-cσ๓

“I suspect that he must have relied on the advantages of the right time, the right place, arrays, and pills,” Bai Ming analyzed. Otherwise, I can’t imagine how a Foundation Establishment cultivator could have defeated a Divine Transfiguration cultivator.

Even with all these external advantages, battling those three major realms higher is still a terrifying feat. At the very least, none of us is capable of that.

“It’s a pity we don’t know where these two have gone.”

“Maybe we’ll get to see them at tomorrow’s tournament.”

1. It means something like those who are willing to turn over a new leaf have the kind heart of a Buddha. ☜

Chapter 353: Why Are You All Sitting at the Judges’ Platform?

As the Qing Province Grand Ceremony commenced officially, all eyes were drawn to the centerpiece event—the tournament for the younger generation.

Every year, the tournament would bring forth young cultivators brimming with immense potential, making those average cultivators sigh toward the heavens in inferiority.

History had also proven their worth. Excluding accidental deaths, most attained fame and success, became sect leaders, or founded their own sects. In addition to the Qing Province’s authorities, numerous sects and factions would watch closely, hoping to poach promising talents.

Perhaps due to the imminent arrival of the Great Era, participants in recent years had been even more outstanding, shattering records from previous years.

“Look! Isn’t that Li Shaoyang from the Wind-Stabilizing Sect. I heard he has already reached the Great Perfection Qi Training Stage. When he left the mountains for travels and encountered bandits, he pierced through three Level Nine bandits with a single thrust of the spear!”

“What?! He’s already at the Great Perfection Qi Training Stage at such a young age? His cultivation realm is guaranteed to rank among the top eight!”

While one could already attempt to break through to the Foundation Establishment Stage at Level Nine Qi Training Stage, to improve the chances of a successful breakthrough, most would conscientiously polish their cultivation realm to achieve what outsiders called “Great Completion Qi Training.” Most cultivators in the audience were at the Qi Training Stage, with the Great Perfection Qi Training Stage representing their greatest goal.

On the other hand, such a concept didn’t exist in the Five Great Immortal Sects. They weren’t even interested in distinguishing between the levels of the Qi Training Stage. In their eyes, there was no difference between the Level One and Great Perfection Qi Training stages.

“And that especially beautiful female cultivator over there! She’s Qiao Hongye from the Sleeveless Sect, a first-class sect. She is also at the Great Perfection Qi Training Stage and has Wood-Fire Dual Spirit Root. During their sect’s internal tournament, she secured first place among several Great Perfection Qi Training disciples!”

“Great Perfection Qi Training cultivators might have been able to rank among the top eight in previous years, but it’s hard to say this year. Rumors say that several Foundation Establishment cultivators are competing this time!”

“Foundation Establishment cultivators under eighteen?! And there are even several of them?!”

His companion acted all mysterious. “Have you heard of Gu Qisheng from the Rainbow Palace? Born at a Yin hour of a Yin month in a Yin year with a Mystic Yin Body. If it weren’t for the palace leader, Gu Qisheng would have died as a baby.

“Heaven envies those with a Mystic Yin Body. They face a great tribulation at birth. If they can overcome it, their cultivation will be smooth. But if they can’t, they will die prematurely.

“Someone saw Gu Qisheng here yesterday, and he was already at the Basic Foundation Establishment Stage.”

~~~

“Hello, we are here to register for the tournament.”

The yamen bailiff at the registration area looked up with a cold demeanor. Most participants registered in advance, but a few would decide to participate at the last minute. Briefly glancing at the two smiling young men, he couldn’t discern their cultivation realms, though he didn’t care much about that. It was common to carry cultivation-concealing magical artifacts when outside.

He pointed to a stone nearby. “This is the lowest-grade black iron stone. Only Advanced Qi Training cultivators can shatter it. Try breaking it.”

The dark iron stone was no different from a block of tofu before the two. With a gentle smack of their palms, the stone split into pieces.

“Foundation Establishment Stage then. This year’s competition seems to be full of hidden talents.

“This is a Growth Ring Stone. Place your hand on it and infuse it with spirit qi.”

On the other side of the bailiff sat a similar stone with multiple ring patterns, specifically used by the cultivation world to assess one’s age.

The two placed their hand on it and infused it with spirit qi. The growth rings lit up one after another before stopping at the seventeenth ring.

“Under eighteen. Eligible for the tournament.

“Name?”

“Lu Yang.”

“Sect?”

“Dao-Seeking Sect.”

“Hmm?” The bailiff’s head snapped up, examining the two as if he had seen ghosts.

Lu Yang was puzzled. “Is there a problem?”

The bailiff remembered the provincial governor’s instructions. “We must encourage more people to participate in the tournament—the more the merrier. Don’t fear notable figures joining; only fear them not joining.”

Having two Dao-Seeking Sect disciples participating would surely make His Excellency very happy.

“No, it’s nothing. You can participate.

“And you, what’s your name?”

”Meng Jingzhou, also from the Dao-Seeking Sect.”

“Here, these are your serial numbers. In just fifteen minutes, there will be a lottery to determine the combat matchup and sequence. Prepare yourselves.”

“No problem!”

~~~

“Strange... the first match of the tournament is about to begin. Why are there still no signs of Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou?” Lan Ting mused while sitting upright at the judges’ platform.

“Maybe they were delayed by unforeseen circumstances on the way,” Bai Ming speculated. That’s a common occurrence. I always run into unexpected situations when I leave the mountain for my own travels and training.

“Wait.” Yan Tianzhi was as terse as usual.

Lan Ting had just gotten to know Yan Tianzhi, and Bai Ming told Lan Ting that with Yan Tianzhi’s laconic nature, it would be hard to count on him for commentaries. She could only resign to her fate. Looks like the important responsibility of providing commentaries has fallen to my shoulders.

Below the judges’ platform, spectators noticed the three of them and whispered among themselves.

“Who are these three people? They look so young. Can they really act as judges? Especially that girl! I’ve certainly never seen someone as beautiful as her, but she just doesn’t seem experienced in combat.”

“That’s because you don’t know. These three are disciples of the Immortal Sect and incredible prodigies. I heard they are the most outstanding among their peers in the sect! And that's not all! Someone in my family works at the administrative office and said they are all at the Golden Core Stage!”

“Golden Core Stage?!”

“Now you know how big the gulf in talent is, don’t you?”

With the cultivation of participants capped at the Foundation Establishment Stage, Golden Core cultivators were enough to serve as judges.

Lan Ting briefly reviewed the details of the cultivators in the first match and announced gently, “Our first contestant is Feng He, true lineage disciple of the first-class sect, Seven Emotions Sect. Not long ago, he broke through to the Foundation Establishment Stage in one go without the aid of Foundation Establishment Pills, instead relying on the foundation he built during the Qi Training Stage. He is now at the Foundation Establishment Stage.

“The Seven Emotions Sect conveys comprehension of the seven emotions and six desires through music, and Feng He has obtained the true legacy of the Seven Emotions Sect. He is proficient in the Dao of Music, and his rendition of the melody Parting Joy made birds halt and flower buds blossom.

“Feng He is also a seeded contestant in this tournament. Let us look forward to his performance!”

The corners of Feng He’s mouth curled into a confident smile. With my Basic Foundation Establishment Stage, there is no doubt I will shine in this tournament.

When one roams the jianghu, strength comes first, and fame comes second.

This tournament is my starting point to attain fame!

“Feng He’s opponent is a cultivator who registered at the last minute...Lu Yang of the Dao-Seeking Sect?!” Lan Ting almost lost her professional composure in the middle of the announcement.

She placed the documents down and looked toward the arena stage. Seeing a familiar figure standing there, her face morphed into an odd expression. She turned to look at Bai Ming and saw that he had the same expression.

When Lu Yang saw Lan Ting and Bai Ming, he first greeted them, but he soon scratched the back of his head in confusion.

What’s going on?

Aren’t we supposed to participate in the tournament? Why are you all at the judges’ platform?

Chapter 354: How Am I Supposed to Give a Commentary on This?

On the stage, Lu Yang sank into contemplation.

Below the stage, Meng Jingzhou sank into contemplation.

Big Senior Sister told us that the Qing Province authorities had invited disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect to participate in the grand ceremony, with the requirement being cultivators under the age of eighteen. We registered to take part in the exchange among the younger generation. No one can find fault with that.

But why are Lan Ting, Bai Ming, and an unfamiliar face sitting at the judge’s platform?

Are they all over eighteen?

Gasps echoed throughout the audience below the stage upon hearing that Lu Yang was from the Dao-Seeking Sect. They didn’t expect someone from the Five Great Immortal Sects to be a contestant. There was no such precedent.

“But who is Lu Yang? Have you heard of him before?” The people were befuddled. Though the Dao-Seeking Sect’s reputation spread far and wide, few recognized Lu Yang.

“Never heard of him. I only know his opponent, Feng He.”

“Me too. Rumors say that Feng He entered the Dao through listening to music, drawing qi into his body and stepping on the path of cultivation. After reaching the Foundation Establishment Stage, he acquired a damaged guqin[1] at an auction, which appeared to be the personal relic of some expert. It caught the attention of plundering cultivators, one at the Basic Foundation Establishment Stage and two at the Advanced Qi Training Stage. However, Feng He captured them instead with the guqin.”

Lu Yang lacked the fame of seeded contestants.

These popular contestants had the backing of their sects, which helped build up their reputation. Their sects would promote how their disciples descended the mountain to exterminate evil for the people, slay the bandits and demons, or clinched first place in their sect’s tournament and were unmatched among peers of the same cultivation realm. If all else failed, the minimum was tragic backstories, where they were orphaned, faced endless adversities, and surmounted countless hurdles to pursue the path of cultivation... In short, whatever stood out would be used for publicity.

As for Lan Ting, Bai Ming, and Yan Tianzhi, through working on their sect missions, they had eradicated evildoers numerous times. Even the local gentry, town mayors, and commandery governors treated them with utmost respect, afraid they might use their immortal sect’s enforcement authority. Their deeds were widely circulated among the common folk, earning them even greater fame than seeded contestants.

In contrast, when Lu Yang was at the Foundation Establishment Stage, he infiltrated the Everlasting Creed, eliminated the provincial governor who doubled as the leader of the Yanjiang Branch, tricked the vice creed leader to his death in the Dao-Seeking Sect, then wiped out the fourteen-thousand-year-old Everlasting Creed.

At the Golden Core Stage, he established the Heavenly Court Creed and deceived the Nine-Netherworlds Creed into temporarily abandoning thoughts of murder and running a barbeque business.

Not only were these operations classified, but even if they were leaked, no one would believe them.

“Oh, it’s a fellow Daoist from the Dao-Seeking Sect! Come, let’s fight!” Feng He was full of confidence, flashing a wide smile. He produced an exquisite guqin from his storage ring, whose golden strings glistened in sunlight.

His shifu had the guqin appraised. This guqin was the relic of a Divine Transfiguration cultivator. With seventy percent of it repaired, though it couldn’t unleash the full power as it did in the hands of a Divine Transfiguration cultivator, even a fraction of such a high-level magical artifact would be a challenge for peers at the same level to withstand.

Feng He indeed had reason to be proud. Lu Yang’s dozen junior brothers and sisters from the same cohort were all under eighteen. Most had recently broken through to the Foundation Establishment Stage, with a few faster ones possibly reaching the Intermediate Foundation Establishment Stage.

Feng He’s cultivation talent was evident.

Notwithstanding, Lu Yang’s junior brothers and sisters were more self-reliant, while Feng He was meticulously groomed by his sect. They were not at all comparable.

Despite facing a peer of the same age who was brimming with confidence, Lu Yang didn’t let his guard down, activating his Unbeatable Golden Core.

Soon, the Unbeatable Golden Core gave its verdict.

“Fight as you please.”

Clang!

The guqin chimed like golden bells, its timber resonating like coiling dragons and crouching tigers. A glimmer of golden light began to vibrate, releasing a powerful sound wave sweeping toward Lu Yang. In an instant, the music from the guqin drew an accurate arc in the air like a white snake, its sound waves carrying a scorching heat and power with hostile intent permeating the air.

Feng He was the first to strike. Channeling his powers into the guqin, he seized the initiative to gain the upper hand from the outset. Regardless of whether Lu Yang forcefully withstood the attack head-on or dodged it, Feng He had already calculated his next step.

Combat is all about schemes!

“The sound waves materialized! He has already mastered this method despite just reaching the Foundation Establishment Stage?” A knowledgeable cultivator gasped. Countless cultivators specializing in music spend one or two decades before mastering this art, yet a junior like Feng He has already achieved it.

“It’s said that Feng He used this very method to defeat the veteran plundering cultivators!”

“The guqin was still damaged then. Now that it has been repaired, it will only be more powerful!”

“Deploying his trump card right from the get-go?”

“Can Lu Yang of the Dao-Seeking Sect withstand this attack?”

Faced with the materialization of the sound waves, Lu Yang didn’t hold back. With a downward swing of his right hand, he dispersed the deadly sound waves. Taking a step forward, he extended his forefinger and released intangible sword qi.

Feng He couldn’t react in time, and his magical artifact automatically moved in front of him to protect its master.

The sharp yet heavy sword qi struck the guqin, its residual shockwaves jarring Feng He’s organs. With his guqin in his arms, Feng He fell out of the arena.

The audience was silent for a split second before erupting into a deafening cacophony of discussions.

“Did you see that move just now? Was that sword qi? It’s my first time seeing sword qi!”

“He dispersed the sound waves with just a swing of his hand and defeated Feng He in one move! This Lu Yang guy is so strong!”

“What exactly is his cultivation realm?!”

~~~

At the judges' platform, Lan Ting was left speechless for a long while.

When the provincial governor first entrusted them with this matter, she thought it would be straightforward. The worst thing that could happen was some skirmishes among Foundation Establishment cultivators, and offering commentary on the contestants’ strengths and weaknesses wouldn’t be difficult.

This situation before her had completely caught her off guard.

What should I say? Praise Lu Yang for defeating contestant Feng He with his Golden Core cultivation?

I can’t bring myself to say that.

Or should I commend Feng He for his soundwave attack, which demonstrated his talent and great potential for the future?

But those supposedly impressive sound waves were smacked into oblivion by Lu Yang...

She turned to look at Bai Ming and Yan Tianzhi.

Bai Ming was silent and seemed to have temporarily gone blind, unable to see the arena stage, while Yan Tianzhi parted his mouth, slowly uttering one word, “Amazing.”

Amazing? What’s amazing? Are you complimenting the supreme precision of Lu Yang’s sword qi, which sent Feng He flying out of the arena without causing him injury?

In the midst of Lan Ting’s confusion, she heard Yan Tianzhi add a few more words. “...lack of shame.” [2]

Lan Ting, “...”

Clearly, I can’t count on these two.

Taking a deep breath, she racked her brain for all the words she could use as she provided her commentary. “Contestant Feng He’s soundwave attack truly exceeded our expectations, living up to his title as a musical genius. Even if other seeded contestants could withstand that blow, they would have been left severely drained and exhausted.

“Unfortunately, Contestant Ma He’s opponent was Contestant Lu Yang, a sword cultivator completely devoted to the Sword Dao and dedicated to pursuing the highest sword techniques. His formless sword qi harbored profound mysteries of the cosmos, showcasing his supreme mastery in the Dao of the Sword!

“Of course, none of the above was the decisive factor that led to Contestant Lu Yang’s victory. The most crucial point is that Contestant Lu Yang is at the Golden Core Stage.”

1. Guqin is probably one of the most common instruments you see in historical C-dramas. It is one of the oldest forms of Chinese qin or zither, which is why guqin is made up of the word “gu” which refers to ancient and “qin.” In the past, it was simply referred to as “qin.” ☜

2. The original first character is actually “good,” but when combined with the additional characters which mean “shameless,” it becomes “so shameless.” ☜

Chapter 355: Challenging Beyond One’s Level, Striking Down Foundation Establishment Opponents

“Golden Core Stage?!”

“A Golden Core cultivator under eighteen? What kind of cultivation talent is this?!”

“It wouldn’t be an exaggeration to call this monstrous!”

“Such cases were rare even in history, right?”

“Not only was it rare, but according to historical records, such talents only emerge once every few centuries!”

The crowd was unaware of Lan Ting and the others’ ages. In truth, Bai Ming was the oldest at eighteen and a few months, while Lan Ting and Yan Tianzhi were a few months shy of eighteen.

The contestants felt mounting pressure, especially the seeded contestants, who were originally brimming with confidence. Having reached the Foundation Establishment Stage, they believed they could defeat the numerous opponents and emerge as the champion. Never could they have imagined that a Golden Core cultivator would participate this year.

What cursed luck is this?

A Foundation Establishment cultivator against a Golden Core cultivator? We might as well bang our heads against a wall.

Only one contestant showed excitement, murmuring, “Golden Core Stage? Interesting.” He was cloaked in black, his facial features obscured.

Wandering the continent, he chanced upon the Qing Province Grand Ceremony and decided to sign up at the last minute. While presenting his cultivation outwardly to be at the Basic Foundation Establishment Stage, that was not his true strength.

He was Zhou Fangge, and his true cultivation was at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage.

“I haven’t fought with an immortal sect disciple before. Although this guy Lu Yang’s cultivation speed is faster than mine, cultivation is not everything in battle. Even if he’s faster than me, it won’t be that much faster. He probably formed his golden core recently.”

Zhou Fangge had once defeated a Basic Golden Core cultivator. Though he struggled, he ultimately won.

“It’s possible to win this battle.

“Hehe, Lu Yang, hope you are a worthy whetstone for my blade!”

~~~

“Get ready, it should be your turn soon.” Lu Yang bumped fists with Meng Jingzhou. It was his first time participating in such a large-scale exchange event, and he found it quite enjoyable.

“Everyone is at a similar age. Maybe there are some formidable opponents hidden among them.”

Meng Jingzhou chuckled. “You don’t say! When have I ever held back in a fight?”

They approached every battle with utmost seriousness, never showing complacency or carelessness.

~~~

From the judges’ platform, Lan Ting’s eyelids twitched at their fist bump. She sent an auditory message to Bai Ming. “You’re handling the commentary for Meng Jingzhou’s match.”

Under Lan Ting’s murderous gaze, Bai Ming had no choice but to nod solemnly, reluctantly accepting this duty.

~~~

The tournament proceeded with spectacular duels. Facing opponents of the same age, both parties didn’t dare let their guard down, employing various intricate schemes and covert spells.

With the contestants going all out and displaying the full gamut of their abilities, it was a thrilling watch for the cultivators in the audience. Most spectators were at the Golden Core Stage, and they didn’t expect that such entertaining battles could occur between Qi Training cultivators.

Even the talent scouts sent by various sects nodded approvingly, finding the quality of participants this year exceptionally high.

“We’re halfway through the tournament, right? Counting the first match, we’ve already seen five Foundation Establishment cultivators. There weren’t so many in previous years.”

“Exactly! Especially the Intermediate Foundation Establishment cultivator from the fifth match! He would’ve been guaranteed first place in previous years!”

Bai Ming briefly scanned the participant roster. “The upcoming match features Shang Deshui from the Vast Sea Sect, who is also a widely recognized seeded contestant. His cultivation is at the Basic Foundation Establishment Stage, and he is proficient in water-type spells, particularly his Water Control Technique.”

Speaking of the Water Control Technique, the corner of Bai Ming’s eye twitched involuntarily as he recalled how Lu Yang had obliterated him with the Water-Repelling Mantra.

Shang Deshui flashed a confident smile. A Basic Foundation Establishment cultivator can sweep through the preliminary rounds with ease.

Bai Ming continued to announce, “Shang Deshui’s opponent is also a cultivator who registered at the last minute—Meng Jingzhou of the Dao-Seeking Sect.”

Meng Jingzhou’s face was wreathed in smiles as he waved at Bai Ming.

“Why is there another disciple from the Dao-Seeking Sect?” Shang Deshui’s smile froze on his face. One wasn’t enough, so there are now two?

Is the Qing Province Grand Ceremony some big event that warrants the participation of two Dao-Seeking Sect disciples?

Calm down. Calm down. Being a disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect doesn’t necessarily imply that he is at the Golden Core Stage. Golden Core cultivators under eighteen only emerge once every few centuries. The worst-case scenario is that he is at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage. With appropriate skillful maneuvers, victory is not out of reach.

Spurring himself on, Shang Deshui retrieved a small bottle from his sleeve. He had spent an exorbitant amount to procure it. Inside was water sourced from the depths of the East Sea, exceptionally pure and suitable for deploying water-type spells.

“Water-Control Technique—Serpent Mimicry!”

Water vapor surged, waves overflowed, and the deep waters of the East Sea flowed out of the bottle as fine threads. As the water accumulated and shifted, it transformed into a menacing python.

“Go!”

The python opened its ferocious maw and charged toward Meng Jingzhou with lightning speed, as if a raging tsunami was crashing toward him. The petrifying aura the python emitted left everyone present affected.

“Heaven-Shaking Six Forms!” Meng Jingzhou placed his hands into position and shattered the python into a curtain of rain with one punch, the undiminished force of his punch halting right in front of Shang Deshui’s face. Unable to withstand the wind from the punch, Chang Deshui staggered several steps back until he fell off the stage.

Bai Ming, “...”

You’re a Golden Core cultivator, yet you used the Heaven-Shaking Six Forms right out of the gate? If I hadn’t known better, I would think your opponent was Lu Yang!

Bai Ming gave a serious commentary. “The Water Control Technique’s Mimicry Chapter is divided into three phases: Serpent Mimicry, Jiao Mimicry, and Dragon Mimicry. Only upon reaching the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage can one grasp the basics of the Water Control Technique. For Shang Deshui to display such exquisite control over water and mimic the serpent at the Basic Foundation Establishment Stage is truly deserving of applause.

“It is clear that Shang Deshui has put in relentless effort off the stage. His deep comprehension of the Dao of Water is also rare for this age. I’ve only witnessed such a level of comprehension from a few of my junior brothers.

“On the path of cultivation, victory and defeat are governed by the will of the heavens. I hope Shang Deshui won't be discouraged by this setback, but instead, will persevere in his pursuit of the Dao of Water with even greater resolve.

“Meng Jingzhou. Golden Core Cultivator.

“End of commentary.”

A new wave of uproar spread through the crowd, the audience filled with admiration for the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Another Golden Core cultivator under eighteen! Is the Dao-Seeking Sect really so powerful? Such peerless prodigies are supposed to appear only once in a few centuries, yet we have seen two appearing at the same time?!

With the first preliminary rounds concluded, aside from the two prominent Golden Core cultivators—Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou—the ten Foundation Establishment cultivators were the most notable. As for those fifty Great Perfection Qi Training cultivators, they were completely overshadowed.

Lu Yang was jubilant about his subsequent matches. The next two matches were against Basic Foundation Establishment cultivators. The suggestion from his Unbeatable Golden Core was “Fight as you please.”

Lu Yang couldn’t help but lament in nostalgia. It’s been a long time since I’ve had such effortless battles.

Recalling the brutal battles in the Dao-Seeking Sect, Lu Yang felt that a tournament like this was best suited for him.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy also found this scene nostalgic, as if she had returned to her glorious days in the ancient era, where she battled those beyond her level. She clamored to take control of Lu Yang’s body to experience it for herself.

With a resigned sigh, Lu Yang relinquished control of his body to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy two matches later so that she could also have a taste of the fun.

Meng Jingzhou mirrored Lu Yang’s sentiments. Ever since he joined the Dao-Seeking Sect, the exchange with the Five-Elements Sect was the only time he had a proper duel with peers of the same age.

I didn’t know fighting with peers of a similar age is so satisfying.

He had much better luck; his next two opponents were at the Great Perfection Qi Training Stage.

Lan Ting and the other two watched the grinning duo, wishing they could pretend they didn’t know them.

After four rounds concluded, eight finalists emerged.

Alongside the undisputed Golden Core cultivators—Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou—was Zhou Fangge, who had concealed his cultivation, an Intermediate Foundation Establishment cultivator, and four Basic Foundation Establishment cultivators.

According to the rules of the tournament, the top eight contestants would face off in a free-for-all battle to be assessed on their adaptability and teamwork skills.

Chapter 356: Unbeatable Golden Core: I Have Never Fought a Battle With Such Overwhelming Advantage

“Six Foundation Establishment cultivators and two Golden Core cultivators. This lineup...” The lucky Foundation Establishment finalists wore troubled expressions.

According to custom, the top eight contestants would duel on the arena stage, with the sequence of elimination determining the top three. Therefore, with the assistance of their sect’s elders, they had crafted strategies, plotting how to eliminate competitors and let themselves remain as long as possible. The tactics included but were not limited to: feigning cooperation, ambushing from the rear, double agents, last-minute betrayals...

However, all plans were useless in this situation. Their only hope of achieving victory was to have six Foundation Establishment cultivators team up against Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

Just as the seeded contestants contemplated how they could deal with this situation, a steady voice declared, “Only if all of you listen to my instructions do we stand a chance of attaining victory.”

The seeded contestants saw that the one who had spoken was the sole Intermediate Foundation Establishment cultivator present.

“So it’s the heir of the Yan Family.”

The Yan Family was a prominent clan in Qing Province, flourishing for six thousand years, with three old Fusion ancestors. Even the provincial governor had to treat them respectfully.

“Heir Yan, if you’re the one giving the commands, we could give it a try.”

With someone accepting the proposal, the remaining cultivators nodded. As Heir Yan had the highest cultivation among everyone present and was backed by the influential Yan Family, he held the highest prestige here. Everyone wholeheartedly agreed to have him take the lead.

“Zhou Fangge, what about you?” Heir Yan turned his gaze to the black-robed youth.

“I’m naturally fine with it.” Zhou Fangge replied with a smile. “But I have one condition. The five of you will handle Meng Jingzhou. Just leave Lu Yang to me.”

Everyone burst out in fury, thinking that Zhou Fangge was overestimating himself. “Are you joking? Your performance so far has been mediocre, yet you dare dream of taking on Lu Yang alone?!”

At this point, only by uniting could the six have any hope of defeating Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou. Now that one of them was practically screaming to throw his life away, how could they not be enraged?

Suddenly, Zhou Fangge unleashed his true cultivation, causing everyone’s expressions to freeze.

His cultivation is even stronger than Heir Yan’s!

“Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage?”

He concealed himself so well. Had it not been for Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, this person would have been the greatest threat. Just imagine—eight fighters engaged in a chaotic battle on the stage when Zhou Fangge reveals his true cultivation at the last moment. Who could possibly resist that?

Zhou Fangge had already anticipated their reactions. He spoke unhurriedly, “Now, am I qualified to face Lu Yang alone? Truth be told, I could have already formed my golden core, guaranteed to be upper third grade. The only reason I’ve held back is to form a first-grade golden core.”

Heir Yan furrowed his brow as he advised, “With all due respect, even if you are already at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage, your chances against Lu Yang still aren’t particularly high.”

Zhou Fangge smirked faintly. “Actions speak louder than words. Since you doubt me, Heir Yan, let’s wait and see.”

“Never mind. The finals are about to begin. Let’s step onto the stage.”

Zhou Fangge laughed heartily as he strode onto the platform.

Seeing Zhou Fangge’s overwhelming confidence, Heir Yan relaxed. If he dared to speak so boldly, it must be because he has something to rely on. Whatever it is, he just needs to defeat Lu Yang.

“As everyone knows, my Yan Family is the most renowned for the Hundred Insights into Weapons, which is unparalleled in offense. Having been taught by my great-grandfather since I was young, I understand it best, so I’ll lead the offense.

“Gu Qisheng, your Mystic Yin Body naturally imbues your attacks with thirty percent cold energy. Even I wouldn’t necessarily gain the upper hand against you. The two of us will attack Meng Jingzhou simultaneously.

“Shi Xuan, you’re familiar with arrays. Use them to disrupt Meng Jingzhou.”

“Yang Jianyi, you have inherited the authentic legacy of talismans. Use the talismans to provide support as you deem fit.

“Sima He, your World-Helping Manor is famed for its Sweet-Dew Restorative Spell. In previous matches, your opponents couldn’t land hits faster than you could heal. Stay in the back and heal Gu Qisheng’s and my injuries!”

Heir Yan made all the arrangements, and before long, a temporary team with well-defined roles was assembled.

~~~

“Senior Brother Meng, please show your guidance!” Heir Yan cupped his fists, his expression resolute.

“Senior Brother Meng, please show your guidance!” the four behind him chorused in unison.

Meng Jingzhou was startled. Before the match, he and Lu Yang had agreed to split the opponents equally. Why are there five coming at me?

Heir Yan didn’t give Meng Jingzhou any time to think. Wielding an axe in his left hand and a yue-axe[1] in his right, he deftly brandished his weapons, making them seem like a dragon swimming through the clouds and an eagle soaring through the sky. His movements were fierce and rapid, causing one to shake involuntarily.

Gu Qisheng tensed his muscles, and with a slight jolt of his spear tip, he thrust it toward Meng Jingzhou with a whoosh. Surging true qi stirred a violent gust, creating an unusually grandiose sight.

The other three weren’t idle either.

A dazzling array flared beneath Meng Jingzhou’s feet, trapping his legs as if they were sunk in quicksand and rendering him immobile.

Paper swallows folded from talismans flew out from Yang Jianyi’s sleeves, sealing off every possible escape route, giving Meng Jingzhou no chance to dodge.

Sima He silently recited an incantation that streamed into the ears of Heir Yan and Gu Qisheng. With their psyche and spirit platforms cleansed, their spiritual consciousness temporarily surged. Discarding all external distractions, they dedicated their all to the battle, the weapons in their hands gaining newfound power.

The seamless coordination of the five drew gasps from the audience. Even Golden Core cultivators watching the scene paled slightly as they recognized how thorny the situation was, doubting they themselves could escape unscathed. It’d be extremely embarrassing for Golden Core cultivators to be wounded by Foundation Establishment cultivators.

Lu Yang retracted his gaze and studied Zhou Fangge with a baffled expression. “Just you alone? You seem to be only at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage, right?”

Zhou Fangge’s heart skipped a beat. Since his debut, this was his first time encountering someone who could see through his cultivation realm. Nevertheless, he remained dauntless, replying with a cold smirk. “I alone am enough.”

He had once defeated a Basic Golden Core cultivator without resorting to his trump cards, relying on his solid foundation and skills. However, now that I’m up against an elite cultivator like Lu Yang, I naturally can’t secure victory so easily.

Hence, he decided to use his trump card.

I understand the mindset of high-level cultivators. The higher their cultivation, the higher they set their sights. They only spar with peers of the same realm, looking down on those lower-level cultivators. When facing an opponent with a lower cultivation realm, they’ll inevitably let their guard down. And that will be my opportunity!

I will make Lu Yang understand that cultivation realms aren’t everything! Combat prowess is the core—what truly matters!

Noting Zhou Fangge’s brimming confidence, Lu Yang figured he possessed some extraordinary methods. Staying vigilant, he retrieved the Qingfeng Sword from his identity jade token and prepared to give it his all.

Then, he activated the Unbeatable Golden Core to search for a countermeasure. The Unbeatable Golden Core extracted a wisp of Lu Yang’s spirit energy, spinning rapidly before delivering its analysis.

“The other party is at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage. His pupils are black with flecks of gray—a trait of the Vast Haziness Dao Physique. The Vast Haziness Dao Physique is vast, hazy, immeasurable, and boundless, granting him a spirit energy reserve ten times that of those at the same level and allowing him to excel in prolonged battles. The longer the fight drags on, the more disadvantageous it becomes for his opponent. It’s hard for him to find a rival among those at his level. Challenging opponents beyond his level is also normal for him.”

Lu Yang pressed further. “So, how should I fight him?”

“Fight as you please.”

Chapter 357: Modest Declinations

“What kind of nonsense golden core is this? It rambled on and on, but the conclusion didn’t change at all!” Lu Yang snapped in anger.

“What do you mean ‘it rambled on and on?’ It was analyzing the situation for you.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was determined to defend the reputation of her Unbeatable Golden Core. After all, I’m the creator of the Unbeatable Golden Core. I can’t let Lu Yang slander it.

Just as Lu Yang and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy were locked in a heated debate over the pill’s usefulness, Zhou Fangge seized his opportunity to strike.

“Kill!” Zhou Fangge whipped out four small flags from the front of his robes and flung them into the air. Landing in the four cardinal directions, they encircled Lu Yang.

Lu Yang felt darkness loom over him. Looking up, he saw a mountain appear overhead, descending at a terrifying speed.

“Mountain-Moving Divine Ability!” Lan Ting recognized the spell Zhou Fangge had used. Even Golden Core cultivators would struggle to cast this mighty ability, yet Zhou Fangge had leveraged the four small flags to unleash a divine ability beyond his cultivation realm.

Zhou Fangge wasn’t taking any chances, dishing out one of his trump cards. This will be enough to immobilize a Golden Core cultivator.

As the mountain bore down on Lu Yang, he countered with an ancient mighty ability.

“Swallowing Heaven Devouring Earth!” Lu Yang opened his mouth and swallowed the mountain whole, even letting out a satisfied burp.

“It’s Swallowing Heaven Devouring Earth from the Taotie Tribe!” Bai Ming’s face twisted in incredulity. This is the cornerstone of the Taotie Tribe’s existence. To think that Lu Yang mastered it.

Compared to the Mountain-Moving Divine Art, learning Swallowing Heaven Devouring Earth was several magnitudes harder. Bai Ming had heard that even pure-blooded taotie couldn’t master this mighty bloodline ability at the Golden Core Stage.

“I knew Lu Yang had more than one ancient mighty ability!” Yan Tianzhi narrowed his eyes. As expected of a cultivator who can challenge those at a higher level. He’d even learned a mighty ability like Swallowing Heaven Devouring Earth. I also know Swallowing Heaven Devouring Earth, but it’s a shortcut. It can’t be compared to Lu Yang, who mastered it with genuine skill.

Zhou Fangge hadn’t expected his meticulously prepared trump card to be so easily neutralized. “As expected of an immortal sect disciple. But I came prepared!”

He clapped his hands together, unleashing a blinding white light and an ear-splitting noise that forced the audience to cover their ears. A searing ball of lightning coalesced in Zhou Fangge’s palms, its glow casting eerie shadows across his face.

“This is Palm Lightning.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy recognized the spell. “The Heaven Mandate Immortal developed this. He used it when he was one of the opponents I challenged beyond my level back then. However, to catch me off guard, he had condensed the spell in the soles of his feet. After that, this move was circulated, and I don’t know how it evolved into a palm version.[1]

“...maybe it’s for aesthetic purposes.”

While Lu Yang was in the middle of his conversation, Palm Lightning struck down at him.

Boom!

The Palm Lightning erupted with terrifying force, engulfing the stage in dust. Even Heir Yan and the others, who were in the midst of battle, felt the impact of the shockwaves.

Zhou Fangge panted heavily. Palm Lightning was a spell he had inherited from a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator. Despite possessing ten times the spirit qi of his peers, he had exhausted his spirit energy to execute Palm Lightning.

“Even an Intermediate Golden Core cultivator would be lucky to survive this move, let alone a Basic Golden Core cultivator like you!” Zhou Fangge snickered. This is the price for underestimating me.

“Oh, is that so? I was wondering why it didn’t even tickle.” Lu Yang’s voice echoed from within the dust, sending chills down Zhou Fangge’s spine.

As Zhou Fangge assumed his stance and braced himself for Lu Yang’s attack, Lu Yang appeared behind him and patted his shoulder cheerfully.

Zhou Fangge instinctively leaped toward the front, but Lu Yang’s hand was unexpectedly heavy like a mountain, tilting Zhou Fangge off-balance.

Swallowing a Qi Restoration Pill, Zhou Fangge eyed Lu Yang warily. “As expected of an immortal sect disciple. If even that couldn’t hurt you, I won’t hold back anymore.”

His third trump card came at a heavy price, yet it was enough to rival an Advanced Golden Core cultivator. For the sake of victory, however, he felt it was a gamble worth taking.

Just as Zhou Fangge steeled himself to activate his ultimate move, he suddenly became weightless. The scenery before him changed so quickly that it blurred.

It was because Lu Yang had grabbed his collar and hurled him off the stage.

In the midst of their gruelling battle, Heir Yan and the others saw Lu Yang effortlessly defeating the confident Zhou Fangge and could only sigh helplessly.

And he dared claim he could defeat Lu Yang? The guy wasn’t even using his full strength. Didn't you realize that Lu Yang never even raised his sword arm the whole time?

Following which, they heard the dreaded words as despair consumed their hearts. “Haha, Old Meng, you’re still not done? So slow! Let me join!”

Lan Ting and the other two couldn’t help but close their eyes, unable to bear the sight. Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou could contend with even Basic Nascent Soul cultivators. Beating a bunch of Foundation Establishment cultivators is easier than beating children.

Seeing Lu Yang enter the fray, Heir Yan and his team abandoned their battle plans and allocated roles, scattering in panic.

Rather than going headstrong into battle, they thought it’d be better to flee and compare their luck. The lucky one might be the last one to step out of the arena and snag third place.

As the audience watched the gleeful duo chase Heir Yan and the others around like little chicks, they couldn’t help but feel that Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou weren’t good people.

“Why do I feel so bad for Heir Yan and the others?”

“Right? Golden Core cultivators beating Foundation Establishment cultivators and grinning so happily? Do they even have any sense of shame?”

“Big Brother Meng, I’m from the Qing Province Yan Family! We’re both from ancestral clans!” Heir Yan stated his identity, trying his best to build some rapport as fellow members of ancestral clans. He had long heard of Meng Jingzhou’s reputation.

Meng Jingzhou had a solemn expression. “This is a tournament. We are all equal here. How could you use your status to determine the outcome? Holding back against you would be an insult to the spirit of competition. Acting this way will disgrace the Yan Family’s honor.”

Heir Yan gingerly asked, “Then, Big Brother Meng, wouldn’t you participating in this tournament as a Golden Core cultivator bring disgrace to the Meng Family?"

“Of course not. I’ve run away from home.”

And then, Heir Yan was kicked off the stage.

After Gu Qisheng voluntarily leaped off the stage, only Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou remained.

“Looks like first and second place will be decided between us.” Lu Yang grinned. He hadn’t gotten his fill of fighting earlier, but now he could fight without restraint.

Meng Jingzhou was also grinning. As his golden core aura emanated from him, even the pebbles on the ground trembled. “Come to think of it, we’ve never actually sparred. This is a good opportunity.”

“My thoughts exactly.” Lu Yang released his aura, matching Meng Jingzhou’s.

On the arena stage, two aura waves, far exceeding what Basic Golden Core cultivators should possess, clashed violently. The entire stage churned like a pot of boiling water, a fearsome sight.

Suddenly, Lu Yang remembered something and called up to the judges’ platform. “Hey, Lan Ting, I forgot to ask something.”

“Go ahead.”

“Is there a prize for first place?”

Lan Ting showed a trace of a smile, which Lu Yang found oddly unsettling. “Of course.”

“What is it?”

“The prize for third place is a set of golden core formation spirit items, which boosts the success rate by fifty percent, with a ten percent chance of attaining a first-grade golden core.

“The prize for second place is a set of golden core spirit items and the provincial governor’s personal golden core formation insights.

“As for first place? On top of the golden core formation spirit items and insights, the provincial governor said that the contestants lack combat and golden core experience, so he asked the three of us judges to personally give the champion some combat pointers.”

Lu Yang blinked at the eerie smiles of Lan Ting and the other two, his hair standing on end. He immediately turned to leap off the stage.

“Old Meng, I’ll give first place to you!”

Meng Jingzhou grabbed Lu Yang and jumped off the stage himself. “My luck is too thin, and my fate profile cannot bear the weight of first place. It’s all yours!”

Chapter 358: Exchanging Blows

Boom! Boom! Boom!

On the stage, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou clashed fist to fist, their footwork and movements so precise that even the slightest shift allowed them to evade attacks. Noticing the control they exhibited over their power, the Golden Core cultivators in the audience felt their eyes twitch nervously as they gulped. Despite the intensity of their duel, not a single stray wisp of energy leaked out; it’s hard to believe that they’re only at the Basic Golden Core Stage.

No...could such mastery truly belong to Golden Core cultivators at all?

“You have the Single’s Curse Fist! Taking on three at once should be nothing!”

“Nonsense! My Single’s Curse Fist only works on men. It’ll even boost their combat power! You have the Lu-Style Arhat Fist. Why fear three measly opponents?”

“You must be joking. If I use the Arhat Fist, even if Lan Ting spares me, the whole Moon Laurel Immortal Palace won’t let me off! Besides, didn’t you want to be in first place? I’ll just concede it to you!”

“Oh, I’m not in such a rush. First place should still be yours.”

And thus, their battle ensued—for second place.

In one-on-one fights, they feared no one. But one against three? Unless their brains had been wholly replaced by the Unbeatable Golden Core, no one would take such a big gamble.

Lu Yang tried to jump off the stage, only for Meng Jingzhou to yank him back by the shoulder.

Meng Jingzhou tried to jump off the stage, only for Lu Yang to grab his wrist and hurl him backward.

The two scrambled to leap off the stage, but their attempts were thwarted by the other party.

After a heated tussle, the two were in a deadlock and tumbled off the stage together.

Bai Ming stood and applauded. “A tie for first place! Let’s give them a round of applause!”

Skipping the post-match commentary, Bai Ming leaped onto the stage from the judges’ platform, his platinum-patterned spear in hand. Lan Ting and Yan Tianzhi followed close behind.

Bai Ming addressed them with a frosty expression, though it almost cracked with schadenfreude. “Congratulations, Senior Brother Lu, Senior Brother Meng Jingzhou. I didn’t expect you to defeat so many talented Foundation Establishment cultivators and claim victory!”

Lu Yang protested, “I think there’s some misunderstanding between us! Lan Ting, you know me. I never bully juniors or those weaker than me!”

“Attack!” Bai Ming didn’t give Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou any chance to speak. This opportunity to spar is hard to come by. If we waste it, who knows when the next time will be?

As the most gifted disciple in the Five-Elements Sect, it was challenging for him to find worthy opponents. None of his peers at the same realm could defeat him, while fighting those at higher realms felt off. Only the disciples from the other four immortal sects could be his rivals.

As Bai Ming thrusted his spear upward, a white mark was drawn on the stage.

Lu Yang raised his sword in defense and deflected the spear tip, on full alert as if he was facing a formidable adversary.

“Not bad, your spear attack. I didn’t feel such pressure when I was in a violent battle with those Foundation Establishment cultivators just now!” Excitement began to pump through Lu Yang, his eyes gleaming with restlessness. Since they want a fight, let’s have a real one!

Wasn’t this the reason for coming to the Qing Province Grand Ceremony—to engage with peers of the same age?

Provoked by Lu Yang, Bai Ming ignited the Sun True Fire at the tip of his spear. The surrounding temperature soared, the heatwave penetrating even the protective arrays and reaching the audience below the stage.

Lu Yang raised an eyebrow. He remembered Bai Ming unleashing the Jinwu Crow Flame at the Foundation Establishment Stage. Looks like after advancing to the Golden Core Stage, his Jinwu Crow Flame has evolved into the Sun True Fire, equally renowned as the Pure Yang True Fire.

Of course, in terms of raw power, it can’t match Meng Jingzhou’s Pure Yang True Fire, which is the result of two Single’s Golden Cores. No Single’s Spirit Root cultivator in history had dared to go to such extremes.

“Break!” Lu Yang shouted as the sound of his Qingfeng Sword slicing through the air reverberated through the stage. Spectators at lower realms winced, as if needles had pricked their eyes.

“It’s sword qi!” a Golden Core cultivator in the audience gasped. He had heard that once sword qi reached a certain realm, even looking at it could harm the body, though he had never witnessed someone attaining such a realm, yet here was Lu Yang, a Basic Golden Core cultivator whose sword qi could already injure people.

The sword qi sliced through the Sun True Fire, scattering embers that scorched small pits into the stage.

Not even the battle between Heir Yan’s team and Meng Jingzhou had left a scratch on the stage.

Lu Yang laughed heartily, brimming with heroic grandeur. “Lan Ting, you and Bai Ming can come at me together!”

Lan Ting smiled faintly. “As you wish, Senior Brother Lu Yang.” Her skirt’s sash fluttered like a swimming dragon, coiling around Lu Yang before snapping taut, aiming to bind him.

“Shrinking Earth!”

Having anticipated her move, Lu Yang darted underground, dodging the waistband.

“This little girl is quite interesting; she also has an immortal physique. You’ve got a fight on your hands.” Inside his mental space, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was observing the battle in the real world.

“Lan Ting also has an immortal physique?” Lu Yang had assumed she had a Single Spirit Root.

“Yes, she has a Genesis Immortal Physique. Legend says that this was the first immortal physique humanity mastered. Before the cultivation system was established, the mainstream cultivation method of humans was Qi Training—drawing qi into the body and absorbing myriad qi from nature. Those who succeeded were called Qi Refining Practitioners.

“However, the cultivation method of Qi Refining Practitioners was ultimately not universal, so humanity gradually abandoned it.

“The first Qi Refining Practitioner had a Genesis Immortal Physique. He pioneered humanity’s cultivation, leading humans to defend against demon beasts and natural calamities, allowing humanity to anchor their footing in an era of savagery. ‘Genesis first stirred; dawn of humanity.’ That was how the name ‘Genesis Immortal Physique’ came about.

“So, do you want me to help you fight?”

“No need. I’ll test the Unbeatable Golden Core first.”

~~~

Yan Tianzhi silently walked toward Meng Jingzhou, a faint glow tracing from his back to his neck. It was only then that Meng Jingzhou noticed his opponent had a tattoo.

A phantom demon beast emerged behind him. It had the body of a goat, teeth of a tiger, eyes in its armpits, and wails of a crying infant, grating on one’s nerves.

“Taotie?” The crowd below the stage buzzed with confusion.

Someone in charge of scouting talents for their sect explained to the crowd, “That’s the battle tattoo of the Prison Suppression Sect. From the Foundation Establishment Stage, disciples can inscribe the images of demons and monsters onto their bodies to obtain their power and mighty abilities. Each higher realm they progress to allows them to add the tattoo of another demon beast.

“However, it’s my first time seeing a cultivator with a taotie battle tattoo at the Golden Core Stage.”

“So you’re a senior brother from the Prison Suppression Sect. Our elders hold your sect’s battle tattoo method in high esteem.” Meng Jingzhou cupped his fists. “Meng Jingzhou, Dao-Seeking Sect.”

“Yan Tianzhi, Prison Suppression Sect.” Yan Tianzhi opened his mouth, and the phantom taotie grew more distinct, almost as if it were alive.

“Swallowing Heaven Devouring Earth!”

A hurricane howled across the stage, its terrifying suction force threatening to drag Meng Jingzhou off his feet.

“Heaven-Shaking Six Forms: Quaking Earth Swaying Mountains!”

Meng Jingzhou remained unflustered, countering with punches that rumbled like muffled thunder, each strike compressing the air into shockwaves. Yan Tianzhi swallowed them all, but the acute pain in his abdomen forced him to interrupt his taotie ability.

As Meng Jingzhou gathered his inner force, it felt as if the heavens were shaking, the earth was quaking, and gales were surging with frightening momentum. On the other hand, Yan Tianzhi was like a taotie in human form, devouring all things.

Deafening booms resounded with every collision of their massive fists, sending chills down people’s spines. Sweat streamed down from their faces, which were wreathed in exhilaration.

The two had almost blurred into afterimages. Those with weaker eyesight couldn’t even catch sight of their figures. The top eight contestants of the tournament could keep track of their movements—but only barely, and their spirit platforms couldn’t keep up.

“Is this really the combat power of Basic Golden Core cultivators?” The Golden Core cultivators in the audience were filled with disbelief, wondering if the golden cores they had cultivated had been fed to dogs.

“What kind of golden cores are theirs... oh right, isn’t there a Golden Core Appreciation Convention? Bring those people here to take a look!”
