Chapter 359: Golden Core Appreciation Convention

Within a lavish courtyard, dazzling golden light pulsed intermittently. As the golden radiance dissipated, a golden core emanating misty vapor rotated slowly, drawing wisps of spirit qi from all directions.

“I’ve long heard that Fellow Daoist Yuan Zhi had formed a Moon Embracing Golden Core. As expected of an upper third-grade golden core! It truly lives up to its reputation!” An old man stroked his beard, his wrinkles showing as he chuckled.

“You flatter me. Thirty years of arduous cultivation only yielded this third-grade Moon Embracing Golden Core. It’s honestly a laughing stock. Besides, Old Teacher Kang, with your knowledge and experience, this golden core is nothing.”

Old Teacher Kang was an erudite scholar passionately devoted to his studies. Recognized by the academy in the imperial city, he commanded immense respect throughout Qing Province.

Someone quickly interjected, “Fellow Daoist Yuan Zhi, what you said is not quite right. Even forming fourth or fifth-grade golden cores is a struggle for us; a third-grade golden core is already considered a feat. Our greatest wish is to successfully shatter our golden cores to form nascent souls, but you’re different—you can break through the Nascent Soul Stage and attain the Divine Transfiguration Stage or even beyond, becoming a Void Refinement cultivator that even Fusion cultivators fear!”

While mid-third-grade cores offered a chance at achieving the Divine Transfiguration Stage, the odds were overwhelmingly slim. They didn’t dare hope for much, satisfied if they could even reach the Nascent Soul Stage.

On the other hand, Yuan Zhi’s upper-third-grade golden core ensured his future advancement to the Nascent Soul and Divine Transfiguration stages, with even the Void Refinement or Fusion stages plausible. His potential was boundless, far surpassing theirs.

Despite Yuan Zhi’s claim, he was secretly unable to contain his glee. Upper-third-grade golden core. That already places me above ninety percent of Golden Core cultivators. Although I may only be at the Basic Golden Core Stage, even Intermediate and Advanced Golden Core cultivators won’t dare to underestimate me. In fact, they’ll have to treat me with deference.

In Serenity Courtyard, an ongoing Golden Core Appreciation Convention featured a myriad of dazzling golden cores, drawing gasps of awe from the crowd.

Yuan Zhi’s Moon-Embracing Golden Core was the most conspicuous; it was extraordinary even among upper-third-grade golden cores.

Just as Yuan Zhi basked in pride, a figure bolted into the small courtyard. “Quick, go check out the arena! It’s extremely lively over there!”

Yuan Zhi was displeased with the intruder. Just a cultivator with a lower-third-grade golden core who’s not even worthy to attend the Golden Core Appreciation Convention. “What’s there to check out? Isn’t it just a bunch of Basic Foundation Establishment cultivators competing for first place?”

“No! Disciples from the Five Great Immortal Sects are battling, and they’re all at the Golden Core Stage! Apart from the Hanging Monastery, all four immortal sects are present!”

“What?!”

“Immortal sect disciples battling?!” The crowd erupted with joy. It was rare to witness disciples from immortal sects battling.

Old Teacher Kang was the most excited as he hurriedly asked, “Are there disciples from the Dao-Seeking Sect?”

“Yes, and there are even two of them!”

Without another word, Old Teacher Kang sprinted in the direction of the arena, displaying agility that outpaced even the youths.

The crowd followed, leaving Yuan Zhi rooted to the spot in a daze.

“I’d like to see exactly how these immortal sect disciples are stronger than me!” So what if they’re disciples from immortal sects? Aren’t their golden cores also upper-third-grade, just like mine?

By the time Yuan Zhi arrived, the area around the stage was already packed. A clash between the most outstanding immortal sect disciples was an event that one might not have the opportunity to witness in decades. This battle alone made everyone feel that attending the Qing Province Grand Ceremony was worth it—though they could hardly see the battle on stage.

Yuan Zhi could only resort to spells to stealthily worm his way into the front row, rejoining his fellow Daoists from the Golden Core Appreciation Convention.

However, none of his fellow Daoists noticed him. Their eyes were glued to the five combatants on stage, no one daring to blink for fear of missing even the tiniest detail.

Aside from Old Teacher Kang, the group consisted of cultivators who had just reached the Golden Core Stage. Watching the five fighters on the stage filled them with a sense of absurdity—they wondered if they had yet to form their golden cores and were still at the Foundation Establishment Stage.

“Is this the strength and speed Golden Core cultivators should possess?!” Putting combat skills aside, Lu Yang and the other four demonstrated strength and speed that dwarfed them.

The competitive spirit that just sparked in Yuan Zhi’s heart was also doused. He suspected that he couldn’t last more than ten moves against any of the five.

We all have upper-third-grade golden cores, yet the gulf is this massive?

“Old Teacher Kang, have you identified what kind of golden cores these five immortal sect disciples have?” Since it wasn’t a Golden Core Appreciation Convention that was currently happening on the stage, where participants displayed their golden cores for all to see, others could only infer from the combat’s subtleties. Unfortunately, their limited experience didn’t allow them to discern anything.

Old Teacher Kang’s brow was scrunched up; he also couldn’t deduce much. “As of now, what I can be certain of is that their golden cores are first-grade and rank among the highest echelons.”

Everyone nodded. Nothing else could explain the tremendous combat prowess of these five immortal sect disciples.

“The one named Meng Jingzhou is overflowing with yang energy that soars to the heavens and resembles a blazing sun, dispelling all ghosts before him. He appears to have a Sun Golden Core, or rather, a Pure Yang Golden Core. However, neither should exhibit such intensity. How peculiar—could there be a golden core with yang energy that outshines both the Sun Golden Core and Pure Yang Golden Core?

“As for that female disciple, she moves with the grace of an immortal, exhaling white mist with every breath. Her aura is enduring, and her stamina astonishing, while her bright eyes resemble the first rays of dawn. She appears to have the legendary Genesis Golden Core. Alas, historical records of this golden core are sparse. I dare not make an assertive claim. The younger generation is terrifyingly impressive.”

Old Teacher Kang doubted even the old scholars from the Imperial Capital Academy could decipher much.

~~~

On the stage, Lu Yang retreated repeatedly under Lan Ting and Bai Ming’s coordinated attacks.

“Lu Yang, stop pretending. I know you have a cloning technique.” Bai Ming noticed Lu Yang’s signs of weariness and didn’t dare to let his guard down. Lu Yang’s true ability is way more than what he is letting on now.

It was Lu Yang’s clone that defeated me the last time!

“You didn’t fall for it.” Lu Yang was troubled. He had hoped to lure Bai Ming over and ambush him with his Tree-Planting Mantra.

“Cloning technique?” Lan Ting turned to Lu Yang, her eyes sparkling with curiosity. Senior Brother Lu Yang even managed to learn such a technique. As expected of the most gifted spellcaster I know.

Lu Yang produced two Twin Lotus Flower seeds and cast the Tree-Planting Mantra. The lotus flowers bloomed, and Lu Yang and his lotus clone stood on the lotus leaves.

“So what if you have a clone? Can your spiritual consciousness control two people at once?” Bai Ming knew the flaw of the cloning technique. The last time we sparred, Lu Yang’s main body was sitting at the stand, so he could focus on controlling his wooden clone. But it’s different this time. He needs to control two bodies at a time, which places an extremely high demand on his spiritual consciousness

“We’ll just have to test it out.” Lu Yang smiled. I couldn’t do it in the past, but after forming my golden core, my spiritual consciousness has expanded exponentially; no peers at the same realm can outmatch me.

Lu Yang looked at the Qingfeng Sword in his hand. After some thought, he threw it to his lotus flower clone, tasking it with fighting Lan Ting.

“I should forge another sword. Never mind, I’ll think about it another time.” Lu Yang prepared to take on Bai Ming with his bare hands. “Warm-up is over. Time to use the Unbeatable Golden Core... How do I defeat these two people?”

Soon, the Unbeatable Golden Core gave its response.

“Use the Arhat Fist against Bai Ming.”

Lu Yang’s lips widened into a smile.

Chapter 360: Power of the Unbeatable Golden Core

Casting aside the side effect of causing baldness, the Arhat Fist was the supreme fist technique of Buddhist sects. Previously, Lu Yang had refrained from using it for fear of accidentally harming Lan Ting. However, now that his clone was in charge of handling Lan Ting while he dealt with Bai Ming, he could finally unleash the Arhat Fist without restraint.

“Let’s see how you’re going to divide your attention!” Bai Ming was certain that Lu Yang couldn’t control two bodies simultaneously. His sharp spear immediately thrust forward like a shooting star across the night sky.

Lu Yang calmly tracked the spear’s tip, a hollow resonance emanating from within him, as if Buddha was chanting sutras to deliver all living beings from suffering. His fists shot forth with thunderous momentum, meeting the spear in a violent collision that sent ink-wash ripples pulsing through the air.

“Arhat Fist!”

Clang!

The spear shook with metallic echoes while Lu Yang’s fists danced lightly on its tip, pressing relentlessly toward Bai Ming.

Exerting his core strength, Bai Ming synchronized his waist and stance to withdraw his spear, but Lu Yang’s continuous Arhat Fist strikes kept the spear vibrating uncontrollably and challenging to grip.

This is bad, Bai Ming cursed inwardly. He had been guarding against Lu Yang’s mighty abilities and spells, not anticipating that Lu Yang possessed such terrifying prowess even when fighting with his bare hands.

Watching the fists close in, Bai Ming formed hand seals with his left hand. A howling wind blade descended from the sky like an executioner’s blade, threatening to bisect Lu Yang.

Though Bai Ming used this opportunity to evade, the Arhat Fist still grazed him.

“What heavy fists!” Bai Ming’s heart raced. Luckily, I dodged. The momentum in this punch carries so much force that just brushing past it had caused an injury like this. Had it landed directly, the consequences would have been devastating.

I absolutely can’t get hit again.

Suddenly, a few strands of black hair drifted down, making Bai Ming freeze. Before he could process what was happening, more and more hair strands began to cascade down.

Wait, this couldn’t be...

Bai Ming instinctively touched his scalp, and his face paled. “Where’s my hair?!”

Staring at the hair scattered over the ground, Bai Ming glared furiously at Lu Yang. “Fists and spells as one! I never imagined you could integrate fist and spell techniques so impeccably that even I fell for it!” Bai Ming forced himself to analyze the situation calmly and not lose himself to panic.

An endless stream of cultivators was still hurrying toward the arena to watch the battle.

“Eh, who’s that bald guy? I thought the Hanging Monastery didn’t send anyone?”

“I heard something about an arhat from afar. Is this bald guy claiming to be one?” ƒreewebηovel.com

“Another unknown earth-type spell!” Bai Ming refused to be outdone in elemental spells. As he burrowed out of the ground, Lu Yang’s fist met him squarely.

“Draw Underground Prison!” Lu Yang locked him in the underground prison again.

Bai Ming struggled to remain clear-headed. Since I can’t go out directly, I’ll escape from somewhere else. Trapped deep underground in this dungeon, no elemental spells except earth-type spells are viable.

He was about to burrow somewhere else and had just shifted half his body out when Lu Yang’s voice rang out from above. “Draw Underground Prison.”

Back in place.

“Earth Dragon...” Bai Ming formed hand seals, preparing to summon the earth dragon.

“Draw Underground Prison.”

Bai Ming jolted and disappeared from his original position before reappearing, his hand seals interrupted.

“This is not an earth-type spell but a spatial spell!” Bai Ming finally realized the problem. “I don’t believe this! Earth Dragon...”

“Draw Underground Prison.”

Crouched and drawing circles, Lu Yang monitored Bai Ming with his spiritual consciousness. Any movement from Bai Ming, and Lu Yang would interrupt it with Draw Underground Prison.

After several failed attempts, Bai Ming’s temper was deflated. “Fine, I admit defeat!” I have no other choice.

When he emerged from the ground, he was infuriated by Lu Yang’s grin. “If not for you casting spells faster than me...” Bai Ming spoke through clenched teeth. I was held back by my spellcasting speed. My earth-type spells prioritize large-scale attacks and are on the slower side. If I had cast my spells before Lu Yang could cast “Draw Underground Prison,” I would have been able to escape and continue battling with him, and the outcome might have been different.

Lu Yang smiled but did not comment. He recalled the proposal the Unbeatable Golden Core had provided earlier.

Bai Ming’s spear technique serves as the exterior, while his five-elements spells form the core. The foundation of his attacks will certainly be five-elements spells. As the five elements interact, they promote and counter each other, combining with amplified power. It is not advisable to give him any openings.

It is recommended to aggravate the opponent with the Arhat Fist and cause him to lose his rationality. Seize this opportunity to cast “Draw Underground Prison” to confine him underground, limiting his options to earth-type spells. You can take advantage of your fast spellcasting speed to interrupt his spells, forcing him to surrender.

This is the most time- and energy-efficient solution.

Chapter 361: I. Admit. Defeat.

Truth be told, when the Unbeatable Golden Core provided such a meticulous proposal, Lu Yang was awestruck.

Previously, the Unbeatable Golden Core only provided two suggestions—either flee for his life or fight as he wished—making Lu Yang treat the Unbeatable Golden Core merely as a cultivation detection tool.

I never expected that it could really offer reliable strategies against formidable opponents.

As expected of a golden core endorsed by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy!

“Hehe, now you know how amazing my Unbeatable Golden Core is!” It was a rare chance the Everlasting Immortal Fairy got to be smug. She climbed out of bed, conjured a chair, and plopped down, crossing her legs and swinging her foot idly. “From now on, you have to show this immortal more respect! My abilities are far more than this!

“My shoulders are sore. Massage them.” She gestured for Lu Yang to serve her.

As Yun Zhi’s little junior brother, the number one cultivator among peers of his age, the number one Golden Core cultivator in the Sword Dao, and a disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect’s leader, Lu Yang couldn’t find any fault with massaging an immortal senior.

“Is this force acceptable?”

“Use more force. Mmm~, that’s more like it.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was satisfied with Lu Yang’s attitude.

~~~

The moment Bai Ming surrendered, the crowd erupted in an uproar. None of them had expected Bai Ming to lose so quickly. Since Lu Yang and Bai Ming were fellow disciples of immortal sects at the Basic Golden Core Stage, the spectators had assumed that there shouldn’t have been a significant difference in strength.

“It’s said that Bai Ming is proficient in five-elements spells, yet he only cast metal- and earth-type spells before admitting defeat?”

“What else could he have done? Stay buried underground forever?”

“Bai Ming was robbed! He didn’t even get to showcase his full strength before being restrained.”

A seasoned cultivator from the Demon Suppression Pass scoffed at their comments. “Robbed? Who cares about such things on the battlefield? You think enemies will foolishly wait for you to unleash every technique?”

The chastised person stammered, unable to retort.

“Old Teacher Kang, have you identified Lu Yang’s golden core yet?” A group of Golden Core cultivators in the front row of the audience was still waiting for the old scholar’s answer. Even if none of them had the talent to form a first-grade golden core in their lifetimes, broadening their horizons and witnessing it firsthand would at least give them some bragging rights.

Old Teacher Kang nearly yanked out his white beard from stroking it all this time, yet he still couldn’t decipher Lu Yang’s golden core. “With Bai Ming and Yan Tianzhi, there are at least clues, even if I can’t determine their exact golden cores. Bai Ming’s golden core is related to the Five Elements, while Yan Tianzhi’s is related to suppression. But for Lu Yang’s... forgive this old man’s failing eyes, I truly can’t discern anything.”

Old Teacher Kang shook his head. The diversity of golden cores in the Dao-Seeking Sect is so wildly varied that even if I have seen countless golden cores and possess the qualifications to appraise golden cores across Qing Province, I still can’t recognize them all in the Dao-Seeking Sect.

The Imperial Capital Academy had a consensus—anyone who could recognize even thirty to forty percent of the golden cores in the Dao-Seeking Sect would be considered a sage among scholars.

“Perhaps Lu Yang’s golden core is unprecedented.”

At this Golden Core Appreciation Convention, he could only roughly determine Lan Ting’s Genesis Golden Core and Meng Jingzhou’s Pure Yang Golden Core. To give Meng Jingzhou some prestige, he diplomatically renamed Meng Jingzhou’s Singel’s Golden Core to “Pure Yang Golden Core” to sound more dignified.

~~~

On the stage, Lan Ting was still locked in an arduous battle with Lu Yang’s lotus clone, unease gnawing at her heart.

Out of the corner of her eye, she had seen all of Bai Ming’s hair fall off after a single Arhat Fist strike. She was terrified that Lu Yang’s clone might chuck the Qingfeng Sword aside and unleash a round of Arhat Fist on her too.

Best to keep my distance.

Lan Ting pulled away from Lu Yang’s clone and pulled out a palm-sized box from her identity jade tablet.

“What’s this?” With his spiritual consciousness, Lu Yang’s clone detected stacks of talismans inside the box, along with an array at the bottom, one that he couldn’t help but find familiar.

Lan Ting didn’t keep him in suspense. “After returning to the immortal palace, I spent days and nights studying the Automatic Skewering Array. Unfortunately, my talent in arrays is limited and couldn’t yield any results. The bamboo skewers would keep launching at alarming speeds.

“Thus, I decided to change my line of thinking. If sticks can be fired with the array, why not talismans? With this idea, I modified the array, miniaturized it, and replaced the bamboo skewers with talismans.”

Lan Ting aimed the box at Lu Yang’s clone and activated the array. Talismans shot out in rapid succession, transforming into lightning, flames, and wind blades midair. Each was meticulously designed by Lan Ting, capable of severely injuring Golden Core cultivators.

Lu Yang’s eyelids twitched.

Boom!

Crack!

Smack!

Every talisman unleashed a unique attack, relentlessly crashing into Lu Yang’s clone with a discordance of different sounds. Smoke engulfed the arena as the talismans exploded.

Wielding the Qingfeng Sword before himself, his wrists flicked tirelessly to deflect the onslaught.

When the last talisman detonated, the smoke cleared, revealing a battered but intact Lu Yang.

“Impressive, Senior Brother Lu Yang. How about double firepower?” Lan Ting produced two more wooden boxes filled with talismans, aiming them both at Lu Yang’s clone.

Just as Lan Ting was about to launch another barrage of attacks, she saw Lu Yang’s main body walking toward her with a grin. “Bai Ming has already admitted defeat. You’re the only one left.”

“He lost?” Lan Ting was dumbfounded. She was too engrossed in firing her bombardment of talismans to notice what was happening on Bai Ming’s side. It’s only been a while, yet he has already lost?

She turned to see Bai Ming sulking at the judges’ platform.

She turned back and assessed Lu Yang and his clone, concluding that her odds of winning were dismal. “Forget it. I’ll admit defeat too.”

~~~

Meanwhile, Meng Jingzhou and Yan Tianzhi were still engaged in an intense battle. Yan Tianzhi resembled a real taotie that could devour all beings with incomparable ferociousness.

Chapter 365: I Wasn’t Fired Only Because of My High Cultivation

The oppressive pressure of Apex Fusion cultivators blanketed the entire grand event. Most attendees had never even encountered a Nascent Soul cultivator, let alone a pressure of such magnitude. Countless cultivators turned pale, their bodies swaying before collapsing to the ground with dull thuds.

“Lie prone on the ground! Maximize your contact area with the ground!” a cultivator from the authorities shouted, guiding the crowd to mitigate the damage.

Meng Jingzhou and the other three clutched their spirit treasures, neutralizing the effects of the oppressive aura. These were standard-issue spirit treasures for every immortal sect disciple—Meng Jingzhou’s pebble that was shaped like the Body Refinement Peak, Bai Ming’s five-colored disc, Lan Ting’s full moon embroidery, and Yan Tianzhi’s palm-sized prison cage—each reflecting the distinct traits of the Five Great Immortal Sects.

Whenever immortal sect disciples were outside, they represented their sects. If they were forced to kneel under an Apex Fusion cultivator’s oppressive pressure, it would be a slap to their sect’s faces.

Originally, Lu Yang should have possessed a pebble shaped like Heaven’s Gate Peak, but with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy with him, he didn’t fear this level of oppressive pressure at all. Even if a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator was here, they could only dream of making Lu Yang flinch with their oppressive pressure.

“What on earth is going on? Which Fusion cultivator is mad enough to attack here? Do they not want to live anymore?” Meng Jingzhou was flabbergasted.

Battles between Fusion cultivators were never allowed to endanger common folks, else the Great Xia Dynasty’s civilians would have been wiped out long ago. These battles could destroy heaven and earth and sink continents. Forget about civilians, even normal cultivators couldn’t withstand the fallout.

“They’re not modern Fusion cultivators but archaic ones!” This was what Lu Yang had learned from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. The aura waves emanated from two archaic Fusion cultivators, one male and one female, radiating with murderous intent.

Bai Ming frowned. “Everything makes sense now.” He pointed toward the origin of the oppressive aura. “There’s a secret domain in that direction; exploring the secret domain is a part of the event. Someone must have awakened those slumbering archaic cultivators and provoked their wrath to wreck everything.”

It wasn’t the first time something like this had happened. Archaic cultivators saw no need to obey modern laws. In their eras, Fusion cultivators wielded supreme dominion over others’ lives and deaths.

“Such audacity!” A thunderous roar echoed as the provincial governor arrived.

In the blink of an eye, the provincial governor appeared above the crowd, raising an official seal. A peculiar energy surged forth, dispersing the oppressive aura of the two Fusion cultivators.

“Hmm? What a peculiar power.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was surprised at this unfamiliar power.

Lu Yang and the others were also witnessing such power for the first time. Only Meng Jingzhou seemed to know something about it.

“This is the power of the nation’s fortune,” Meng Jingzhou explained. “I heard from my family that below the Great Xia Dynasty is a mystical force that forms its foundation. Every governor of provinces and large commanderies can temporarily mobilize this power for combat or protection. This is precisely how they have minimized damage from archaic Fusion cultivators all this time.”

“Interesting.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy analyzed the power of the national fortune with her immortal consciousness. This trickle of power the provincial governor had channeled was insignificant in her eyes, but if such power covered the entire Great Xia Dynasty, it would make for a terrifying force. That would be very interesting then. “It’s quite innovative. So there are pretty strong people aside from Lass Yun in this era.”

“What audacity! How dare you cause trouble under my watch?!” The provincial governor’s beard bristled like an enraged lion’s mane.

The two archaic Fusion cultivators were not afraid of the provincial governor and snorted coldly. “Fellow Daoist, you are flipping the blame on us? It was clearly your people who disturbed our slumber and forced us to awaken prematurely. How did we become the ones causing trouble?”

Chapter 366: Supreme Sword

High above in the sky, six Fusion experts clashed, their respective mighty abilities on full display. The cultivators below watched in awe, dazzled by the spectacle; even Lu Yang and his four companions stared unblinkingly. Battles between Fusion cultivators were a rare sight to witness.

Chapter 368: Boring

Watching the pleading masses below filled him with perverse delight. He reveled in this high and mighty feeling of controlling life and death.

Which faction does she belong to?

Crack!

“Die!”

Cough!

Chapter 369: Just How Many Fusion Cultivators Are Hiding in the Qing Province Grand Ceremony?

“Huff...huff...” The blood-robed figure panted heavily, his heart pounding so violently it seemed ready to burst from his chest. All traces of his former composure and arrogance were gone.

“Damn it! I’m down on my luck. I originally wanted to observe the might of the national fortune to make plans for the future, but I just had to run into a half-immortal expert! This era indeed shouldn’t be underestimated!

“Fortunately, I was meticulous and prepared for contingencies. Apart from the life-substitution jade, I have this spare corpse!

“I had deliberately self-detonated earlier to create enough confusion to catch that half-immortal expert off guard so I could flee!”

During the Great Yu era, people feared him as the “Calamity Venerable Lord.” His appearance signified bloodshed and catastrophes. Moreover, he was at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, with no one to keep him in check. This allowed him to act as he wished. I mean, who could punish me?

Originally, he planned to leverage the opportunity of his nation’s resurgence to advance his cultivation to the next level during this era. However, he didn’t expect to encounter a peerless expert capable of ending his life.

“Damn it! Since when has this venerable one been in such an embarrassing predicament?!”

The Calamity Venerable Lord cast a disdainful look at his tattered body, which was only at the Fusion Stage. Regret consumed him.

To deceive that half-immortal expert, I had staged an utterly convincing act during my self-detonation. Most of my soul was damaged, and my three ethereal souls and seven corporeal souls nearly scattered. I even purposely left behind some soul remnants on that self-detonated corpse.

The backup body—both the soul and flesh—he had prepared for his revival was only at the Fusion Stage. It was uncertain how many natural treasures would be required for him to return to his peak form.

Times are different compared to the Great Yu era. All kinds of natural treasures now have owners. I’ll need to employ all sorts of methods to acquire them, with the added risk of exposing my identity.

“It’s not the time to think about these challenges. The priority right now is to leave this place!”

He was still not truly out of danger. His resurrection method had distance limitations, and his revival point was in an inn room right at the foot of the mountain.

“With security tightened everywhere, flying out of here would be too conspicuous. Running out of here is safest.”

He walked out of the room and left the inn. Suddenly, his eyes lit up as he spotted a herd of steeds grazing on the grassland leisurely, seemingly unaffected by the oppressive pressure from the two archaic Fusion cultivators earlier.

The group of steeds had glossy coats, all of them mares. In the center was a white horse that appeared aged. Strangely, these mares, whether by chance or design, kept brushing against the old white horse in the middle, their eyes conveying unspoken affection.

The old white horse accepted all advances.

“A pure-blooded dragon horse!” The Calamity Venerable Lord’s eyes sparkled. I didn’t expect to stumble across one here! This legendary species only exists in the East Sea. He had long wanted to snatch one from the East Sea, but tales of the ancient Heaven Mandate Immortal hiding there had deterred him.

“The owner must have intentionally disguised this horse as an old horse. Demon beasts admire the strong, so these ordinary horses were instinctively drawn to the pure-blooded dragon horse. This is the advantage of bloodlines!”

“I can escape with this dragon horse. With its speed, I might recoup some of today’s losses!” After some quick calculations, the Calamity Venerable Lord concluded that this was the fastest way to flee. He released a wisp of oppressive aura, scaring the mares into scattering away.

The dragon horse’s pupils burned with ire, but the Calamity Venerable Lord thought nothing of it, laughing heartily. “Good dragon horse! I know you understand human speech. Follow this venerable one, and you won’t be mistreated!”

He strode toward the dragon horse. The dragon horse is a demon beast after all. It will follow me.

Bang! The dragon-horse kicked with its hind legs, dislocating both the Calamity Venerable Lord’s arms.

“A Fusion-level great demon king!” The Calamity Venerable Lord was aghast. How could there be another Fusion cultivator here? Why didn’t it intervene when those two Fusion cultivators were around just now?

To have tamed a great demon king as their mount...who could its master be?

“It’s that half-immortal expert’s mount!” This possibility immediately hit him. My attempt at making a move on this expert’s mount might imply that she has already discovered me.

Run!

The Calamity Venerable Lord still didn’t dare to fly. Boldly activating his power, he burrowed into the soil and crawled, not even daring to extend his spiritual consciousness for fear of being detected.

After running for a while, the half-immortal oppressive pressure that caused his heart to palpitate still hadn’t descended. He finally allowed himself to breathe a sigh of relief. “Looks like she didn’t discover me just now.”

He poked his head out of the ground. The surroundings were desolate, with only one person nearby sitting in meditation. Feeling reassured, he fully surfaced. “It should be safe enough here.”

Noticing the meditating person, greed grew within him. This place is already very far from the Qing Province Grand Ceremony. Even if a cultivator goes missing, suspicion wouldn’t be traced to me. Devouring a cultivator can more or less restore some of my power.

As he approached the cultivator, he heard the cultivator warn icily with closed eyes. “If I were you, I wouldn’t come close.”

The Calamity Venerable Lord sneered. Is this some intimidation tactic after sensing my malicious intent and realizing there’s no chance of escape?

Looks like the cultivators in this era are fond of bluffing too. What a pity—this is all child’s play that I’ve grown tired of!

“Is that so? I’d like to see what happens if I get close!” The Calamity Venerable Lord walked toward the cultivator step by step.

When Vice Creed Leader Shi opened his eyes and saw the Calamity Venerable Lord still approaching him, he shook his head lightly.

As the Calamity Venerable Lord had changed his body, Vice Creed Leader Qin didn’t recognize him. However, he wouldn’t stop anyone from seeking death.

Boom!

Thunder boomed and reverberated through the land, its deafening peals shaking the sky and turning people’s faces pale. The lightning was like a gigantic silver spear descending from the sky, connecting heaven and earth.

“What’s going on?! Where did this lightning tribulation come from?!” The Calamity Venerable Lord jumped in fright. Why did a lightning tribulation suddenly appear?

Worst of all, it has locked onto me!

“Damn it! It’s you!” He glowered at Vice Creed Leader Shi, realizing he had been dragged into the other party’s lightning tribulation and marked as an intruder.

“I already warned you not to come close.” Vice Creed Leader Qin’s tone was cold.

“It’s a mere lightning tribulation. What’s there to fear for this venerable one!” The Calamity Venerable Lord roared, his robes fluttering as he exerted his full strength.

“It’s you!” Vice Creed Leader Qin’s expression changed drastically. From the aura waves of the other party, Vice Creed Leader Qin could identify that the Calamity Venerable Lord was the culprit who ruined the Qing Province Grand Ceremony!

Vice Creed Leader Qin instinctively tensed, but when he sensed the other party’s weakened state and comparable cultivation, he was no longer afraid. “You were the one who ruined the Qing Province Grand Ceremony, and now my shop can’t continue operating!” he berated angrily.

“Huh?” The Calamity Venerable Lord froze for a moment, trying to process Vice Creed Leader Qin’s words. “You, a Fusion cultivator, running a shop at the Qing Province Grand Ceremony?”

His eyes bulged. Why is there yet another Fusion cultivator that has yet to act?

Just how many monsters lurk in that grand ceremony?!

“Enough talk! You're going through this lightning cultivation with me!” Vice Creed Leader Shi was in peak form, while his opponent was on the brink of collapse. Faced with this lightning cultivation, he’ll definitely end up more wretched than me!

Retribution! He deserves it!

When enemies meet, their eyes would burn with rancor. Vice Creed Leader Shi never expected that sneaking out to face a tribulation would land him face to face with his enemy.

If I don’t take revenge now, then when?! There’s no better time for revenge than now!

Boom!

The lightning tribulation descended. Endless bolts of lightning turned into electric plasma that carried scorching energy, submerging the two men.

Chapter 370: Hiding in a Prison Cell Should Be Safe

After the lightning tribulation, the Calamity Venerable Lord lay nearly lifeless, his body charred and hardly any different from a corpse. “Damn it, you’re just at the Fusion Stage! Why would you attract such a powerful lightning tribulation?!”

Vice Creed Leader Shi remained silent. The lightning tribulation was worth one billion spirit stones; of course, it’d be powerful.

Having endured a lightning tribulation once, Vice Creed Leader Shi was fully prepared this time. His scorched skin cracked like a ceramic statue, revealing fresh skin beneath as he tore away the outer layer.

“Entry-level Cicada Molting Spell?” The Calamity Venerable Lord recognized the method.

Vice Creed Leader cast a glance at him wordlessly and swallowed a pill, eliciting the envious gaze of the Calamity Venerable Lord.

The Entry-Level Cicada Molting Spell could only keep him clean. He still needed pills to replenish his depleted energy from the lightning tribulation.

The Calamity Venerable Lord was tempted to snatch the pills, but his wretched state barely allowed him to move, let alone steal the pills.

As Vice Creed Leader Shi refined the medicinal properties of the pills, he sneered at the Calamity Venerable Lord. “It wasn’t easy for me to turn over a new leaf and start an honest business, yet you bunch of archaic cultivators ruined everything! Serves you right to have fallen into my hands!” Abandoning all techniques and rules, he resorted to pure punches and kicks to vent his fury on the Calamity Venerable Lord.

“You damned bastard! How dare you cut off my path to fortune?!

“Did you really think modern cultivators are easy to bully?!

“If I don’t beat you until your mom can’t recognize you, I’ll renounce my family name!”

The Calamity Venerable Lord was beaten until he had a bloody nose and swollen face, and not a single bone was intact, with special care received in his nether regions.

Vice Creed Leader Shi flicked his right hand and produced iron chains as thick as one’s arms, trussing up the Calamity Venerable Lord like a pig before carrying him off.

“N-no! I can’t let him take me!” The Calamity Venerable Lord could tell that Vice Creed Leader Shi was a ruthless person. There’s no way I’ll survive if I go with him!

I must run!

Biting his tongue, he spat a mouthful of essence blood and transformed into smoke. Slipping through the chains, he ripped apart space and vanished.

“He burned his lifespan!” Vice Creed Leader Shi’s eyes narrowed, not expecting the Calamity Venerable Lord to be this ruthless. My iron chains can restrain the body and soul. Based on his condition, he wouldn’t have been able to escape without burning at least several millennia of his lifespan.

“Truly ruthless! With this much burned, how many years would you have left?” Vice Creed Leader Shi couldn’t do anything about his enemy’s methods. “Whatever. Since he has escaped, so be it. I’ll just take revenge on other archaic cultivators.”

~~~

The Calamity Venerable Lord was still fleeing. Through this debacle, he realized it would be tough for him to obtain any advantage in the upcoming Battle of the Great Era.

“Something went wrong with my line of thought! It was only because I wanted to hide in a desolate place earlier that I encountered that lunatic’s lightning tribulation. This time, I’ll hide in a city!” He changed his approach and headed for the nearest city.

“Dayan Commandery—good name! ‘The dayan wild geese fly south, and one rises again from the mountains.’ It does fit my situation!”

To be safe, he cautiously scanned Dayan Commandery with his spiritual consciousness. “It looks like a prosperous city, and the commandery governor is only at the Divine Transfiguration Stage. Ideal for hiding!” The Calamity Venerable Lord smiled.

Heaven is helping me!

Having burned his lifespan, his cultivation realm had fallen to the Basic Fusion Stage, barely retaining his Fusion cultivation. Due to the unique nature of the Void Refinement Stage, he could have fallen from the Fusion to the Divine Transfiguration Stage.

“Fortune has always been on my side!”

Sneaking into Dayan Commandery, he contemplated the optimal hiding spot for him to return to his cultivation realm. “I can recover my cultivation by devouring other people’s vitality. It’s best to have no disruption during the process. I should find somewhere lifeless!”

A brilliant idea struck the Calamity Venerable Lord.

“I’ll go to the prison!”

Prisoners have no human rights. Nobody would notice even if something happened.

He transformed into smoke and slipped into the prison.

As soon as he slipped in, he heard two people arguing.

“I’ve told you, that’s not how this law works! Is there a problem with your brain?”

“Nonsense! I was the one who formulated this law. How could I not know how to apply it?”

“Just because you formulated it, you think you understand it? I raised Yun Zhi, but I don’t even know how strong she is now!”

“Dogshit logic!”

“You’re the one with dogshit logic!”

As the Taciturn Daoist Priest bickered with the Minister of Justice, the usually refined and easygoing Minister of Justice became increasingly irascible.

“Wait a moment.” The Taciturn Daoist Priest raised his hand, sensing something amiss.

“Who’s there?!”

“What a heavy stench of blood!” The Minister of Justice, Xu Xin, was taken aback. He had prosecuted numerous fiendish criminals, but none of them could compare to the Calamity Venerable Lord’s fetor of blood.

Diabolic cultivators had secret spells to hide their bloody aura out of fear for the righteous path, but the Calamity Venerable Lord bore no such concept. During the Great Yu era, one’s level of bloody aura was irrelevant, sometimes even a symbol of honor.

“Hehe, to think you could detect this venerable one! You two juniors do have some skills. In that case, you shall become my nutrients!” The Calamity Venerable Lord assumed he had leaked his aura out of carelessness. But that’s just a trivial matter. I naturally have my way to control these two people!

Even if I couldn’t deal with others, surely I can handle two criminals?

A sinister and frightening light suddenly flashed, and wicked energy swirled in the narrow space, creating a black hole-like suction force accompanied by silent screams that seemed to have come from the abyss.

“Become my slaves!”

The Minister of Justice struck out violently, and an intangible golden hand slapped the dense smoke apart, sending the Calamity Venerable Lord tumbling to the ground.

The eerie light, malignant energy, and silent screams disappeared.

“Who do you think you are? How dare you play such tricks before this official?”

The Calamity Venerable Lord was sprawled on the ground, yet to regain his senses. How did I fall?

“Diabolic cultivator! Seize him!” The Taciturn Daoist Priest attacked. His sword heart pulsed as tens of thousands of sword qi circulated in a grand, unceasing display, filling the entire space.

It was impossible for the Calamity Venerable Lord to tear open space and escape even if he wanted to!

As someone who frequently escaped, the Taciturn Daoist Priest naturally knew how to deal with others who frequently escaped. Only Yun Zhi can lock me up. Anyone else won’t have the same confidence.

The Calamity Venerable Lord, “...”

He remained speechless for a long time, unsure of what expression he should even show to convey his feelings.

What’s going on? Why are there such powerful people imprisoned here? They’re even stronger than that lunatic who endured the lightning tribulation earlier!

The prison cells have no restrictions either. Why are the two of you locked up here? Because the prison is warm in winter and cool in summer? freeωebnovēl.c૦m

“Who is this?” Xu Xin had never seen someone this eager to court death.

“Who knows? But I bet he’s a bad egg. Maybe he’s some archaic cultivator rube who got beaten and fled to the prison to recuperate from his injuries. Let’s capture him first. It will count as a great meritorious service, and we might get a reduced sentence!” The Taciturn Daoist Priest exclaimed in delight. We were just sitting in prison when this opportunity fell from the sky and into our laps.

Xu Xin was also delighted upon hearing the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s words.

Yun Zhi had been tailing the Calamity Venerable Lord this whole time. Watching this scene unfold, she sighed slightly, realizing her hopes of following him back to his lair were dashed.

It couldn’t be helped. The Calamity Venerable Lord was simply too unlucky. First, he encountered the old horse and got kicked by its hind legs. Then, he got caught in Vice Creed Leader Shi’s lightning tribulation. After that, he crashed the prison cell housing the Taciturn Daoist Priest and Xu Xin in Dayan Commandery and was apprehended. It was truly miraculous for him to have survived this series of unfortunate events.

Yun Zhi had never met someone with such bad luck.

Best to take him back for interrogation and torture.

She materialized in the cell. “Shifu, Lord Minister, it’s been a long time.”

Chapter 371: Kind-Hearted Cultivator Vice Creed Leader Shi

The Taciturn Daoist Priest and Minister of Justice were scrutinizing the Calamity Venerable Lord when they heard an ethereal and familiar voice, making them both shudder.

“Shifu, Lord Minister, it’s been a long time.”

“It’s you!” Seeing the figure who had reduced him to this plight, the Calamity Venerable Lord shrieked in terror and crawled forward desperately.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest and Xu Xin cast sidelong glances at the Calamity Venerable Lord. Why did this old fellow react more intensely than we did?

Being shrewd individuals, the two immediately deduced the reason. This man has been fleeing Yun Zhi’s pursuit and hoped to conceal himself with the prison’s gloomy atmosphere, only to be captured by us.

“If I’m not mistaken, this is the Calamity Venerable Lord from the mid-Great Yu era. He took advantage of the Qing Province Grand Ceremony to order two archaic Fusion cultivators to go on a rampage, forcing the provincial governor to mobilize the national fortune and Supreme Sword Projection for battle, thereby achieving his goal of gathering intelligence.

“Fortunately, Little Junior Brother was astute and detected the anomalies with those two archaic Fusion cultivators and alerted me in time. That was how I managed to capture him. Had he relayed the intelligence about the national fortune and Supreme Sword Projection to other archaic cultivators, it would have caused significant trouble.”

Xu Xin gnashed his teeth at the Calamity Venerable Lord. “I knew it was strange! Why would an unfamiliar Fusion cultivator pop up from nowhere? So it’s because it’s yet another archaic Fusion cultivator!”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest dropped his lighthearted demeanor. Archaic cultivators were one of Great Xia’s crises.

Yun Zhi narrowed her eyes. This was her second time capturing an archaic Transcendent Tribulation cultivator. Previously, she had reached a consensus with the other four leaders of the Five Great Immortal Sects and the Xia Emperor that archaic cultivators would awaken in succession as time passed. Since the cultivators awakening now were at the Fusion Stage, those awakening next would be at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage.

But based on this archaic Transcendent Tribulation cultivator’s behavior, he seems to have learned about the national fortune and Supreme Sword Projection long ago, which suggests that he had probably awakened early on.

“Looks like many archaic cultivators are hiding in places unknown to us.” Yun Zhi’s cold tone carried a trace of displeasure. This mediocre and dull-witted bunch even calculates the timing of immortal ascension and schemes various things, bringing disasters to the world.

The Calamity Venerable Lord’s body resembled a withered tree, his breathing barely perceptible as if he could die any moment. Seeing his current state, Yun Zhi yanked his soul out with a tap of her forefinger.

Bringing only the soul back will be much more convenient. Rather than a body on the verge of crumbling, I might as well just take the soul.

Yun Zhi gripped an invisible chain in her right hand, with the other end tied around the Calamity Venerable Lord.

“By the way, Shifu, Your Excellency, capturing the Calamity Venerable Lord counts as a meritorious service. I’ll inform the Xia Emperor about this matter,” Yun Zhi suddenly added before departing.

After the initial daze, the two rejoiced. Such a great contribution is enough to secure our release.

They had thought they would miss this opportunity.

~~~

“Where to find archaic cultivators for revenge?” Vice Creed Leader Shi pondered. He was never one to delay his revenge.

“Fellow Daoist, you are of noble character and high integrity to specially seek out archaic cultivators! I, Sun, greatly admire your virtue!” A hearty laugh laced with delight rang out.

Vice Creed Leader Shi found the voice familiar. Turning around, his eyelids twitched.

It’s the provincial governor.

The provincial governor cupped his hands at Vice Creed Leader Shi with a sincere attitude. “Fellow Daoist, may I know where you are from and what your name is? Leveraging the lightning tribulation to injure the Calamity Venerable Lord gravely is truly a great meritorious deed. Could I invite you to follow me back to my estate, Fellow Daoist? There will certainly be generous rewards. Afterward, I’ll also report this to the court to confer an award!”

Similar to Yun Zhi, the provincial governor had tailed the Calamity Heavenly Lord, though he was slower than Yun Zhi and missed the full sequence of events.

By the time the provincial governor arrived, he saw Vice Creed Leader Shi drag the Calamity Venerable Lord into the lightning tribulation, thwarting his numerous escape attempts. Vice Creed Leader Shi even gloated, clearly holding a grudge with the Calamity Venerable Lord. After the lightning tribulation, Vice Creed Leader Shi trussed him up to prevent him from fleeing.

The provincial governor added his embellishments to conjure a scene of what had happened.

A reclusive rogue cultivator was undergoing lightning tribulation in a desolate area. Sensing the Calamity Venerable Lord’s strong stench of blood and malevolent aura, he made use of the lightning tribulation to detain him forcibly.

What a kind-hearted individual! The provincial governor was deeply moved and insisted on rewarding Vice Creed Leader Shi.

Vice Creed Leader Shi shook his head repeatedly. How would I dare to go with the provincial governor? What if he discovers my identity? Wouldn’t that mean a promotion for him?

That’s what the bounty stated.

“You’re too polite, Your Excellency. I simply couldn’t tolerate this bunch of lawless archaic cultivators’ atrocities and decided to punish them. As for the rewards, how can one expect rewards for righteous and chivalric acts? Wouldn’t that be putting the cart before the horse? Goodbye!”

He left hastily, denying the provincial governor any chance to persuade him otherwise.

As the provincial governor watched Vice Creed Leader Shi vanish, he lamented from the bottom of his heart, “Truly a virtuous cultivator who’s in isolation.”

~~~

At the Qing Province Grand Ceremony, the two archaic cultivators had been captured and had their cultivation sealed, with several Fusion cultivators taking turns to keep watch on them. The court would soon dispatch the Luoshui Guard to take the two away, sever their meridians, and throw them in the imperial prison.

The officials maintained order according to their roles. With the provincial governor absent, Xia Qun held the highest position. He assumed command of the yamen and coordinated the recovery efforts.

It should be noted that “recovery” referred more to the mental impact rather than material loss.

Archaic Fusion cultivators, national fortune, Supreme Sword Projection, an archaic Transcendent Tribulation cultivator, a mysterious expert who could effortlessly suppress a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator...all of this was beyond the reach of ordinary cultivators.

Forget about ordinary cultivators; even Lan Ting and the others were still in a daze.

Lu Yang remained unfazed. What are archaic Transcendent Tribulation cultivators? Inside my mental space is the number one ancient immortal who was the first among the top ten ancient beauties and casually shares ancient secrets at every turn. When immortals are involved, there’s no place at all for Transcendent Tribulation cultivators.

He overheard bystanders discussing the events from earlier.

“Thankfully, that expert stepped in. Otherwise, we would have been in danger!” A Golden Core cultivator was glad to have narrowly avoided death. I feel so lucky to be alive right now.

His companion agreed. Fear had yet to fade from his eyes. “You don’t say! Speaking of which, what did that expert look like again?”

”You forgot our savior’s appearance... Right, what did that expert look like? Were they male or female?”

The two stared at each other in bafflement.

On the other side, bystanders were also talking about the earlier battle.

“The provincial governor was amazing! He withstood a Transcendent Tribulation-tier magical treasure alone!”

“That’s nothing! He nearly slew that archaic Transcendent Tribulation cultivator! Especially that heaven-defying sword!”

“Sword? What sword?”

“Is this how you use your brain? It was made of... what was the sword made of again?”

“Speaking of which, what weapon did His Excellency use to defeat the archaic Fusion cultivators?”

Their heads were filled with question marks, and they soon forgot everything that had happened.

Lu Yang frowned at the scene. The national fortune, Supreme Sword Projection, and Big Senior Sister... I remember every detail.

“Immortal Fairy, what’s going on here?”

Chapter 372: Special Trait of Immortals

“So, you’ve come to seek this immortal’s wisdom again?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was more than happy to answer Lu Yang’s questions. “You should first ask the young fellows from the other immortal sects how much they still remember.” She was not in a hurry, guiding Lu Yang to uncover the truth himself.

“Lan Ting, do you remember the battle earlier?”

Lan Ting rolled her eyes at Lu Yang, finding the question silly. “Of course, I remember. Didn’t Senior Sister Yun Zhi display her divine mighty abilities and suppress that Transcendent Tribulation cultivator?”

“And before that?”

“You mean the battle between the provincial governor and the archaic Fusion cultivators? Didn’t the provincial governor use...” Lan Ting suddenly faltered. The answer seemed to linger on the tip of her tongue, yet she couldn’t recall it no matter how hard she tried.

What had the provincial governor used again?

Lu Yang didn’t press further. It was the same with Lan Ting—she had forgotten about the national fortune and Supreme Sword Projection.

He turned to Yan Tianzhi. “Do you remember Big Senior Sister?”

“Yun Zhi. Senior Sister. Remember.”

“What about the combat method the provincial governor used?”

Yan Tianzhi blinked and answered candidly, “Forgot.”

“Old Meng, what about you? Is your mind still clear?”

“My ass! When has my mind ever been unclear? Didn’t the provincial governor use the national fortune to manifest the Supreme Sword Projection and wage war with the archaic Fusion cultivators, and then Big Senior Sister suppressed the archaic Transcendent Tribulation cultivator?”

Lu Yang ruminated. Ordinary cultivators had forgotten about the national fortune and Big Senior Sister, while Lan Ting and the other two had only forgotten about the national fortune. Only Meng Jingzhou and I remembered the entire battle.

“Does the key lie in the national fortune? It erased everyone’s memories, but Meng Jingzhou is from the Meng Family, which once vied for the throne and had multiple intermarriages with the imperial family. In other words, Old Meng has the bloodline of both the Meng Family and the imperial family. Is that why he could remember the national fortune?

“But what about Big Senior Sister? Did she not want to draw attention from the public and erased nearly everyone’s memories except for the five of us?” Lu Yang felt he had figured out the answer and sought the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s confirmation.

“Something like that. The national fortune erased everyone’s memories, but it wasn’t that Yun Zhi didn’t erase yours—she deliberately preserved them. Do you understand the difference?”

Lu Yang lowered his head in contemplation and jolted in realization. “The memory erasure by Big Senior Sister and the national fortune happened automatically!”

“Correct. This is a special characteristic of immortals, which automatically makes people forget an immortal’s methods unless the immortal deliberately lets them remember.”

“The national fortune and Lass Yun’s actions all count as ‘immortal methods.’

“The provincial governor oversees this region, so he won’t forget about the national fortune. That Xia Qun is of imperial bloodline, so he won’t forget either. Same goes for little fellow Meng.”

Lu Yang suddenly discovered another problem. “Wait, if you’re talking about immortal methods, does that include Dao Fruits?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was pleased with Lu Yang’s swift internalization. “You have a sharp mind. Dao Fruits are the primary characteristic of immortals, so of course, they count as immortal methods.

“It’s just like the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s Tribulation Mandate Dao Fruit and Epoch Immortal’s Epoch Dao Fruit—they’re all classic immortal methods. Take a look at the Epoch Immortal. Even though he has named himself after his ability, people still can’t remember the Epoch Dao Fruit and that his methods are related to time.”

This was one of the reasons immortals were so enigmatic.

“Then how am I able to remember all this?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy puffed up proudly. “What kind of question is that? You have this immortal looking after you. How could you forget?

“You’re the second-in-command of the Everlasting Lineage. If word gets out that you know nothing about other immortals, it’d bring disgrace to our Everlasting Lineage!”

Only then did Lu Yang realize how precious such knowledge was.

“Of course, not all immortals possess this trait of making people forget immortal methods. This immortal is an exception. Otherwise, there would have been no Everlasting Creed!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy held up two fingers. “Based on this trait, immortals can be divided into two categories. One type includes those who can automatically make people forget immortal methods.

“And the other is this immortal, who bears no such trait!

“These are two paths and two different choices.”

Lu Yang was silent for a long time before slowly raising his hands to cup his fists solemnly. “Immortal Fairy, you’re truly impressive!”

His serious attitude flustered the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. Her cheeks flushed, and she fidgeted, unsure where to put her hands. Crossing her arms, she tilted her chin up slightly with a pout. “Aiya, I have always said I’m impressive. You just didn’t believe me.”

After she finished speaking, she cracked an eye open to peek at Lu Yang’s reaction.

Seeing him still so earnest, she grew even more flustered.

“I’m going to sleep! Shoo shoo shoo! Don’t disturb my sleep!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy booted Lu Yang out of his mental space.

~~~

Though the Calamity Venerable Lord seemed to have escaped for a long time, it had actually been brief. After waiting in place for a short while, Lu Yang and the other four saw Yun Zhi dragging the Calamity Venerable Lord’s soul back to the Qing Province Grand Ceremony.

“Big Senior Sister, you’re back already?” Lu Yang was shocked. Hadn’t we agreed to track the Calamity Venerable Lord to his lair? This is absurdly fast.

Yun Zhi, “...”

“Change of plans.” She didn’t elaborate. How am I supposed to explain? Do I say that the Calamity Venerable Lord didn’t pick an auspicious day to flee, running headlong into four Fusion cultivators and incidentally helping Shifu and the Minister of Justice reduce their sentences?

“Se-Senior Sister Yun Zhi, “Lan Ting greeted timidly, not daring to meet her gaze. Yun Zhi’s display of divine might in the sky above had been downright terrifying. Anyone would have been intimidated.

Yun Zhi glanced at Lan Ting and nodded slightly. “I remember you. Your shifu brought you to propose marriage to Lu Yang. After I agreed, she went back on it and ran off with you.”

Lan Ting fell silent for a long while, utterly failing to connect Yun Zhi’s words to that past experience.

“Senior Sister Yun Zhi.”

“Senior Sister.”

Bai Ming and Yan Tianzhi greeted ner nervously, more so than they ever had been before their respective sects’ ancestors.

“The provincial governor informed me that this year’s Qing Province Grand Ceremony has concluded. You’re free to arrange your own travels,” Yun Zhi reminded them kindly. She tugged the chain in her hand. “I still need to interrogate this one, so I’ll return to the sect first.”

Just as she was about to leave, she spotted Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou and seemed to have thought of something, turning back to Lan Ting. “By the way, how did my Little Junior Brother and Junior Brother Meng perform at the grand ceremony’s tournament? Did they accurately critique the contestants’ strengths and weaknesses?”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou stiffened, cold sweat breaking out. So Big Senior Sister had really sent us here as judges, not contestants.

After a brief pause, Lan Ting smiled sweetly. “Senior Brother Lu Yang and Senior Brother Meng Jingzhou are role models for our younger generation. They are exceptionally talented and possess a wealth of combat experience. Their commentaries were incisive and spot-on, with every word full of wisdom. The participants were deeply convinced and vowed to work hard on their cultivation upon returning.”

Yun Zhi nodded. “That’s good then. I was worried they might have joined the competition. It’s a relief they didn’t.”

Hearing Yun Zhi's words, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was suddenly wide awake. She shot up from bed, ready to expose Lu Yang, only for him to clamp his hand firmly over her mouth.

Chapter 373: Great Yu’s Imperial Preceptors

Upon hearing Lan Ting’s defense on their behalf, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were deeply moved. This favor is no less than second parents who have granted us another life.

In stark contrast, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy wore an expression of someone eagerly anticipating chaos. Fortunately, Lu Yang reacted with lightning reflexes and clamped his hand firmly over her mouth. Otherwise, his survival today would be up in the air.

“Let’s go. We’re returning together.” With these words, Yun Zhi flew to the foot of the mountain.

Noticing that, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou bid goodbye to Lan Ting and the others before hurriedly catching up with Yun Zhi.

“We’ll take our leave first!”

“Until we meet again.”

“Come visit Moon Laurel Immortal Palace when you have time.”

With the grand ceremony concluded, the five had to exchange goodbyes as they each had their own affairs to attend to.

When Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou reached the mountain’s base, Yun Zhi lifted the carriage curtain. “Get on.”

Meng Jingzhou stared at the old horse with a peculiar expression. Normally, the old horse’s coat lacked luster, and its eyelids drooped, resembling a picture of an elderly person counting each day alive as a blessing.

Yun Zhi tugged the soul chain in her grip, its other end extending beyond the carriage where the Calamity Venerable Lord floated outside comically like a balloon.

Witnessing the old horse withdraw its haughtiness as a great demon king and willingly pull Yun Zhi’s carriage, the Calamity Venerable Lord became convinced of his speculation.

This dragon horse great demon king must be the mount of a half-immortal!

“Don’t grow arrogant! His Excellency the Imperial Preceptor will definitely restore Great Yu!” The Calamity Venerable Lord roared with savage laughter.

Yun Zhi frowned at the grating laughter and casually sealed his five senses with a sigil, rendering him mute and insensate to the external world.

“Imperial Preceptor? The Great Yu’s imperial preceptor is the mastermind behind this?” Inside the carriage, Lu Yang rummaged through intelligence about the Great Yu’s imperial preceptor in his mind.

“What’s an imperial preceptor?” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy inquired. She hadn’t even fully grasped the knowledge of the modern era, much less the now-defunct system with an imperial preceptor.

“The imperial preceptor was part of a system unique to the Great Yu Dynasty. If you treat the Great Yu Dynasty as a sect, the imperial preceptor is a protector who ensures the longevity of the sect.

“This system can be traced back two hundred thousand years, when the Great Yu Dynasty was founded. It was said that the first imperial preceptor was the teacher of the founding Yu Emperor, who established the dynasty with his aid.

“To have overthrown the rule of the previous dynasty and unified the Central Continent, the first Yu emperor must have been a formidable and ambitious hero. Unfortunately, his children were disappointing, lacking cultivation talent and the vision to govern the nation.

“At that time, the founding emperor thought of his teacher and set up the position of imperial preceptor, inviting his teacher to assume the role, thus beginning the lineage of imperial preceptors.

“Based on historical records, this system of imperial preceptors did make meritorious contributions after the founding Yu Emperor’s passing. The prosperity of the early Great Yu Dynasty stemmed largely from the imperial preceptors’ tutelage of emperors and quality governance.

“However, this created another problem. The imperial preceptors became de facto rulers of the Great Yu Dynasty. “Moreover, while the first imperial preceptor selflessly served the Great Yu Dynasty, could such altruism be the same for subsequent imperial preceptors, or were they driven by personal ambition?

Assassinations, schemes, honey traps, succession wars...all unfolded one after another, with no one knowing what hidden cards their opponents held.

“110,000 years ago, at the ‘Summit of Pingding Mountain,’ tensions erupted into open warfare between the factions of the Imperial Preceptor and the Yu Emperor. At least eight Transcendent Tribulation cultivators participated in the battle, and it was unknown how many more acted from the shadows.

“Both sides suffered devastating losses. With their top-tier combat powerhouses gone, the Great Yu Dynasty’s authority plummeted. Long-repressed conflicts resurged, and the dynasty entered its final days.

My research later revealed that during the waning years of the Great Yu Dynasty, the Blood Devil Venerable Lord had supported a Yu emperor, while he himself assumed the position of imperial preceptor. After that, he chose to hibernate for the Battle of the Great Era, only to be captured by Big Senior Sister upon awakening.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy replied insipidly, “Oh. That’s not high. Does Great Xia have imperial preceptors? I can reluctantly take on the role.”

Peeking his head out, he realized they were already at the entrance to their mountain peak back at the sect.

How much time has passed? Has it even been an hour?

Meng Jingzhou shot unfriendly stares at the old horse. Our journey to Qing Province had taken days, yet with Big Senior Sister around, we returned in less than an hour?

Aren’t you going overboard with sandbagging and concealing your shortcomings?!

“I’m going to Incarceration Peak to see if I can extract any information. The two of you may do as you please.” With the Calamity Venerable Lord in tow, Yun Zhi flew toward Incarceration Peak.

Chapter 374: Envious Li Haoran

Incarceration Peak served as the Dao-Seeking Sect’s dedicated penitentiary, housing primarily wicked archaic cultivators.

Beneath Incarceration Peak, each cage contained an archaic Fusion cultivator who commanded the wind and clouds in the past. Now, they were reduced to prisoners, milked for every last shred of their worth.

The imperial court and four other immortal sects maintained similar facilities to restrain these archaic cultivators from doing evil.

Within the cages, listless souls slumped against walls, their gazes hollow. Sensing someone coming, their eyes ignited with malicious glints, hoping to intimidate the visitor. This was their only form of entertainment here.

However, upon recognizing Yun Zhi, their complexions blanched. They scrambled to the corners and suppressed their auras while trembling, desperately minimizing their presence lest they attract her attention.

Numerous vacant cages in Incarceration Peak bore inscriptions at their upper-right corners: Wilderness-Breaking True Lord, Mount Tai True Lord, Mystic Spirit Mad Devil, Stillness-Returning True Person... In the past eras, these names alone could drain color from people’s faces and cause them to shake like sieves.

But nowadays, Yun Zhi had fused them into magical artifacts to be refined as artifact spirits. Should they make her upset, they would be the unlucky ones next in line.

When Yun Zhi removed the Calamity Venerable Lord’s seal, he swept his gaze across his surroundings, instantly realizing the place was specially designed to incarcerate them.

He was slightly startled. No wonder some individuals who should have awakened remain unreachable despite my attempts to contact them. So it’s because they have been locked up here all along.

This Great Xia proves more intractable than I had imagined...

Suddenly, he noticed an adjacent cell, its top-right corner labeled “Blood Devil Venerable Lord.”

Having seen portraits of the Calamity Venerable Lord, the Blood Devil Venerable Lord recognized this senior of his who predated him by several thousand years.

The Calamity Venerable Lord roared. “Blood Devil! You luck-begotten trash! How is a mere Basic Transcendent Tribulation Stage qualified to lay claim to the imperial preceptor position?!”

Despite both of us being at the Basic Transcendent Tribulation Stage, I was the imperial preceptor’s subordinate, while Blood Devil could become the imperial preceptor. The disparity is too big.

After awakening from his slumber, he learned of Great Yu’s history and the Blood Devil Venerable Lord’s existence.

The Blood Devil Venerable Lord supported a trash to become the Yu emperor out of his selfish motives and manipulated the emperor to plunder countless benefits. To pander to the influential ancestral clans back then, he enacted measures to strengthen them, accelerating the Great Yu’s destruction.

When Great Yu collapsed and the world was in turmoil, those same ancestral clans vied for dominion, and the Blood Devil Venerable Lord was the root of it all.

I refuse to acknowledge such trash as an imperial preceptor!

The Blood Devil Venerable Lord was not afraid of him, smirking through his tirade. “Senior Calamity, your words were too harsh. With the position of imperial preceptor available, even if I hadn’t taken the role, someone else would have. How could you call this luck?”

“If the Imperial Preceptor were to know you’re here, he would definitely kill you!”

“I'll wait and see then.”

“Lass Yun, another captive?” A childlike voice echoed as a white-haired child materialized, scrutinizing the Calamity Venerable Lord.

The Calamity Venerable Lord started. He hadn’t detected how the other party had appeared.

“A fragmented soul burning lifespan—quite ruthless toward himself, huh? He was formerly at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage?”

“Yes. Calamity Venerable Lord, a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator from the early Great Yu era,” Yun Zhi replied.

The white-haired child chuckled in recognition. “Ah, it’s him. His reputation precedes him.

“You have captured two Transcendent Tribulation Stages within half a year. It looks like some people are growing impatient.”

Yun Zhi displayed a rare hesitation, embarrassed to voice the truth.

I have never apprehended Transcendent Tribulation cultivators in the past, yet I’ve suddenly caught two within half a year. I don’t think it’s because some people are growing impatient, but rather an issue with luck.

The first time, the lead came from Buyi Town, and the second time, Lu Yang had bumped into it directly.

The only constant between the two events was the presence of Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

Considering that Lu Yang had resurrected the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, it’s hard to say whether forces in the shadows are growing impatient or Lu Yang is simply fated with high-level cultivators.

“Grand-Shifu, I’ll use some methods on him first.”

“Go on. Hope it’ll yield fruitful results this time.” The white-haired child tittered, filled with satisfaction for this talented junior.

The Blood Devil Venerable Lord’s period of activity was too late in the era, rendering him mostly useless for intelligence. But it was different for the Calamity Venerable Lord. He was a cultivator from the early Great Yu era, active during the second imperial preceptor’s reign—he was bound to be privy to many matters.

Replaced by the Calamity Venerable Lord’s blood-curdling shrieks.

It’s a pity I had to help Qin Yanyan form her golden core and couldn’t go.
