Chapter 375: Tao Yaoye’s New Script

When Lu Yang arrived at the summit of Hundred Refinements Peak, half of the Dao-Seeking Sect’s elders were gathered there: Second Elder, Fifth Elder, and Sixth Elder—present only as a projection.

Fifth Elder eyed Second Elder and Eighth Elder. These two eccentric monsters. “Since when do the two of you invent new things? And you even want me to apply for a patent?”

In his memory, Second Bro has entered retiree life in advance, spending his days guarding the herb garden. If not for his glowing spirits from a second spring—another chance at his love life, I would have thought Second Bro has turned moldy.

And there’s Old Eight. He’s been holed up in the sect lately. He’s probably seeking refuge in the sect due to some trouble he stirred up outside.

“It’s not the two of them; Tao Yaoye came up with the idea. Old Two and Old Eight are responsible for bringing it to fruition,” Sixth Elder explained.

Fifth Elder nodded. This makes far more sense.

“Junior Niece Tao, what have you invented?” Fifth Elder’s attitude was amiable. He always encouraged his disciples to think outside the box and push the boundaries of conventional wisdom.

In this regard, I hold high hopes for Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou. Li Haoran’s creativity is slightly lacking, so he’ll need to keep up with his efforts.

“It’s a combination of arrays and talismans that allows people to enter illusory domains—” Tao Yaoye paused mid-explanation when she noticed Lu Yang strolling toward them. “Senior Brother Lu, what brings you here?”

Seeing the lively gathering, Lu Yang could roughly guess what they were up to, so he smiled and asked, “Junior Sister Tao, is the construction of the illusory domain complete?”

“Thanks to the help from Second Elder and Eighth Elder, we’ve finished the preliminary version. I was just about to demonstrate it to Fifth Elder. Would you like to try it too, Senior Brother?”

Lu Yang agreed readily. He was curious to see how Tao Yaoye’s “film production” had turned out.

Tao Yaoye retrieved two talismans from her identity jade tablet and handed one each to Fifth Elder and Lu Yang. Then, she unfurled a scroll drawn with an array that Lu Yang couldn’t decipher.

“Is this a talisman designed by Old Eight? And an array drawn by Old Two?” Fifth Elder recognized the origins of the talisman and array, both of whose designs were relatively simple.

“Fifth Elder, Senior Brother, please stand on the array and tear the talisman in half from the middle. After that, you will feel a slight tug, a sign that you’re entering the illusion.” This was an illusory domain designed for mortals and low-level cultivators. Tao Yaoye was worried that if either of them resisted even slightly, the talisman would be nullified.

Lu Yang followed her instructions and split the talisman cleanly. A faint pull tugged at his consciousness, which he did not resist. With that, his consciousness was dragged into another world.

Boom!

The moment he arrived, Lu Yang could see endless streaks of lightning in the sky and hear peals of deafening thunder, as if no other sounds existed in this world.

Amidst the lightning, a peerless figure stood unwavering in the sky, enduring the lightning strikes dauntlessly. freēnovelkiss.com

“This person is about to break through to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage. It’s quite convincing,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy whispered in Lu Yang’s ear, startling him.

Lu Yang sneaked a glance at Fifth Elder, who had entered the illusory domain with him before answering softly, “Immortal Fairy, what are you doing here? What if someone discovers you?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy flashed a smug smile. “A simple illusory domain like this can’t keep me out; I can come and go as I please. As for getting discovered? My concealment skills are unmatched in this world. No one can find me!”

Lu Yang exhaled in relief, then recalled her earlier words. “Immortal Fairy, you mentioned this person is breaking through to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage?”

“That’s right. This is the lightning tribulation one must face to break through to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage—the Ninety-Nine Murky Sky Lightning Tribulation, designed by the Heaven Mandate Immortal. Whoever designed this illusory domain must have witnessed it before.”

Faced with the relentless thunderstorm, the Sky-Blanketing True Lord threw his head back and laughed, choosing to meet it head-on with his proud Sword Dao. One by one, the heavenly thunderbolts were sundered by his sword, leaving him unscathed.

However, there seemed to be no end to the barrage in sight, and the Sky-Blanketing True Lord’s strength waned. When the final heavenly lightning struck, it shattered his Sword Dao and hit him.

As the thunderstorm dispersed, the Sky-Blanketing True Lord plummeted from the sky.

Crash! He slammed into a mountain, carving out a crater. Before losing consciousness, he murmured to himself, “Alas! After more than two thousand years of cultivation, I, the Sky-Blanketing True Lord, stood just one step away from the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, only to fail at the final hurdle! My Sword Dao is shattered, and my cultivation has been sealed by the heavenly lightning. I can’t muster even a sliver of power!”

It was unclear how much time had passed until a young woman from a nearby village cautiously approached the crater. Noticing a person within, she plucked up her courage and carried the Sky-Blanketing True Lord home.

When he woke up, his memories were gone. He had no recollection of who he was or what cultivation was.

Upon realizing he had lost his memories, Xiuxiu, the woman who saved him, named him “A’Lei.”[1]

The villagers in the mountains felt that A’Lei was an inauspicious person and demanded that he be driven out. However, Xiuxiu refused, insisting he could stay until he recovered his memories.

Hence, A’Lei lived together with Xiuxiu in the mountains, helping her farm, fish, and hunt. On one occasion, when a demon beast attacked, A’Lei displayed extraordinary strength.

“A’Lei, you...” Xiuxiu was stupefied. A’Lei, who seems like a mortal, had just killed a Foundation Establishment wolf demon with a single punch.

“I...I also don’t know how I did that.” A’Lei was equally bewildered.

Half a year later, a diabolic cultivator placed a magical treasure in the mountains and ordered his underlings to capture all the villagers as sacrificial offerings to enhance the quality of the special treasure.

Xiuxiu was among them.

A’Lei was out when Xiuxiu was taken. When he returned and found her gone, he searched for her like a madman. Tracking down the diabolic cultivators’ lair, he slaughtered several minions in an attempt to rescue Xiuxiu.

Unfortunately, it was too late.

Xiuxiu had already been sacrificed to the unusual treasure, whose quality rose by leaps and bounds after the refinement.

The diabolic cultivator laughed maniacally. With this magical treasure, he would fear no pursuit from the righteous path, allowing him to roam the world carefreely.

A’Lei went berserk, his fury reopening the heavenly lightning’s seal. His shattered Sword Dao pieced together again as heavenly lightning converged to strike him dead, though his radiant Sword Dao pierced through the clouds and scattered the thunderstorm.

He had fully regained his power and memories.

As A’Lei burned with wrath, boundless Sword Dao spread across heaven and earth, engulfing ten thousand mountains. With every step he took, a layer of his seal was broken. Accompanied by endless spirit qi surging with momentum around him, he resembled a devil king who had descended from the sky to annihilate the mortal realm.

“You’re. Courting. Death!”

“I-it’s you!” The diabolic cultivator collapsed to the ground, finally recognizing A’Lei’s identity.

The Sky-Blanketing True Lord, the number one in Sword Dao, and the strongest below the Transcendent Tribulation Stage—he’s the last person you’d want to provoke!

“No no no! With this special treasure in hand, I’m not the same as before!” The diabolic cultivator activated the special treasure, summoning tornadoes and earthquakes to bury the Sky-Blanketing True Lord.

A sword light fell like divine punishment, reducing both the treasure and the diabolic cultivator into ashes.

“Xiuxiu, I’ve avenged you...” the Sky-Blanketing True Lord muttered, cradling her lifeless body as a single tear slipped down his cheek.

The illusory domain ended.

“How was it, how was it?! How was the script this time?” As soon as the illusory domain concluded, Tao Yaoye eagerly asked for Lu Yang’s feedback. She had taken his suggestions to heart and meticulously added a richer narrative.

A male lead with his cultivation sealed and memories lost, lives with a pretty village girl. Over time, he secretly grows feelings for her. Later, the pretty village girl is murdered, and he breaks his seal in a burst of fury, slaying the mastermind in one strike.

Just the thought of it is thrilling.

Lu Yang had a complicated expression, unsure how he should comment. “The script is good, but why did the male lead have my shifu’s face the entire time?”

Sure, Shifu is dashingly handsome with an immortal-like appearance and otherworldly demeanor, but it’s not my first day meeting him. With his face on the male lead, I just couldn’t find it immersive.

Fifth Elder fully agreed.

It should have been a moving finale, but when I saw Old Nine hugging Xiuxiu’s body, I almost laughed out loud.

Chapter 376: Fragile Immortal Sword

Tao Yaoye also helplessly shrugged. “There was no other way. When constructing the illusion domain, I discovered a major problem—the appearance of people conjured out of thin air feels unreal.

“Later, Shifu told me that this is a common problem in constructing illusory domains. Whether you conjure a person out of thin air or piece together features from people you know, the result always feels fake.

“Thus, I could only use the appearance of someone I knew. After considering every option and consulting Shifu, Second Elder, and Eighth Elder for their opinions, we finally agreed that the sect leader’s image fit best.

“Senior Brother, it’s because you know the sect leader too well that you can’t feel immersed with him as the protagonist. But outsiders won’t think the same. After all, they have never even met him.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Fine. You have a point.

Fifth Elder remarked leisurely, “Setting aside Old Nine’s face, the plot itself was quite interesting.”

After experiencing the illusory domain, a new idea had struck him. I could pretend to be a weak cultivator and then reveal my true cultivation at a critical juncture. That does sound thrilling.

He saw the business potential in Tao Yaoye’s invention. It’ll definitely captivate mortals and low-level cultivators; even mid-to-high-level cultivators will find it appealing.

Moreover, it is simple to replicate for mass production.

Setting up the illusory domain isn’t difficult; Tao Yaoye had created the framework in less than half a month. But if outsiders catch wind of it, pirated versions would appear.

The real challenge to such an illusory domain lies in who thought of it first.

We must apply for a patent as quickly as possible.

“The array and talisman are a set. Have you named them yet?”

“Not yet. Senior Brother Lu, could you help think of a name?” Tao Yaoye turned to Lu Yang for help. Senior Brother Lu’s mind is a wellspring of unique ideas.

“Me?” Lu Yang had been enjoying the show. How did this land on me?

“Let me think. The illusory domain isn’t real. Although we’re deeply engaged and wish we could replace the characters while watching, once it’s over, we are filled with melancholy. Ultimately, it’s a reflection in water, a transient dream that doesn’t exist in reality... How about calling it ‘Dreamlike Bubble Mirage?’”[1]

“Dreamlike Bubble Mirage?” Tao Yaoye’s eyes sparkled. She repeated it under her breath a few times, and the more she muttered it, the more she found the name perfect. “Alright, let’s call it Dreamlike Bubble Mirage then!”

“Dreamlike Bubble Mirage—great name.” Fifth Elder nodded approvingly. I’ve always been reassured about Lu Yang’s naming sense.

After all, Lu Yang was the one who came up with my title “Myriad Treasures Heavenly King.”

“Junior Niece Tao, do you have more talismans? I’ll need to take some back for the patent application.”

“Yes, I do!” Tao Yaoye didn’t expect Fifth Elder to agree so readily. She handed over the remaining talismans and the rolled-up array scroll to Fifth Elder.

After tucking them away, Fifth Elder recalled something and revealed an enigmatic smile. “Applying for the patent is not hard, but have you decided who the patent should belong to?”

“Who the patent should belong to?”

Seeing Fifth Elder’s grin reminded her that she had only proposed the idea. Packaging illusory domains into the talismans and simplifying the arrays was the work of Second Elder and Eighth Elder.

Technically speaking, Second Elder and Eighth Elder also hold partial ownership of the patent.

Chapter 377: Enlightened Senior Monk

The moment the immortal sword snapped, Fifth Elder had already planned out the rest of his life.

I, Zhou Xin, have diligently cultivated for two thousand years, finally reaching the cusp of the Transcendent Tribulation Stage and becoming the master of Hundred Refinements Peak. With countless patents in my hand, I’ve amassed massive wealth for the Dao-Seeking Sect year after year.

Whether my lifelong savings can buy even one immortal sword is hard to say. Immortal swords are incredibly hard to forge. After all, they’re weapons exclusive to immortals.

Unlike the immortal treasures from the Everlasting Creed, which are at best half-finished products, Lu Yang’s immortal sword is a bona fide immortal artifact. The difference in power is like night and day.

Legends say that when an immortal artifact took form, its quality was so impeccable that heaven and earth couldn’t tolerate its existence. Countless trials and tribulations would descend upon it. If left alone, the immortal artifact would inevitably crumble. To preserve the immortal artifact, the immortal had to confront the mighty force of heaven and earth—a challenge no less harrowing and perilous than ascending to an immortal again.

To have been formed from manifold trials and tribulations, the value of immortal artifacts is beyond my imagination. How could a mere Fusion cultivator like me ever compensate for one? Optimistically, a lifetime of labor might scrape together enough to afford a single immortal artifact.

Watching Fifth Elder’s spectacular display of expressions, Lu Yang coughed awkwardly. “Fifth Elder, this immortal word isn’t as sturdy as you think. Based on my research, an immortal likely crafted a sword that mimics a real immortal artifact to tide them through a crisis. It’s actually an immortal sword without much power.”

This sword was forged by the Heaven Mandate Immortal, who controlled lightning tribulations, to deceive the two Dragon and Phoenix prodigies, both half-immortal experts.

If it could fool those two, it can naturally fool Fifth Elder.

“Is that so?” Fifth Elder exhaled a sigh of relief.

Right after that, he was worried that Lu Yang was just comforting him, so he began to scrutinize the blade.

Spiritual consciousness scans, quench tests, metallurgy forging analysis... After a series of inspections, Fifth Elder finally figured out the structure and composition of the immortal sword.

“Which lunatic forged this?! It nearly gave me a heart attack!

“First, Fire-Borne Stones and Summit Spirit Stones were mixed and tempered into a blank. Then, with some unknown technique, this sword embryo was rapidly shaped into a spirit sword. Finally, immortal golden power was coated on the spirit sword to fake lightning marks. Even someone as knowledgeable as myself in this trade was fooled into believing it was a genuine immortal sword. No, it’s not just me—it’d be the same for any other Transcendent Tribulation cultivator.

“Unless you touch it, just by using your eyes or spiritual consciousness, this sword is no different from an immortal sword!”

Fifth Elder turned his head to Lu Yang. “You mentioned that an immortal had crafted this sword to tide them through a crisis. What crisis was that? Did the immortal lack money and have to stage scam accidents to swindle others of money?”

Lu Yang, “...”

Although the Qilin Immortal tricked me into eating dirt, exposing how he scammed his wives doesn’t feel appropriate.

Lu Yang believed in one-sided grudges.

Besides, Fifth Elder, do you know the “lunatic” you scolded was the ancient immortal who controlled the heavenly tribulations?

“Didn’t you say you wanted to forge a sword? That’s easy, leave it to me!” Fifth Elder stared at the immortal sword in his hand, raging with flames of fury. If I don’t refine this crappy sword into something else, I’ll renounce my surname!

“This layer of immortal golden power is useless. It only serves the purpose of faking it as an immortal sword. However, the Fire-Borne Stones and Summit Spirit Stones are top-notch materials—perfect for you.”

“How so?”

“You are at the Golden Core Stage, though with your talent, fighting Nascent Soul cultivators is not a problem. These stones are perfect for forging a Nascent Soul-tier spirit sword.”

With Fifth Elder’s status in the artifact refining community, crafting a Nascent Soul-tier spirit sword was like using a sledgehammer to crack a nut. In the past, he always delegated such matters to his disciples. However, he had agreed to take on the task today to vent his anger.

“By the way, do you want a spirit sword or spell sword?” Fifth Elder asked.

Spirit swords were used in direct combat, while spell swords were a medium for spells. Both were tools of sword cultivators. At the moment, Lu Yang had only mastered spirit swords.

“Spirit sword.”

The vast, domed chamber’s walls were lined with vibrantly colored vials. Fifth Elder offhandedly retrieved a cyan vial from the wall and unstopped it. A ball of flame darted out, and the cyan vial now turned jade white. The vial had originally been white, but had changed color due to the flame.

“In my youth, Old Third and I traveled to the Golden Buddhist Kingdom, hoping to find the Lust Desire True Fire in the brothels. Unfortunately, luck was not on our side, and we couldn’t find it in the brothels, though we did encounter an enlightened senior monk who had achieved the Dao in a brothel.

Lu Yang, “...”

Why do I remember that Third Elder got beaten up by someone using the Arhat Fist in the Golden Buddhist Kingdom, which motivated him to work hard and invent the Heaven-Shaking Six Forms?

Chapter 378: Mingyue Sword

Lu Yang was amazed. As expected of an enlightened senior monk from the Golden Buddhist Kingdom. Their words are the epitome of profound Chan wisdom.

His curiosity piqued further. “Elder, how did you get to know this senior monk back then?”

Fifth Elder replied, “This senior monk held an exceptionally high seniority and possessed high ambitions. As a master from the ‘Ming’ character generation,[1] his dharma name was ‘Mingtian (Tomorrow).’ Those who knew him addressed him as Master Mingtian.

“Back then, both Master Mingtian and I took a liking to the same girl, but since one maiden cannot serve two masters, we competed, mainly by comparing who had more spirit stones. In my youth, I had already applied for numerous patents, so I feared no one when it came to wealth.

“When Master Mingtian realized he couldn’t outmatch me in spirit stones, he asked if I could yield to him. Claiming we had affinity with each other, he willingly offered me the No Desire True Fire. I said, ‘No need, no need,’ but he said, ‘You do, you do,’ practically forcing it on me.

“At the time, I felt that beautiful women were nothing more than skeletons under rouge; no matter how attractive they were, they would turn into skeletons one day. Why should I fritter away my days in a brothel? And so, I left the brothel.

“Later, I sought out Master Mingtian to discuss the matter, secretly hoping for a chance to teach him a lesson. Unfortunately, his proficiency in spells put me to shame. Most importantly, he was already at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage—neither I nor Old Third could defeat him.”

Lu Yang, “...”

So Third Elder’s ‘Heaven-Shaking Six Forms’ wasn’t meant to shake the heavens but to shake Master Mingtian, whose name contains the character for ‘heaven?’[2]

“Speaking of which, Immortal Fairy, did Buddhist sects exist in your time?”

“Yes.”

Lu Yang was astonished. According to Buddhist sects’ records, their history dated back to the ancient era. However, after Lu Yang met the Everlasting Immortal Fairy and learned of the existence of the Five Ancient Immortals, he assumed that the Buddhist sects had fabricated such origins to bolster their prestige.

If Buddhist sects and the Buddhist founder existed in the ancient era, why hadn’t the Immortal Fairy ever mentioned the Buddhist founder?

Lu Yang didn’t feel he could associate the Five Ancient Immortals with the Buddhist founder. “Really? Then the Buddhist founder existed too? Was he an immortal?”

“I remember the Buddhist sects having a Buddhist founder, countless enlightened Buddhists, arhats, and bodhisattvas, and something about thirty-three layers of heaven, right?”

“Yes, all documented in various texts.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy revealed a sly smile. “Doesn’t this framework remind you of the Heavenly Court?”

Exclamation marks almost popped out of Lu Yang as a shocking possibility struck him.

Pleased by his reaction, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy chuckled. “That’s right. The Buddhist sects were fabricated by the five of us.”

Now it makes sense why the Immortal Fairy was confident that her Arhat Fruit Fist was more orthodox than the Arhat Fist—that’s because she’s one of the founders of the Buddhist sects. With her status and absolute authority, her word alone could dictate what was orthodox.

Lu Yang drew a sharp breath. The Ancient Five Immortals’ sabotage abilities are even more terrifying than I’d imagined.

The five of you fabricated multiple versions of the Heavenly Court that didn’t get passed down, yet your framework for the Buddhist sects did and even flourished under later generations!

Fifth Elder was unaware of Lu Yang’s conversation with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. He simply saw the change in his expression and found it peculiar.

Though in the Dao-Seeking Sect, this barely counts as strange.

Back in those days, when Old Nine was the same age as Lu Yang, he even fantasized about an ancient ferocious beast sealed within him, where the aura that leaked out would destroy mankind. Thus, Old Nine would maintain a stoic face all day long and pretend to be aloof, telling others that he had sealed away his emotions.

Sometimes, he would even clutch his wrists in agony, claiming that he couldn’t suppress the ferocious beast in him and warning others to flee before he lost control. Now, if anyone brings this up to Old Nine, he’d blow up and swing at them with his sword.

Compared to Old Nine’s random kneeling and wailing, the change in Lu Yang’s expression was pretty normal.

“Perhaps this is the master-disciple legacy and the destiny of a Sword Spirit Root,” Fifth Elder murmured.

“Ah, Fifth Elder, what did you say about the destiny of a Sword Spirit Root?” Lu Yang snapped back to attention, his heart tightening.

Could those with a Sword Spirit Root have some hidden destiny, like how every generation of Sword Spirit Roots faced enemies but failed and carried regrets for the rest of their lives?

Is Shifu’s frivolous lifestyle of playing around in the mortal world a manifestation of a regretful person venting their emotions?

The more Lu Yang pondered, the more plausible he found it.

“The No Desire True Fire is my most frequently used true fire. Magical treasures tempered with this true fire can grant their wielders maximum composure during battles.” Fifth Elder believed “composure” to be the ultimate treasure in increasing one’s win rate.

With a wave of his hand, he took true fire from another vial. “This is the Six Ding Divine Fire, an ancestral true fire passed down through generations of Hundred Refinements Peak’s masters. It can devour impurities and is perfect for forging artifacts. Separating the Fire-Borne Stones and Summit Spirit Stones within the immortal sword requires the Six Ding Divine Fire.”

He placed the Six Ding True Fire in the center of the artifact-refining chamber and activated the arrays beneath his feet and on the walls. The temperature rapidly rose, and Lu Yang was forced to protect himself with the Three Flavor True Fire.

Unfazed by the high temperature, Fifth Elder stared fixedly as the flames licked away the immortal sword’s outermost coating of immortal golden powder, revealing the layer underneath. The original appearance of the immortal sword was blackish-gray and nondescript, bearing no signs of an immortal forged from two precious, mystic stones.

Under the Six Ding Divine Fire, the immortal sword melted and split into two lumps of metallic liquids filled with spirit nature, one red and one black. Fifth Elder brandished an iron hammer, fiercely smashing the metal liquid. Despite exploding within the flames, the metal liquid could never escape them.

As Fifth Elder pointed with his left hand, the No Desire True Fire hovering in the air rushed into the Six Ding Divine Flame, and the two fused, creating a hybrid with dual properties.

Lu Yang didn’t grasp the brilliance packed in this simple move. If a skillful artifact-refining master had been present, it would have been enough to upend their understanding of artifact refinement.

After the metal liquids formed from the Fire-Borne Stones and Summit Spirit Stones merged, it gradually took shape and formed a sword embryo.

Retrieving the sword embryo from the true fire, Fifth Elder extended two fingers and gently traced them against both sides, and decorative patterns emerged. These were sword patterns aimed at minimizing wear and tear.

Every magical treasure had its unique pattern, but most artifact-refining masters weren’t capable of such engraving methods. Those who could produce such patterns with just a touch were exceedingly rare.

Hiss! The bright red sword embryo was repeatedly quenched with water until its temperature cooled, revealing its original silver-white color.

After that, Fifth Elder fitted the sword hilt and sword tassel, finally finishing the sword.

“Here, test it.” Fifth Elder tossed the spirit sword to Lu Yang.

As Lu Yang wielded the sword, he found it so light that it felt like an extension of his arm, allowing him to swing it to his heart’s content.

“Break!”

“Cleave!”

“Slash!”

Lu Yang executed the sword mantras, his motions fluid and practiced, as if he had used this blade for a long time. After he completed his set of sword techniques, he withdrew his sword, beaming widely. “Good sword!”

“Give it a name,” Fifth Elder urged with a grin.

Examining the sword pattern of his new spirit sword, Lu Yang proposed, “A sword is a tool that kills. The sword is silver-white, like the silver moon in the sky. What about calling it Mingyue Sword, as in ‘Nether Moon?’”

Fifth Elder nodded. “Qingfeng Sword, Mingyue Sword—they sound matching.”

1. Some clans or families like to use the same character in the names of people from the same generation. You might have seen examples of this in siblings who share the same character in their names. ☜

2. This was truly difficult to translate into English. Basically, the ‘tian’ character in the technique can mean heaven, sky, day etc, and while ‘Mingtian’ means tomorrow, the ‘tian’ character is the same. Hence, the technique's name misleads people into thinking it’s supposed to be grand, but it might have referred to just the person instead. ☜

Chapter 379: Intermediate Golden Core Stage

“The Mingyue Sword is quite formidable, more than enough for you to wield at your current Golden Core Stage. But if you reach the Nascent Soul Stage, this sword will no longer match your strength.” Fifth Elder chuckled. Though the Mingyue Sword may be a Nascent Soul-tier magical treasure, it doesn’t mean it is suited for Lu Yang when he is at the Nascent Soul Stage.

Lu Yang nodded in understanding. Magical treasures were also categorized into different tiers, and if mismatched to one’s cultivation, they would become a hindrance instead. This was why cultivators prize growth-type magical treasures, though such treasures were exorbitantly rare and demanded exceptional craftsmanship.

“What tier is the Qingfeng Sword, then?” Lu Yang recalled the sword he frequently used. It was a gift from Yun Zhi to celebrate his successful Foundation Establishment.

“The sword Junior Niece Yun gave you... I can’t tell what tier it is.” Fifth Elder shook his head slowly. He had long noticed there was something special about Lu Yang’s Qingfeng Sword.

“Is it a growth-type magical treasure?” Lu Yang had wielded the sword from the Basic Foundation Establishment Stage all the way to the Basic Golden Core Stage, never once experiencing incompatibility issues. In his mind, only a growth-type magical treasure could fulfil this condition.

Besides, this was a gift from Big Senior Sister—how could anything she bestowed be ordinary?

Fifth Elder corrected Lu Yang’s misconception. “No, growth-type magical treasures aren’t like this. To grow from Foundation Establishment to Golden Core-tier, they require various spirit metals and divine ores.

“Think of them as frameworks. To enhance their quality, you must constantly feed them materials like spirit metals and divine ores. Tell me, has your Qingfeng Sword ever required such additions of materials?

“Moreover, growth-type magical treasures evolve by major realms. The feel of wielding one at the Basic Foundation Establishment Stage differs from the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage. Have you noticed it?”

Lu Yang pondered and realized it was true. “So is my Qingfeng Sword...”

“It’s been sealed by Junior Niece Yun, with so many layers of seals that they’re uncountable. That’s why I said I couldn’t determine the Qingfeng Sword’s tier.

“With each increment in your abilities, a seal will fade. Thus, no matter how far you progress in your cultivation realm, you will always find the Qingfeng Sword perfectly attuned to your hand.

“Junior Niece Yun cares a lot about you. This sword and its countless seals are priceless treasures.”

Lu Yang hadn’t expected Yun Zhi to invest so much thought into the Qingfeng Sword and was deeply touched.

Fifth Elder interrupted his thoughts. “Alright, enough chatter. I still have to file patent applications for Junior Niece Tao.”

Lu Yang hurriedly said, “Many thanks for forging the Mingyue Sword, Elder. Please don’t let me hold you back from your busy schedule.”

With a wave of his hand, Fifth Elder produced his flying shuttle and vanished with a swoosh.

“Immortal Fairy, can you identify the true nature of the Qingfeng Sword?” Lu Yang remembered that apart from his sect and seniors he relied on, he still had a golden finger cheat—the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

She glanced at the Qingfeng Sword and shook her head frankly. “It’s pasted too tightly. I can’t discern anything.”

Lu Yang took a moment to parse the meaning of her words. The seals are too numerous to see through the sword’s quality.

Returning to Heaven’s Gate Peak, Lu Yang didn’t see Yun Zhi around. She’s probably still interrogating and torturing the Calamity Venerable Lord. Either he has an unbreakable backbone and a stubborn mouth, or he knows too many secrets to spill in a short time.

“It’s a pity. I was planning to help you ask about the royalty payments.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy secretly let out a sigh of relief, the burden disappearing from her shoulders.

Lu Yang side-eyed her. Immortal Fairy, you might as well write “terrified” on your forehead.

“Time to cultivate.” Lu Yang remembered his fundamental duty as a cultivator.

I’m not just a genius, but a genius who works hard!

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy side-eyed Lu Yang. “Ever since you formed your golden core, when have you cultivated properly?”

Lu Yang shot back with conviction, counting on his fingers. “How could you say that?! Was it because I didn’t want to cultivate? No, it’s clearly because there was too much happening!

“After returning from the jungle, I was first dragged to the Everlasting Ruins by Big Senior Sister, then we paid Shifu a visit in passing.

“Later, Junior Brother Li was troubled by Qin Haoran’s memories, so Old Meng and I took him outside for a change of mood, only to accidentally bump into the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s members, which forced us to fabricate the Heavenly Court Creed to establish a connection with the Nine-Netherworlds Creed.

“Subsequently, we took Fifth Elder with us to look for the Nine-Netherworlds Creed again, reinforcing the Heavenly Court Creed’s credibility.

“To continue writing the Clear Heart True Nature Mantra, I even camped in the scripture library for half a month, successfully composing the Golden Core Chapter.

“Finally, Old Meng and I attended the Qing Province Grand Ceremony and ran into archaic cultivators.

“Only two months have passed since I formed the Unbeatable Golden Core!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy, “...”

Well, that does seem to be the case.

Has Lu Yang’s life been so eventful that it’s misled me into thinking a long time has passed?

Choosing to reside in Lu Yang’s mental space was a great decision! Where else could I have encountered such fun events?

Lu Yang continued with force, “Besides, despite being occupied by so many matters, I still found pockets of time to cultivate! Was my cultivation progress affected?” I’m speaking the truth. Whenever I had time, I’d open my mouth to devour spirit qi, allowing me to cultivate anytime and anywhere, which made it convenient.

Seated on a boulder scarred with sword marks, Lu Yang closed his eyes, sensing the boundless sword intent within.

Big Senior Sister told me that Shifu loved using this rock for sword practice in his youth. Over time, it inevitably became imbued with sword intent. To sword cultivators, this rock was a precious treasure of immense worth. By sitting on the rock, one can cultivate and comprehend sword intent, elevating their enlightenment of the Sword Dao, thereby effectively killing two birds with one stone.

Assuming the lotus position, Lu Yang opened his mouth and tilted his head back. Those who didn’t know would think he had fallen asleep.

Spirit qi gushed into him, expanding his meridians. His cultivation rose bit by bit, with each increment bringing an inexplicable euphoria. No wonder some are happy to cultivate and go into seclusion for decades or even centuries, emerging to find the world transformed.

Lu Yang wouldn’t go into seclusion for so long, and the Dao-Seeking Sect also discouraged such seclusion methods. Even the cultivation-obsessed Yun Zhi’s request for her master was only a seclusion of three days.

“Seclusion builds experience, not brains—you know that, right?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy concurred with the Dao-Seeking Sect’s philosophy, increasingly assured that becoming the Dao-Seeking Sect’s honorary guest elder was a correct choice.

She added, “Back then, I had to claw my way up. Countless famous individuals were defeated at my hand, and I grew rapidly with every battle.

“You should learn from me! Improve through combat by facing the vast world and its myriad beings. This cultivation method can enhance your cultivation realm and make you as smart as me!”

After hearing her words, Lu Yang reckoned that prolonging his seclusion might not be a bad idea.

Half a month later, Lu Yang opened his eyes slowly and exhaled a clear breath. His eyes gleamed frostily, and his momentum flared and withdrew with ease.

The corners of his mouth curved into a smile.

“Intermediate Golden Core Stage, huh?”

Chapter 380: Progressive Body Refinement Philosophy

The moment Lu Yang successfully advanced to the Intermediate Golden Core Stage, a rainbow appeared overhead. The spirit qi swimming through the air resembled fish frolicking in the water and blowing bubbles. Wild grass and leaves rustled despite the absence of wind, while dew condensed from spirit qi gathered on their surfaces, rolling and dripping to the ground before rising as mist.

An unusual celestial phenomenon had manifested in celebration of Lu Yang’s breakthrough.

“Congratulations, you’re at the Intermediate Golden Core Stage now!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy clapped enthusiastically.

Lu Yang helplessly reminded her, “Immortal Fairy, this is just a minor breakthrough, not an immortal ascension. I don’t need any unusual celestial phenomenon. Disperse it, please.”

“Oh.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy waved her hand, dispelling the spell.

All phenomena vanished.

Lu Yang hadn’t expected himself to advance to the Intermediate Golden Core Stage so quickly. I didn’t even feel a bottleneck. It’s probably because I ate the meals prepared by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

After all, surviving an immortal’s trial ought to yield some rewards.

Lu Yang felt something warm against his chest. It was a wooden plaque inscribed with “Nine Netherworlds.”

A message slowly materialized on the wooden plaque: Running low on fire seeds and barbeque grills. Meet you at the shop’s headquarters.

This was a magical treasure Vice Creed Leader Shi used to communicate with Lu Yang. Each party could only send one message before a lengthy cooldown.

Lu Yang replied tersely: OK

The barbeque grills aren’t an issue; Fifth Elder has long produced a huge batch of Automated Barbeque Grills.

Fire seeds will need Meng Jingzhou’s cooperation though.

“Let’s see what Old Meng is up to.”

~~~

Approaching Body Refinement Peak, Lu Yang could already feel the overwhelming yang energy. Any ordinary ghost lingering nearby would have its soul scorched to cinders.

At the foot of the mountain, Lu Yang could hear Third Elder’s thunderous voice. “Body refinement means tempering every inch of your body! No weakness is allowed!

“You must know that our greatest asset as physique cultivators is our strong physical bodies. If it fails, what other advantages do you have?!

“Lately, I’ve noticed slackers among you, shaving their heads to avoid cultivating their hair. This is self-deception!

“Others focus solely on cultivating their hair and have neglected their shadows. What are you trying to achieve by leaving such a glaring vulnerability to your opponents?!

“We physique cultivators fear no challenge, but neither can we tolerate complacency!”

With Third Elder’s wealth of combat experience, he knew that fortifying oneself was the best defense against unpredictable attacks.

Lu Yang, “...”

Refining the body includes training the shadow?

Is this how physique cultivators outside train?

Traces of life daily remained, clear evidence that people had once lived here, yet they had all disappeared without explanation. It was as if someone had frozen time and plucked away the occupants one by one before time flowed again.

Tao Yaoye’s hair stood on end. This bore an uncanny resemblance to the ghost stories she had huddled under blankets to read at night as a child. She gingerly tugged at the corner of Lu Yang’s sleeve, instantly feeling reassured.

“Creed Leader Shi, can you tell what happened here?”

Vice Creed Leader Shi analyzed, “As far as I know, there are two methods that could achieve this: Space Confinement and Time Suspension.

“If it’s Space Confinement, that’s somewhat manageable. A Fusion cultivator proficient in spatial spells could pull it off. But if it’s Time Suspension, we are in serious trouble. To stop time, one would need to be at least at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage!

“In my memory, I’ve never heard of anyone capable of stopping time. Even Transcendent Tribulation cultivators can only do so in theory!”

Lu Yang nodded. “The Epoch Immortal could accomplish it.”

“Epoch Immortal?” Vice Creed Leader Shi was startled. I’ve never heard of this immortal before.

Lu Yang nodded again. “The Epoch Immortal wielded the Epoch Dao Fruit. His understanding of time was number one in the ancient era; no one could even come close.”

“Something like that happened?!” Vice Creed Leader Shi blurted out. The Dao of Time is profound and elusive; even grasping the basics is a challenge.

To think that an ancient immortal had once wielded time as their Dao Fruit! The sheer power of such Dao Fruit must have been terrifying!

Tao Yaoye was also stunned. Why does Senior Brother Lu speak so casually of immortals all the time? Judging by Vice Creed Leader’s reaction, this is probably something even the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s vice creed leaders are unaware of.

So where did Senor Brother Lu learn about such things?

Has the gap between us already grown so vast?

Gradually, the shock faded from Vice Creed Leader Shi’s face. He blinked and turned to Lu Yang. “Oh, my mind wandered for a bit just now. What were you saying?”

“Nothing much.” Lu Yang had thought a Fusion cultivator could be immune to the immortal-forgetting trait. But it seems like even an Advanced Fusion cultivator like Vice Creed Leader Shi can’t resist the effect of immortals.

“The likelihood of our foe being a Transcendent Tribulation expert who manipulates time is slim. I’m more inclined to believe it’s a Fusion cultivator capable of using Space Confinement.”

From the moment they stepped into the village, Lu Yang’s brow had been furrowed. So many deaths, and in such a bizarre manner—just how terrifying must the culprit be?

To have killed people right under the imperial court’s nose without detection...

If Huai’an Village is like this, what about other villages? Exactly how many people had the culprit killed?

Vice Creed Leader Shi crouched down and scooped up a handful of soil. Rubbing it between his fingers, the original dark-brown earth revealed a dark crimson hue.

Noticing Lu Yang’s and Tao Yaoye’s confusion, he explained, “Too many people have died here that even the soil reeks of blood! But this has let me confirm one thing!”

“What?”

“The bloody aura here is overwhelming, yet the scent is too faint in comparison. Someone must have transferred the bloody aura elsewhere!”

“I remember that bloody aura can be refined into a Myriad Souls Banner, a major weapon of the diabolic path?” Lu Yang sieved through his knowledge of the diabolic path.

“That’s right. Be it crafting Soul-Summoning Banners, Soul-Luring Banners, or Myriad Souls Banners, bloody aura and resentment energy are necessary.” Brimming with confidence, Vice Creed Leader Shi crushed the soil into powder and tossed it into the air. With one hand, he swiftly formed seals and shot out a black sigil.

The soil powder gathered around the sigil, drifting through the air like silk before floating into the distance.

“Come, follow it. If they had refined the bloody aura on-site, tracking it would be difficult. But since they transferred it first, I can trace the residual bloody aura to the true refinement location!”

Vice Creed Leader Shi grabbed Lu Yang and Tao Yaoye, flying several hundred li in one go before landing in a mountain range.

“The trail ends there!” Vice Creed Leader Shi pointed ahead.

The three exchanged glances and nodded, approaching cautiously while holding their breath.

Suddenly, Vice Creed Leader Shi and Lu Yang halted simultaneously, with Lu Yang grabbing Tao Yaoye to stop her from moving forward.

Tao Yaoye peered ahead. Lush trees, birds singing, floral scents—nothing seems amiss.

Vice Creed Leader Shi looked at Lu Yang in surprise, not expecting him to react as swiftly as himself.

“You sensed it too? One more step and we’d hit a barrier!”

Lu Yang nodded. “In the ancient era, this was called the Ghost Wall Array. Those who enter this array will lose all sense of direction and become hopelessly lost until they die trapped inside!

“It still goes by the same name now.”

“To have placed a Ghost Wall Array here to deter intruders must imply there are secrets within!”

“And not just that! Various arrays are hidden within the Ghost Wall Array, blocking external detection while preventing those inside from sensing the outside!”

“Someone is likely cultivating inside and doesn’t want to be disturbed!”

“I catch a whiff of blood. It's leaking from the array!”

“Judging by the arrangement of the arrays, it doesn’t seem to be the work of a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator.”

“As long as it isn’t a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator.”

Their back-and-forth analysis pieced together what might have happened inside the array: A Fusion cultivator had set up arrays in the mountain to refine bloody aura without being disturbed, and their cultivating within the array was undoubtedly connected to the Huai’an Village massacre.

Tao Yaoye followed behind silently, struggling to keep pace with Lu Yang’s deductions. Why can Senior Brother Lu discuss such matters so fluently with a Fusion cultivator?

During external missions, Tao Yaoye had met stellar cultivators at the Foundation Establishment and Golden Core stages. They spoke eloquently before me and appeared omniscient, but they would stammer timidly in the face of Divine Transfiguration cultivators. If they encountered Void Refinement or Fusion cultivators, they wouldn’t even be able to form a coherent sentence. Compared to Senior Brother Lu, they fall far short.

Vice Creed Leader Shi chuckled. He particularly enjoyed interrupting other people’s cultivation. Best if I can drive the archaic Fusion cultivator inside into qi deviation!

He whipped out an eight-sided hammer and tossed it upward. As if air was being blown into the hammer, it inflated to the size of a hill, each corner gleaming coldly.

The hammer plunged downward like a meteor with overbearing momentum.

Crack. The colossal hammer appeared to have struck something invisible.

Rubbing his hands, Vice Creed Leader Shi attempted to press down harder, imbuing the eight-sided hammer with more force until it shattered the invisible barrier.

Crack. Crack. Crash. The barrier broke, unleashing a wave of blood fetor.

Tao Yaoye’s beautiful eyes widened in disbelief as she stared at the sight before her.

Gone was the picturesque scenery.

Trees were withered, blood flowed like rivers, the earth was stained red, and ghost shadows howled furiously in bitter winds. At the center sat a wizened old man cross-legged beside a tattered blood-red banner.

“Who are you?!” The old man’s eyes snapped open, automatically ignoring Lu Yang and Tao Yaoye to glare fixedly at Vice Creed Leader Shi with his teeth gnashing.

My arrays should have been undetectable! The only flaw was the leaked bloody aura, which can only be discovered by seasoned old monsters.

But they have no grudge with me? Why would they destroy my arrays?!

“I’m your grandfather!” Vice Creed Leader Shi roared with laughter, recalling his eight-sided hammer and swinging it toward him.

The shriveled old man grabbed his tattered banner and dodged, all the while reciting something.

Vice Creed Leader Shi didn’t think much of it. Wielding a bone scythe in his other hand, he hacked relentlessly at the old man. He could tell that breaking the array had caused a backlash to the old man, leaving him in poor condition.

Time to beat a drowning dog! Pulverize the enemy when he’s down!

“That’s all you have? What an embarrassment to archaic cultivators! And you even refined some Myriad Souls Banner? I outgrew such toys long ago!

“Your grandfather wants you dead!” Vice Creed Leader Shi displayed his might, driving the old man back without allowing a single proper counterattack.

Boom! The eight-sided hammer and bone scythe descended simultaneously, smashing the wizened old man into the mountain.

“Good, good! The younger generation truly is to be feared!” The old man was so irate that he laughed as he walked out of the mountain cave, the tattered banner in his hand now glowing.

Vice Creed Leader Shi clicked his tongue. “Got too careless.”

“How so?” Tao Yaoye asked.

Vice Creed Leader Shi pointed at the wizened old man and spat a mouthful of spit. “I was too carried away just now that I didn’t notice that he kept refining his Myriad Souls Banner throughout the fight. It’s now complete. This won’t be easy to deal with.”

The old man’s face was so dark as if ink could drip out, and his words sounded like they had slithered through clenched teeth, giving people an uncomfortable feeling.

“This esteemed one chanced upon a vast amount of bloody aura, perfect for refining the Myriad Souls Banner. Today, I’ll let you juniors know my true power!

“Myriad Souls Banner, rise!”

Bitter winds screeched with a bone-piercing chill as they converged on the wizened old man. Countless ghostly apparitions of massive sizes manifested behind him, their numbers far beyond ten thousand.

As the old man laughed out loud, the Myriad Souls Banner’s refinement was finally completed, the silhouettes of the ghosts growing more distinct.

Lu Yang recognized their forms: pig, cow, sheep...

“Hmm?”

All four present were dazed.

Chapter 385: How Could I Not Have Gained Anything From Being Struck by Lightning Every Month?

The frigid wind brushed against their faces as silence fell, save for the mournful wails of various ghosts reverberating through the area.

Oink oink—

Moo—

Baa—

Neither the wizened old man nor Vice Creed Leader Shi, both of whom were Fusion cultivators with millennia of experience, had ever witnessed a spectacle like today’s.

Vice Creed Leader Shi’s expression became disjointed. Just moments ago, he had solemnly declared the situation dire now that their opponent had successfully refined the Myriad Souls Banner.

But judging by the current circumstances, even if our opponent refines ten of such banners, it likely won’t pose any trouble.

The wizened old man hadn’t expected to produce such playthings. He had simply passed by a small village and discovered its astonishing concentration of bloody aura, which was perfect for refining a Myriad Souls Banner. Thus, he swept all the bloody aura away and hurriedly chose a remote location.

Yet this absurd barnyard assembly is what I summoned?

Vice Creed Leader Shi, “...”

“Yes, you can use infants’ souls to refine Myriad Souls Banners, but you’re overlooking one thing. Diabolic cultivators don’t immediately refine the infants’ souls into a Myriad Souls Banner. This process takes years. During this time, while the souls’ forms remain unchanged, their minds gradually mature until reaching an age where they can understand the commands. Only then is refinement complete.”

Before the Everlasting Immortal Fairy became an immortal, she’d frequently interact with diabolic cultivators. During the chaotic ancient era, diabolic cultivators were everywhere; her understanding of them surpassed even Vice Creed Leader Shi’s.

Senior Brother Lu is so erudite.

Lu Yang and Tao Yaoye immediately felt like they were mired in a swamp, barely able to move.

“You think you’re the only one who can set rules? I hereby establish the rule: Within five hundred zhang, no one is allowed to use diabolic artifacts!”

The Eighteen-Generations Clan Necklace dimmed, and its eighteen diabolic skulls vanished.

“You’re only left with a soul, yet you dare challenge me?!” The wizened old man charged at Vice Creed Leader Shi, only to be sent flying by the hammer.

“Try getting struck by heavenly lightning worth a billion every month—you’d be like this too!” Vice Creed Leader Shi bellowed in rage. I put my life on the line every month to endure the lightning tribulation. How could I not have gained anything?!

Chapter 386: This Esteemed One Is a Protector of the Heavenly Court—The Nether World Heavenly King

Among the Great Yu Dynasty’s Fusion cultivators of the diabolic path, I was ranked as one of the strongest. Only the most elite Fusion diabolic overload could pressure me.

Run!

“Fake. But they’re genuinely close to the real deal. Had they infused the soul of plants into it, it would have become real. Even in my era, such a skill was rare.”

“How are you at the Painting Dao, Immortal Fairy?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy waved her hand nonchalantly. “A minor art only poor scholars dabble in. This immortal doesn’t deign to learn this kind of thing.”

First Elder seemed to have recalled something and turned around. “Speaking of Painting Dao, I once saw an ancient text with records of two ancient immortals: a demon immortal and a wood immortal. When the demon immortal was imprisoned in a painting by the wood immortal, they started an all-out fight, which radiated with immortal light and shook the universe. If it weren’t for the Dragon and Phoenix old ancestors intervening, numerous stars might have been destroyed. Multiple ancient texts record this event to different extents.

“Lu Yang, you’re familiar with ancient history. Have you heard of this?”

Lu Yang shook his head. It was his first time hearing of it. Demon immortal and wood immortal—could it have been the Qilin Immortal and Epoch Immortal?

Time to use my golden finger cheat.

“Immortal Fairy, have you heard of this?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy pondered, and realization sparkled in her eyes. “I remember now! After eating one of my meals, the Epoch Immortal spilled the truth about this matter!

“You’ve asked the right person! No one else would know!”

“...Setting that aside, why would the Epoch Immortal spill the truth after eating your food?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was bewildered why Lu Yang would ask such a question and answered matter-of-factly, “Isn’t that perfectly normal? You get a food coma after a full meal. After the Heaven Mandate Immortal, the Epoch Immortal, and the rest ate my meals, they often became drowsy and face-planted onto the table, rambling away. Ask them anything in this state, and they’d spill everything. Moreover, they wouldn’t remember what they’d said afterward.”

”Please continue.”

She resumed, “I didn’t deign to learn the Painting Dao, but the Epoch Immortal was highly interested in it and did have some skills. Even I struggled to distinguish his creations from reality. After all, he was a Jianmu World Tree demon spirit and stood at the peak of plant beings, carrying an innate connection with paper.”

Chapter 388: Battle Between the Demon Immortal and the Wood Immortal

“A painter’s two most essential tools are immortal paper and immortal brush. At that time, he had already become an immortal, and it was hard to find a brush suitable for immortals. Even the materials to craft one weren't available. Without them, not even the Heaven Mandate Immortal could forge one.

“Immortal paper wasn’t a problem for him. He could take some of his wood shavings to create it. But the immortal brush was a different matter.

“The closest materials were our hair. Perhaps because we were all human, our hair couldn’t be refined into an immortal brush. Thus, he turned his attention to the Qilin Immortal.

“A tuft of fur from the Qilin Immortal’s tail was perfect for the task.

“First, he painted a ‘Hundred Beasts Painting’ with a half-immortal brush, depicting females that were peerlessly beautiful in the eyes of demon beasts. Then, he invited the Qilin Immortal to his house to admire the painting. Seeing the Qilin Immortal tempted, he suggested that the Qilin Immortal could try entering the painting.

“Overjoyed and unsuspecting, the Qilin Immortal proclaimed the Epoch Immortal his good brother before eagerly immersing himself in the Hundred Beasts Painting.

“While the Qilin Immortal was distracted, the Epoch Immortal slipped into the painting and shaved off all the fur from the Qilin Immortal’s tail.

“Flying into a rage, the Qilin Immortal scuffled with the Epoch Immortal, dishing out various immortal spells in succession, astonishing cultivators from several planets. The commotion even drew the attention of the Dragon and Phoenix prodigies. Rushing to the scene, they asked for an account of what’d happened.

“Naturally, the Qilin Immortal couldn’t admit that he gave in to lust and was sabotaged by the Epoch Immortal. He could only indignantly claim that in his moment of carelessness, the Epoch Immortal had trapped him in the painting.

“The Epoch Immortal explained that he simply wanted to determine his progress in the cultivation of the Painting Dao and tested it out on the Qilin Immortal, pleading the Qilin Immortal for forgiveness.

“The Epoch Immortal said, “This is what I should do.’

Reconciliation, huh?

The ancient texts also mentioned that the wood immortal drew a Hundred Beasts Painting and trapped the demon immortal inside, commanding the hundred beasts to attack him. Does that ring a bell?”

Lu Yang replied inwardly, What ancient texts? Their embellishments have gone way past the line. Better to bury the truth in my stomach. If the Dragon and Phoenix prodigies catch wind of it and beat up the Qilin Immortal again, he’ll trace it to me. My life may be gone then.

He shook his head blankly. “I’ve never heard of it before.”

“Alright then.” First Elder didn’t suspect Lu Yang. After all, Lu Yang is still young; he can’t possibly know everything.

Pressing him underfoot and looking down at him, I slowly announced my title, ‘This esteemed one is a protector of the Heavenly Court Creed—the Nether World Heavenly King!’”

Grandpa Ba’s eyes gleamed. How did I miss out on this flashy event?

First Elder inwardly remarked, I manage the intelligence in the Dao-Seeking Sect—of course, I knew about Lu Yang’s trip before you did.

Chapter 389: Alignment of Nine Stars

Returning to Heaven’s Gate Peak, Lu Yang sat cross-legged on the sword qi boulder and opened his mouth to devour spirit qi as he calmed his mind to cultivate. An endless stream of spirit qi gushed into his body, converting into pure spirit energy under the effects of the Clear Heart True Nature Mantra and surging through him.

Slowly extending two fingers, a one-zhang-long cyan sword qi condensed at his fingertips.

“Go!” With a sudden thrust of his fingers, the cyan sword qi shot forth, piercing clean through three trees and embedding half an inch into the fourth before dissipating.

These were no ordinary trees from the outside world but Qiu-Dragon Trees specially planted by the Taciturn Daoist Priest on Heaven’s Gate Peak. Their roots were as thick as qiu dragons[1], and their barks were layered like the scales of dragons.

Legends speak of a great battle that once erupted in the Demon Realm, which the Dragon Tribe participated in. Innumerable true dragons perished, their blood dyeing the rivers red and seeping into the trees by the bank, mutating these trees to obtain the power of true dragons.

This was the origin of Qiu-Dragon Trees.

Priced exorbitantly, second-class and third-class sects could only afford one or two Qiu-Dragon Trees for decoration purposes, a stark contrast from Heaven’s Gate Peak, which had an entire grove of Qiu-Dragon Trees.

Peering through the holes in the first three trees, Lu Yang’s heart leapt with joy at the half-inch indent in the fourth tree. Previously, his sword qi could pierce through only three trees before depleting upon striking the fourth, not even leaving a scratch on its bark.

“All those days of cultivation paid off!” Lu Yang felt that his control over sword qi had become more seamless. The three-inch cyan sword qi coiled around his fingers deftly like a snake. He could even use it to clean his ears now.

“It’s a pity that no peers at the same cultivation realm can match me in the Sword Dao. Otherwise, a friendly discussion would have been delightful.” Lu Yang shook his head regretfully.

Although he hadn’t pitted his Sword Dao against peers of the same cultivation stage, the confidence from his Unbeatable Golden Core made him believe that he was number one!

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded secretly. This is the Unbeatable Momentum! Lu Yang resembles my younger self; he’s destined for greatness!

“By the way, Immortal Fairy, since the five of you made up the Buddhist sects, do you know ‘Buddhist Kingdom in Palm?’”

“What’s that?”

“You’ve never heard of this mighty ability? It’s a supreme spatial ability from the Buddhist sects, surpassing even the Six Mighty Abilities like the Heavenly Eye Ability and Heavenly Ear Ability.

“Buddhist Kingdom in Palm—a great nation in the palm with infinite space. Once you land within the palm, neither supreme mighty abilities nor extreme speeds can let you escape. Once a single palm descends, it signifies the fall of a nation. It is unparalleled.

“Some say that the Golden Buddhist Kingdom in the west is actually a manifestation of Buddhist Kingdom in Palm.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy mused, “I’ve never heard of Buddhist Kingdom in Palm, but it should be a spell created by later generations or a renamed spell from our era.

“For example, I know a mighty ability called Cosmos in Palm, where the palm encompasses heaven, earth, and the cosmos. The stars in the sky are mere playthings in the palm, and the sun and moon are mere yin and yang orbs.

“Perhaps Cosmos in Palm was rebranded by later generations as Buddhist Kingdom in Palm.

“Remember how the Ancient Nameless One refined the stars into the continent? They might have used this move!”

The thought of the Ancient Nameless One wielding Cosmos in Palm made Lu Yang’s scalp tingle. To casually rearrange the stars—what terrifying power must it have been?! Even natural disasters become as trivial as dust before the mighty force of immortals!

“Do you know the rotation of the stars follows a pattern? Oh right, you’ve never been to space, so you haven’t seen stars orbit.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy continued in a smug tone. “During my travels through outer space, I observed asteroids orbiting stars and small stars orbiting larger stars. I couldn’t help but hypothesize—is the orbit of smaller bodies around larger bodies some law or pattern of stellar motions?

“According to my observation, hypothesis, modeling, calculation, and verification, finally—”

“You finally figured out the pattern of stellar motions?” Lu Yang interjected. The Immortal Fairy still has rare intellectual moments.

“—Finally, the Nine-Layers Immortal told me that someone else had already deciphered the law that governs the motion of stars.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Fair enough. It’s not like you can go to space only after becoming an immortal. Even Fusion and Transcendent Tribulation cultivators can travel to outer space. Any motivated person who camps beside the stars for a few years can figure it out. If someone has temporal spells, half an hour might be all they need to solve it.

“Back then, astrological divination with stars was trendy. A great divination master pointed to a nebula and predicted that when nine stars align, chaos would break out in their respective regions, with the common people displaced and the star regions destroyed.

“And according to the orbital patterns of stars, the nine-star alignment will occur in three years!

“This diviner was Shi Cang of the Exalted Shi Clan, renowned for his fifty-percent prediction accuracy.

“As you know, some cultivators believe in fate, while some don’t, and everyone began discussing how to deal with this disaster.

“Believers felt that Master Shi Cang was right and urged inhabitants of these stars to evacuate to habitable stars with sparse populations.

“Skeptics felt no need to make billions of living beings migrate just based on one man’s words, for this process would inevitably result in a high death toll. Upon arriving at the new stars, everything must start over, but how many generations would that take?”

“So, Immortal Fairy, were you a believer or a skeptic?”

“After listening to it, I smashed one of the uninhabited stars. That way, the alignment of nine stars would never be possible!”

Lu Yang silently gave her a thumbs-up. The Immortal Fairy is truly impressive.

“Although I had yet to become an immortal then, crushing one or two stars was simple. After breaking that star, I realized that an array was hidden in the star core. Puzzled, I investigated further and discovered that the same array was present in the star cores of these eight stars.

“According to my speculation, when the nine stars align, the array will resonate with one another and trigger a giant explosion.”

“It was a deliberate setup?!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy fiercely spat. “That’s right! It was that bastard Shi Cang who used divination as a guise to sow chaos and line his own pockets. In fact, every disaster they supposedly predicted was orchestrated by them in the shadows!

“In a fit of rage, I recklessly slaughtered Shi Cang. Despite his clan stepping in with apologies and reparations, I still chose to kill him without hesitation. Offended by my refusal to give them face, the Exalted Shi Clan hindered my path to ascension.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy huffed. “But their attempts were futile. With my unparalleled talent across the ages, when it was time for me to advance to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, nothing could stop me!”

Lu Yang applauded vigorously. The schemes and conspiracies during the ancient era really operated on an unimaginable level, easily plotting on the scale of stars. Just how many lives would have been caught in the catastrophes?

While Lu Yang was mulling over how terrifying the ancient schemes were, he heard the Everlasting Immortal Fairy ask, “By the way, do you want to learn Cosmos in Palm? I know it.”

“Cosmos in Palm? Me?” Lu Yang stared at his small palms. The Immortal Fairy is overestimating me.

Chapter 390: Learning Cosmos in Palm

“I find you remarkably gifted in the comprehension of the Dao of Space. Think about it, Close Horizon From Cliff is not a technique someone of your cultivation should’ve mastered, yet you did.” As the leader of the Five Ancient Immortals, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy highly approved of Lu Yang’s talent in spatial spells.

During the ancient era, earning the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s compliment surpassed countless fortuitous opportunities, enough to elevate one to the heavens in a single step.

However, Lu Yang wasn’t aware of all that. To him, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had brought nothing but trials. Had it been the ancient times, he would have undoubtedly been branded as ‘ungrateful’ and ‘not knowing what was good for him.’

“Fine, I’ll learn it then.” Lu Yang reckoned that after cultivating for so long, he might as well treat this as a break to relax his mind.

“Not that I expect you to master Cosmos in Palm. Even grasping its principles will greatly benefit your execution of other spatial spells, boosting your speed in both learning and casting!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy knew it would be a challenge for Lu Yang to learn Cosmos in Palm, but she was determined to teach him anyway. If I want to teach, who can stop me?

Lu Yang jumped from the sword qi boulder, somersaulted thrice midair, spread his arms, and landed gracefully.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy pulled him into his mental space. With a thought, she swapped her usual sleepwear for the Confucian robes often worn by private teachers, instantly appearing smarter.

“Hehe, this feels more like it! Before I teach you, let me demonstrate!”

Before Lu Yang could react, his mental space, once the size of four rooms and two living rooms, expanded into a boundless void, pitch-black save for the conspicuous giant stars before him and the distant twinkling lights of faraway stars.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy stood in front of him. Extending a hand, she pressed down fiercely!

Lu Yang lifted his head, his eyes squinting. The universe was so dark that he couldn’t make out the details. He simply felt something on his head.

“Hmm?” Lu Yang realized the stars overhead had suddenly vanished, as if they were obscured by something!

A large hand emerged from the darkness, filling his entire line of sight. The palm lines were starkly clear, the whorl-like fingerprints resembling stellar orbits, where the stars were akin to grains of sand in the palm.

Lu Yang had experienced collapsing mountains and a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator’s oppressive pressure, but compared to this gargantuan hand, they were insignificant and incomparable! Oppression, suffocation, despair, and various other emotions sprouted wildly in his heart, growing uncontrollably.

“Watch closely. This is Cosmos in Palm.”

The enormous hand came crashing down. Darkness swallowed Lu Yang’s vision as his consciousness scattered.

When he awoke, he saw the Everlasting Immortal Fairy hovering over him and peering at him unblinkingly. “Did I scare you?”

“No, you slapped me to death.”

“Oh, right. So, did you see the mighty power of Cosmos in Palm?”

Fear lingered in Lu Yang’s heart. I should treat the Everlasting Immortal Fairy with more respect to keep myself safe.

“Immortal Fairy, you can expand my mental space?” Lu Yang remembered her previous complaints about his mental space’s cramped size hindering her movements.

Planting her hands on her hips, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy proudly declared, “I can expand it temporarily. I couldn’t do it before, but I’ve been sleeping every day lately, and that restored some of my strength.

“As the saying goes: A flower reflects a world, a tree reflects a fleeting life, a blade of grass reflects a bodhi, a leaf reflects a tathagata, a grain of sand reflects ultimate bliss, a region reflects a pure land of paradise, a smile reflects bonds of fate, a single thought reflects serenity—all the tiniest things represent the world.[1]

“Cosmos in Palm stems from this philosophy. Within a palm is a world, a vast and boundless great world!”

Lu Yang ruminated. I’ve heard of the popularity of spatial spells in Buddhist sects. Perhaps they originated from such concepts.

“If you wish to cultivate Cosmos in Palm, you must first visualize yourself as a great world. At the same time, since you need to visualize the true great world, every detail of the world will manifest in your mind, constructing a real great world.

“Integration of inner and outer, inversion of space, a tiny mustard holding Mount Sumeru, and infinite large and small sizes... If you can comprehend the meaning of these phrases, you’ll roughly master Cosmos in Palm.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy meticulously explained the principles of Cosmos in Palm, breaking down the profound segments into digestible points and varying perspectives in an attempt to make Lu Yang master the technique now.

“Alright, I’m more or less done teaching you. Go out and practice.” With a kick, she booted Lu Yang out of his mental space.

Back in reality, Lu Yang steadied himself and recalled what the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had taught him.

“Integration of inner and outer is about merging what one visualizes with reality... Being infinitely large is being infinitely small, and the shift between large and small is the essence of spatial spells...

Lu Yang extended his palm, studying its lines. Could my palm lines really correspond to stellar orbits?

Channelling spirit energy into his eyes to temporarily sharpen his vision, he peered deeper into his epidermal cells. Various components come together to make up a cell, which mirrors the structure of the human body. Could we see these cells as alternate lifeforms? Since there are countless cells in my hand, doesn’t that mean there are countless living beings in my palm?

“Is this the meaning of ‘a flower reflects a world?’” Lu Yang frowned in thought as he integrated his knowledge with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s teachings, gradually deducing the Buddhist sects’ philosophy, or rather, the foundational principles of Cosmos in Palm.

“The Immortal Fairy has already demonstrated it to me. The cosmos is the world, and Cosmos in a Palm means a world within the palm. It is the pinnacle of spatial spells, balancing both offense and defense...”

Muttering to himself, Lu Yang flipped his palm repeatedly, enlightenment gradually dawning in his heart like a ray of morning light piercing the fog and unveiling the legendary mighty ability. “So that’s how it is...”

Lu Yang shot up and dusted the mud off, a confident smile hanging at the corners of his mouth. “I’ve mastered it.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy materialized. Assuming that Lu Yang had given up, she consoled him. “It’s fine. Even if you haven’t mastered it, you have grasped the principles. When your cultivation rises to a certain level, you’ll be able to master it.

“Wait, did you just say you’ve mastered it?” She stared at Lu Yang in shock.

“Cosmos in Palm demands immense power. My spirit energy is insufficient to sustain it, but my Unbeatable Golden Core expands my spirit energy reserves by five to ten times that of my peers, just enough to cast it for an instant!”

Closing his eyes and treating himself as a crucible, Lu Yang sketched out the world’s appearance. It was an impossible feat for most, but with the memories from his past life, his understanding of the universe’s true form, and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s demonstration, the confluence of these factors allowed him to execute Cosmos in Palm.

Lu Yang spread his palms flat, and spirit energy coursed inside him madly as he shouted, “Cosmos in Palm!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy watched curiously as a space manifested in Lu Yang’s palm, with stars orbiting within like a miniature universe!

“He actually cultivated it successfully... Wait, why does the space in his palm seem so small? It’s only one or two li in length, and the stars are pathetically small?”

“Well, how was it? Did I cultivate it successfully?” Lu Yang shot her a triumphant look.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had an odd expression.

If mine is Cosmos in Palm, then Lu Yang’s is...Village in Palm?
