Chapter 391: Pills and Poison Belong to the Same Family

“Well, how was it? Did I cultivate it successfully?”

“What you’ve mastered is...” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy struggled with her limited vocabulary, finding it hard to answer Lu Yang’s question. “It counts as Cosmos in Palm, just that...the size isn’t quite right.”

She gestured with her hands. “It’s about the size of a village. You should call this move ‘Village in Palm.’”

Lu Yang examined the miniature space in his palm. It’s indeed not big. But ‘Village in Palm’ sounds terrible. He tried to reason, “How can you call it a village? Although the space is a bit small, it’s still a universe! Look, there are stars orbiting! It should be called ‘Small Cosmos in Palm!’”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy scoffed. “Oh, please. It’s just some sand grains spinning and pretending to be stars.”

She blew on Lu Yang’s palm, scattering the sandy “stars” away.

Seeing his ruse fail, Lu Yang could only admit defeat. “Fine, Village in Palm it is then. At least it’s still a spatial spell.”

He quickly shelved the naming issue in the back of his mind, focusing instead on how to properly cast the spell. “If Cosmos in Palm can bring an entire world crashing down and render everyone unable to resist, then Village in Palm should be able to do the same!”

Lu Yang imitated the Everlasting Immortal Fairy and pressed his right hand downward. “Village in Palm!”

Boom! A gigantic hand descended from the sky. It was the size of a village and overwhelmingly oppressive, shaking people mentally more than it did physically. Before fully descending, the hand gradually faded and vanished.

“Huff, huff...” Lu Yang gasped heavily, devouring spirit qi like a drowning man rescued to shore and desperately gulping mouthfuls of air.

He hadn’t dispelled Village in Palm intentionally; his spirit energy simply couldn’t sustain it. This single attempt had drained all his spirit energy.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shook her head. “This move is still too difficult for you.” Even a child’s version of Cosmos in Palm isn’t what Golden Core cultivators can cast.

That said, if this move could be fully unleashed, no Golden Core cultivator could withstand it! Not even a peerless Golden Core prodigy should dream of standing a chance!

Lu Yang soon devised a solution. “Perhaps I can consume pills while casting Village in Palm.”

Sitting cross-legged, he spent around ten minutes adjusting his mood before trying again. He whipped out his medicine gourd filled with Great Rejuvenation Pills—his best friends since childhood. Popping one into his mouth, he attempted to cast Village in Palm again.

Just like before, the giant palm vanished before it could land, and Lu Yang collapsed to the ground in exhaustion. “No, one pill isn’t enough.”

Another ten minutes later, Lu Yang swallowed three Great Rejuvenation Pills and attempted to cast Village in Palm again.

The giant palm vanished mid-air again.

“Three pills are still insufficient?” Lu Yang gnashed his teeth. Just how many Great Rejuvenation Pills would it take?

Five pills, six pills, seven pills, eight pills, nine pills, ten pills...

Finally, Lu Yang reached a conclusion. I need to stuff my mouth completely with pills.

This begot another question. I can’t swallow the pills with my mouth stuffed full, but if I swallow them one at a time, I won’t recover fast enough.

“Right, I can ask Seventh Elder for help!” As the Central Continent’s premier pill-concocting master, Seventh Elder can surely create pills that rapidly restore one’s spirit energy!

Moreover, since Lu Yang had gifted Seventh Elder a sentient Herding Sky Grass, Seventh Elder had offered to concoct pills for Lu Yang three times. There’s no time like the present!

~~~

Lu Yang found Seventh Elder tending to a pill furnace. The pill scent assaulted his nostrils, and with just one whiff, it was clear that it was not poisonous.

“Haha, my meticulously crafted Realm-Breaking Pill is finally complete!” Seventh Elder laughed heartily, immensely proud of his unprecedented creation.

“Congratulations, Seventh Elder!” Lu Yang approached Seventh Elder only after he was done to avoid disrupting him.

“Ah, Lu Yang! It’s a pity you’re at the Golden Core Stage; you can’t test my newly crafted Realm-Breaking Pill. This is an unprecedented pill!”

Lu Yang was slightly hesitant. Based on Seventh Elder’s words, it seems that ingesting his pill can advance one to the Golden Core Stage. As far as I know, such pills have existed for ages.

Seventh Elder waved his hand. “How could the pills crafted by those laities compare to mine? The Realm-Breaking Pills in the outer world are crudely made and devoid of any aesthetics!”

Lu Yang ventured cautiously. “And the pill you have crafted...”

“Those pills outside only elevate Foundation Establishment cultivators to the Golden Core Stage. That’s way too average!

“These few Realm-Breaking Pills I have concocted not only achieve that, but can also downgrade Nascent Soul cultivators to the Golden Core Stage!”

Lu Yang, “...”

Seventh Elder’s abysmal reputation in the outside world is not without a reason.

Although pills and poison belong to the same family, and most pill-concocting masters are more or less well-versed in toxicology, those who developed both skills equally like Seventh Elder are rare.

Lu Yang recalled his first visit to Pill Cauldron Peak, where he passed out due to a pill’s fragrance. Under Seventh Elder’s guidance, every disciple there excelled in the principles of poison, their expertise not at all inferior to their skills in pill concoction. Of course, even if they concoct pills, there’s no guarantee that they don’t contain toxins, perfectly embodying the philosophy of pills and poison belonging to the same family.

“It’s fate that we met; here, have one.” Seventh Elder flicked a pill with blue patterns into Lu Yang’s lap. “Why are you looking for me?”

“Here’s the thing. I’ve recently mastered a spell that drains enormous amounts of spirit energy. My spirit energy runs out halfway through casting the spell, and I’m forced to stop. I have tried to consume Great Rejuvenation Pills while casting, but the restoration rate couldn’t keep up with the depletion rate. I was hoping you could concoct a pill that would replenish my energy rapidly.”

“Hmm, you’re not the first to encounter such a situation. It’s not difficult to concoct one. Come, let me examine your meridians.”

Chapter 392: Astonishing Power

Beyond the pill liquid was a suspension of black liquid. As more medicinal ingredients were added, it expanded, and its hue shifted from black to cyan, exuding its own pill fragrance.

Chapter 395: The Intruder in the Dao-Seeking Sect!

The Lu-Style Roast Duck was lustrous with a golden hue, emitting an aroma that assaulted the nostrils. Its skin was crispy, while the meat was succulent with a creamy beige. Each bite released a burst of oily juices that were rich and savory, lingering on the palate.

As the senior sister and junior brother slowly enjoyed the roasted duck, Lu Yang focused entirely on his meal, pointedly ignoring the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s pleas.

“Let me taste it!

When night fell, a dark figure silently appeared before the Dao-Seeking Sect’s entrance.

The dark figure seemed extremely familiar with the Dao-Seeking Sect’s layout, knowing where guards were stationed and how to evade detection. With a mysterious footwork, he carefully skirted the River Spirit’s surveillance range and reached the inner grounds of the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“Hmph, the Dao-Seeking Sect is nothing special!” The dark figure snorted, his eyes coldly glinting with contempt.

“But I’m just afraid that the old codger Qin Jiunian is around. Although he is detestable, his cultivation is high, and he might sense my presence! I don’t think he’s around though. That old fellow is obsessed with constructing tombs and hardly shows up at the Great Mission Hall.”

The dark figure’s heart pounded wildly as he traversed through the mountain peak unopposed.

“My luck’s not bad. That old bastard Qin Jiunian isn’t around.”

With this hurdle cleared, the dark figure relaxed and brazenly moved about in the Dao-Seeking Sect. He was confident in his stealth arts. Even elder-level figures won’t be able to discover me!

Even when he strolled through the business district, he remained unnoticed. Despite the numerous veteran Fusion cultivators that lurked here, no one discovered the dark figure. One could only imagine the depth of his cultivation!

“Body Refinement Peak. This is the place. Going through the spirit fields, the dark figure saw the Blue-Eyed Buffaloes tirelessly tilling the fields, and a trace of envy flickered in his eyes. The Blue-Eyed Water Buffalo race is indeed the most suitable for farming. The faction he belonged to had a wide stretch of spirit fields, but they didn’t have the help of Blue-Eyed Water Buffaloes.

Chapter 396: Take My Fist!

Chapter 399: Elders’ Medical Consultation

Wilderness Province was located west of the Central Continent, close to Liang Province and the Buddhist Kingdom in the west. Witchcraft and corpse-driving arts flourished there. The moment he breaks through, the curse will definitely be broken.”

Meng Jingzhou’s face instantly went pale. Reaching the Nascent Soul Stage is not that worrying, but Divine Transfiguration? How many years of cultivation would that take?

“I can dispel some simple curses that are very shallow. For example, the curses you all are subjected to daily have been removed by me, but Nephew Meng’s curse is of too high a level and beyond my cultivation.

“If I could advance to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, I’d have the confidence to settle it.”

Grandpa Ba rolled his eyes. “You? Reach Transcendent Tribulation Stage? Get in line behind Big Bro and Old Nine. How could your cultivation progress compare to theirs?”

Fourth Elder shrugged. “Then I’m out of ideas. Wait, can’t we ask Shifu for help?”

Seventh Elder didn’t favor the idea. “Although Shifu is at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, he’s not familiar with curses. Besides, he’s busy overseeing Incarceration Peak and can’t be distracted.”

“Disciple, why don’t you try using Single’s Curse Fist on Old Two again? Maybe the backlashes would be neutralized?”

Meng Jingzhou vehemently shook his head. Are you joking? You call that backlash neutralization? That’s called backlash compounding!

“Actually, Nephew Meng, you don’t have to be so anxious. Your curse isn’t as severe as you think,” Fourth Elder consoled.

“Could you elaborate, Fourth Elder?”

“The karmic backlash is split between you and Qiu Jin’an. Half a karmic backlash is more manageable than a full karmic backlash.”

Meng Jingzhou’s eyes lit up. “Does that mean you have a solution, Fourth Elder?”

“No.”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

Third Elder proposed, “I heard that Nephew Li can regrow severed limbs, changing his entire body by replacing his body parts to evade karma. Could we apply that method to Nephew Meng? Old Seven, can you concoct a limb regeneration medicine for my disciple?” He was referring to Li Haoran’s Rebirth Golden Core.

“Concocting the medicine is easy. It’s just requesting a few root whiskers from the little herb kings. But would this method really be useful?”

Fourth Elder vetoed the idea. “Nephew Li’s Rebirth Golden Core can evade karma, but Nephew Meng’s karmic backlash is too high a level for this to work.”

Grandpa Ba suggested another idea. “The Heaven Strategy Sect is well-versed in the arts of karma. The location of our Dao-Seeking Sect was chosen based on calculations made by people from the Heaven Strategy Sect at the request of our founding ancestor, and it has been blessed for twelve thousand years. If they could even divine something like this, their expertise in the karma arts must be unparalleled. Karmic backlash should be within their scope. Why don’t we get them to try?”

Eighth Elder shook his head. “I remember the Heaven Strategy Sect’s legacy originated from the ancient Exalted Shi clan. They excel in karma arts and can perform calculations, but the Heaven Strategy Sect believes that karma can’t be erased—it’ll only transform from one type of karma to another. Hence, they rarely involve themselves in worldly affairs. If they meddle too much, the karma might taint them and cause them to lose their divination abilities.”

“I’ve heard about this too. It’s said that the Exalted Shi Clan didn’t have a good reputation in ancient times. They frequently abused their divination abilities for personal gain at the expense of lives, disrupting the order in the world to seek breakthroughs.

“Later, the Exalted Shi Clan offended an unknown expert, who inflicted a devastating blow to their clan. From then on, they never recovered. By the time the Exalted Shi Clan wanted to take revenge, that expert had ascended to an immortal. Fearing they might attract this ancient immortal’s attention, they ordered the entire clan to be sealed off, forbidding any contact with the mundane world lest they get influenced by worldly karma and bring upon terrifying calamities.

“After the Heaven Strategy Sect inherited the remnants of the Exalted Shi Clan, they became a secluded sect. If we ask the Heaven Strategy Sect to handle this matter, they’d probably change Nephew Meng’s situation from ‘unable to meet women’ to ‘unable to meet men.’

“In that case, how about we place another curse on Nephew Meng to make him get romantic peach-blossom tribulations every day. Perhaps these two curses would cancel each other out?”

“That sounds like a plan. Who knows how to cast curses? Old Four, can you do it?”

Fourth Elder rolled his eyes, feeling that his fellow senior and junior brothers were giving him too much credit. “No, I studied how to break curses, not cast them. If I knew how to cast a romantic peach-blossom tribulation, I would have cast it on myself first.”

“Old Four, you’re a proper Confucian cultivator. Why would you need romantic peach-blossom tribulations?”

“To emulate the ancients who maintained their composure even with a beauty in their arms, thereby tempering the heart and character of a gentleman.”

“That’s the same excuse all ‘gentlemen’ use when visiting brothels.”

“They copied me.”

“Has anyone learned how to cast Tame Head Curses from the eastern seas? The principles are more or less similar to curses. It might solve our current predicament.”

“Old Ba, you’ve been to the East Sea, right? Did you learn it?”

“No, I was being hunted down by the merfolk. How would I get the time to study Tame Head Curses?”

While the elders continued their discussion on Meng Jingzhou’s curse, Lu Yang stayed in his mental space to seek an ancient immortal’s assistance.

Logically speaking, with an ancient immortal as my golden finger cheat—and the most powerful one at that—no matter what troubles I run into, the ancient immortal should always have a way.

“Immortal Fairy, do you have any other ideas?”

“Yes.”

“What is it?”

“As the saying goes, when one dies, the Dao vanishes, and all karma is gone. As long as one dies once, their karma will naturally disappear.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy cheerfully proposed her carefully thought-out second solution.

Lu Yang suspected that given Meng Jingzhou’s intelligence, he probably wouldn’t approve of this method.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was displeased with Lu Yang’s attitude. I frequently used this method to evade karma, and it worked perfectly every single time.

The more Meng Jingzhou listened to the elder’s discussion, the more he found their methods unreliable. Better to self-help than to seek help. “Why don’t I make a trip to Wilderness Province? Who knows if I might find a solution there?”

“That actually sounds like a workable plan.”

Chapter 400: The Epoch Immortal Ensures Safety freёwebnoѵel.com

“Going to Wilderness Province sounds good. You should be able to find solutions there.” Third Elder nodded approvingly. I have to give it up to my disciple’s brain.

“I’ll go with you.” Lu Yang felt that he’d been obediently cultivating at Heaven’s Gate Peak for too long and needed to go out for a stroll. My mind is about to atrophy.

Fourth Elder kindly advised them, “If you’re going to Wilderness Province, you could seek help from the Corpse-Driving Sect. They’re on good terms with our sect, with every generation of sect leaders having friendly relations with each other. Even if you request to learn their corpse-driving arts, they wouldn’t refuse.”

The Corpse-Driving Sect was a renowned first-class faction in the Wilderness Province. With their assistance, things would be much smoother. During his travels there, Fourth Elder had received their aid.

Fourth Elder immediately penned a recommendation letter, folded it neatly into an envelope, and handed it to Meng Jingzhou.

Meng Jingzhou took the envelope, then froze in realization. “Just me and Lu Yang? Shifu, are you all not coming?”

All of you were enthusiastically brainstorming solutions for me a moment ago. Although none were useful, it still reflected your concern for me. But why does it now look like only Lu Yang and I are going there?

Third Elder waved his hand. “Not going. This matter of yours is too embarrassing if word gets out.” How is taking Meng Jingzhou to Wilderness Province to lift the curse any different from seeking treatment for yang impotence?

If word of this spreads, how will I continue mingling in the jianghu in the future?

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

Lu Yang, “...”

On the other hand, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was brimming with confidence about their trip. “What are you scared of? With me here, what could possibly go wrong?”

The elders’ medical consultation concluded with the verdict that the patient needed to save himself.

Meng Jingzhou sighed and returned to his cave abode to pack. Unsurprisingly, he didn’t encounter a single senior female disciple along the way.

~~~

Lu Yang also went to pack his things.

“Witchcraft and corpse-driving are specialties of Wilderness Province, along with ubiquitous tombstones and all manner of miasmas and poisons. I’ll need to redeem some detoxification pills at the Great Mission Hall.

“There are many curse practitioners there too. Since I’ve never faced one before, I may be at a disadvantage if I run into one. Should I purchase some items to ward off curses?”

“With me protecting you, why fear curses?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy proudly patted her chest to assert her presence. As the leader of the Five Ancient Immortals, what curse could affect me?

Lu Yang glanced at her. True, the greatest curse in existence is right here. What other curses are there to fear?

Not having to worry about curses would make our trip to Wilderness Province much more relaxed.

“You have it much better now. With me around, you don’t have to worry about curses. Back then, before I became an immortal, I often fought with people, competing for the right to become an immortal. That bunch of fellows were youth prodigies and had some skills and local fame, but once they encountered me, all of that became useless!

“These fellows didn’t deserve to be called ‘youth prodigies.’ They never picked themselves up again after just one defeat from me. Look at the Heaven Mandate Immortal and Qilin Immortal. They got beaten by me all the time, but I didn’t see them giving up on themselves. When they couldn’t defeat me openly, they resorted to secretly casting deadly curses on me.

“Fortunately, I managed to overcome them all with my unparalleled talent.”

Lu Yang recalled that curses originated from ancient times, and curses then were far more vicious and frightening than modern ones. To have resisted those ancient curses and successfully become an immortal is a testament to her strength.

He marveled inwardly, As expected of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. Although she’s usually frivolous, her reputation in the ancient era was built on true substance.

“The worst were some holy maidens. They were unable to defeat me and were jealous of my looks. Worried that the men they liked would like me, they cursed me to be disfigured!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy pouted lividly. It was evident that even after eons, the actions of these holy maidens still rankled.

“Before I became an immortal, I had fame, cultivation, beauty, and wisdom—but I lacked backing. I was often ostracized, and some even mocked me openly, saying that no matter how strong I was, without powerful support, I’d never ascend.

“Bullying me for having no background? Then I’ll become the greatest backer myself!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy laughed triumphantly. What used to rile her now seemed childish.

“Impressive, Immortal Fairy.”

“Right?”

Lu Yang quickly packed everything he could think of, then visited the Great Mission Hall to redeem many additional supplies that could come in handy.

“Detoxification pills are a must. And these herbs can also be used to concoct emergency antidotes in critical moments.” Lu Yang had studied basic toxicology at Pill Cauldron Peak as part of the standard curriculum for Dao-Seeking Sect disciples. Common poisons were ineffective against him.

When traveling, we should mean no harm to others, but we must guard against harm from others—this was the doctrine of the Five-Elements Sect.

Later, the Taciturn Daoist Priest and eight elders felt that Qiu Jin’an made sense, so they adapted the saying to caution their disciples to guard against others from harming them.

“I should buy a few reference books on Wilderness Province too—Anthropology of the Wilderness Province, Corpse-Driving Legends, Calamity of Witchcraft...

“I may get embroiled in fights, so I have to buy some combat-use talismans and Soul-Restoration Pills... That should be about it.”

After Lu Yang finished procuring his supplies, he proceeded to the sect’s entrance to meet up with Meng Jingzhou. The latter had arrived first and was already waiting in the carriage.

“You’re too slow.”

“What’s the rush? You make it sound like going early would guarantee an early return.”

After Lu Yang boarded the carriage, the two verified their supplies before setting off.

En route, the bored Everlasting Immortal Fairy mused, “If only we could find the Epoch Immortal. His Jianmu World Tree’s body has blessing abilities—just a leaf or twig could remove the Meng Family boy’s karmic backlash.”

“The Jianmu World Tree was capable of such things? Why haven’t I heard of it before?” Lu Yang was puzzled. But with the pitifully sparse descriptions of the Jianmu World Tree in ancient texts, it’s only normal for there to be gaps in my knowledge.

“You know New Year?[1] The day when the old gives way to the new, and you cross over bad luck to obtain good fortune in the coming year? He invented this ‘New Year’ concept.

“Wasn’t there a custom of stepping over branches during the New Year? It was likely they were originally Jainmu branches. However, people of later generations couldn’t find Jianmu branches and substituted them with ordinary ones.

“Speaking of which, I initially didn’t know about the Jianmu World Tree’s effect of praying for blessings. It was the Qilin Immortal and the others told me. They said that the Epoch Immortal had a chance of predicting when I would treat them to a meal and when I would visit their cave abodes, which allowed them to make preparations in advance. That was a massive blessing.”

Lu Yang was in full agreement, nodding at the other immortals’ viewpoint.

“The Epoch Immortal indeed had the function of praying for blessings to ensure safety.”

1. “New Year” literally translates to “cross the year” in the Chinese version here. ☜
